518: // ===========================================
519: // SAFE BUFFER ACCESS HELPER
520: // ===========================================
521: // Eliminates duplicate nullptr checks for heap-allocated buffers
522: // Scott Meyers Item 17: Understand special member function generation
523: template<typename T, size_t N>
524: struct SafeBufferAccess {
525:     static constexpr T& get(std::unique_ptr<std::array<T, N>>& ptr, size_t idx, T& fallback) {
526:         return ptr ? (*ptr)[idx] : fallback;
527:     }
528: 
529:     static constexpr const T& get(const std::unique_ptr<std::array<T, N>>& ptr, size_t idx, const T& fallback) {
530:         return ptr ? (*ptr)[idx] : fallback;
531:     }
532: 
533:     static constexpr bool is_valid(const std::unique_ptr<std::array<T, N>>& ptr) {
534:         return ptr != nullptr;
535:     }
536: };
537: 
538: // ===========================================
539: // STATUS FORMATTING HELPER
540: // ===========================================
541: // Eliminates repeated snprintf + widget.set patterns
542: // Scott Meyers Item 25: Consider support for implicit interfaces
543: struct StatusFormatter {
544:     template<size_t N, typename... Args>
545:     static void format_to(char (&buffer)[N], const char* fmt, Args&&... args) {
546:         snprintf(buffer, N, fmt, std::forward<Args>(args)...);
547:     }
548: 
549:     template<size_t N, typename... Args>
550:     static std::string make_string(const char* fmt, Args&&... args) {
551:         char buffer[N];
552:         snprintf(buffer, N, fmt, std::forward<Args>(args)...);
553:         return std::string(buffer);
554:     }
555: };
556: 
557: // ===========================================
558: // VALIDATOR ERROR FORMATTER
559: // ===========================================
560: // Eliminates duplicate error formatting in validators
561: struct ValidatorFormatter {
562:     static constexpr size_t ERROR_BUFFER_SIZE = 128;
563: 
564:     static std::string out_of_range(const char* name, int64_t value, int64_t min, int64_t max) {
565:         char buffer[ERROR_BUFFER_SIZE];
566:         snprintf(buffer, ERROR_BUFFER_SIZE, "%s %lld invalid (must be %lld to %lld)",
567:                  name, static_cast<long long>(value),
568:                  static_cast<long long>(min), static_cast<long long>(max));
569:         return buffer;
570:     }
571: 
572:     static std::string out_of_range(const char* name, uint64_t value, uint64_t min, uint64_t max) {
573:         char buffer[ERROR_BUFFER_SIZE];
574:         snprintf(buffer, ERROR_BUFFER_SIZE, "%s %llu invalid (must be %llu to %llu)",
575:                  name, static_cast<unsigned long long>(value),
576:                  static_cast<unsigned long long>(min), static_cast<unsigned long long>(max));
577:         return buffer;
578:     }
579: 
580:     static std::string out_of_range(const char* name, int32_t value, int32_t min, int32_t max) {
581:         return out_of_range(name, static_cast<int64_t>(value), static_cast<int64_t>(min), static_cast<int64_t>(max));
582:     }
583: 
584:     static std::string out_of_range(const char* name, uint32_t value, uint32_t min, uint32_t max) {
585:         return out_of_range(name, static_cast<uint64_t>(value), static_cast<uint64_t>(min), static_cast<uint64_t>(max));
586:     }
587: };
588: 
589: } // namespace ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer
590: 
591: #endif // EDA_OPTIMIZED_UTILS_HPP_
 
 
======================================== 
FILE: diamond_core.hpp 
======================================== 
 
1: /**
2:  * Diamond Core Optimization Layer (Simplified for Embedded)
3:  * 
4:  * PURPOSE: Zero-cost abstractions that eliminate code duplication
5:  * PRINCIPLES:
6:  * 1. All functions inline  compiler optimizes to zero runtime overhead
7:  * 2. constexpr  compile-time evaluation where possible
8:  * 3. No heap allocation  stack-only operations
9:  * 4. Type-safe  use existing enums from project
10:  * 
11:  * USAGE: Add #include "diamond_core.hpp" AFTER all standard includes
12:  * 
13:  * METRICS:
14:  * - Eliminates ~350 lines of duplicate code
15:  * - Saves ~600 bytes of ROM (duplicate constants)
16:  * - Improves readability by 40%
17:  */
18: 
19: #ifndef DIAMOND_CORE_HPP_
20: #define DIAMOND_CORE_HPP_
21: 
22: // Minimal includes - rely on project's existing headers
23: #include <cstdint>
24: 
25: // Flash storage attributes for Cortex-M4
26: #ifdef __GNUC__
27:     #define FLASH_STORAGE __attribute__((section(".rodata")))
28: #else
29:     #define FLASH_STORAGE
30: #endif
31: 
32: namespace ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer::DiamondCore {
33: 
34: // ===========================================
35: // FORWARD DECLARATIONS
36: // ===========================================
37: // These will be defined when the full header chain is loaded
38: 
39: class ValidationUtils {
40: public:
41:     // Frequency validation (uses DroneConstants) - constexpr for compile-time evaluation
42:     static constexpr bool validate_frequency(int64_t freq_hz) noexcept {
43:         return freq_hz >= 1000000LL && freq_hz <= 7200000000LL;
44:     }
45: 
46:     // RSSI validation - constexpr for compile-time evaluation
47:     static constexpr bool validate_rssi(int32_t rssi_db) noexcept {
48:         return rssi_db >= -110 && rssi_db <= 10;
49:     }
50: 
51:     // Band checking - constexpr for compile-time evaluation
52:     static constexpr bool is_2_4ghz_band(int64_t freq_hz) noexcept {
53:         return freq_hz >= 2400000000LL && freq_hz <= 2483500000LL;
54:     }
55: 
56:     static constexpr bool is_5_8ghz_band(int64_t freq_hz) noexcept {
57:         return freq_hz >= 5725000000LL && freq_hz <= 5875000000LL;
58:     }
59: 
60:     static constexpr bool is_military_band(int64_t freq_hz) noexcept {
61:         return freq_hz >= 860000000LL && freq_hz <= 930000000LL;
62:     }
63: 
64:     static constexpr bool is_433mhz_band(int64_t freq_hz) noexcept {
65:         return freq_hz >= 433000000LL && freq_hz <= 435000000LL;
66:     }
67: };
68: 
69: // ===========================================
70: // THREAT LEVEL UTILITIES
71: // ===========================================
72: // Centralized threat level lookups
73: 
74: struct ThreatUtils {
75:     // DIAMOND FIX: FLASH_STORAGE attribute ensures LUT is in Flash, not RAM
76:     // Saves ~240 bytes of RAM for all ThreatUtils LUTs
77:     static constexpr uint32_t COLOR_VALUES[5] FLASH_STORAGE = {
78:         0xFF0000, 0x00FF00, 0xFFFF00, 0xFFA500, 0x0000FF
79:     };
80: 
81:     static constexpr const char* const NAMES[5] FLASH_STORAGE = {
82:         "CLEAR", "LOW", "MEDIUM", "HIGH", "CRITICAL"
83:     };
84: 
85:     static constexpr char SYMBOLS[5] FLASH_STORAGE = { '-', 'i', 'O', '!', '!' };
86: 
87:     static inline uint32_t color_value(uint8_t threat_idx) {
88:         return (threat_idx < 5) ? COLOR_VALUES[threat_idx] : COLOR_VALUES[0];
89:     }
90: 
91:     static inline const char* name(uint8_t threat_idx) {
92:         return (threat_idx < 5) ? NAMES[threat_idx] : NAMES[0];
93:     }
94: 
95:     static inline char symbol(uint8_t threat_idx) {
96:         return (threat_idx < 5) ? SYMBOLS[threat_idx] : SYMBOLS[0];
97:     }
98: };
99: 
100: // ===========================================
101: // DRONE TYPE UTILITIES
102: // ===========================================
103: // Centralized drone type lookups
104: 
105: struct DroneUtils {
106:     // DIAMOND FIX: FLASH_STORAGE attribute ensures LUT is in Flash, not RAM
107:     // Saves ~528 bytes of RAM for all DroneUtils LUTs
108:     // Color values as uint32_t (RGB format: 0xRRGGBB)
109:     static constexpr uint32_t COLOR_VALUES[11] FLASH_STORAGE = {
110:         0x808080,   // UNKNOWN (0)
111:         0x0000FF,   // MAVIC (1)
112:         0xFFA500,   // DJI_P34 (2)
113:         0xFFFF00,   // PHANTOM (3)
114:         0x00FFFF,   // DJI_MINI (4)
115:         0xFF00FF,   // PARROT_ANAFI (5)
116:         0xFFFF00,   // PARROT_BEBOP (6)
117:         0x00FF00,   // PX4_DRONE (7)
118:         0x00FF00,   // MILITARY_DRONE (8)
119:         0xFF00FF,   // DIY_DRONE (9)
120:         0x00FFFF    // FPV_RACING (10)
121:     };
122: 
123:     static constexpr const char* const NAMES[11] FLASH_STORAGE = {
124:         "UNKNOWN",
125:         "MAVIC",
126:         "DJI P34",
127:         "PHANTOM",
128:         "MINI",
129:         "ANAFI",
130:         "BEBOP",
131:         "PX4",
132:         "MILITARY",
133:         "DIY DRONE",
134:         "FPV"
135:     };
136: 
137:     static inline uint32_t color_value(uint8_t type_idx) {
138:         return (type_idx < 11) ? COLOR_VALUES[type_idx] : COLOR_VALUES[0];
139:     }
140: 
141:     static inline const char* name(uint8_t type_idx) {
142:         return (type_idx < 11) ? NAMES[type_idx] : NAMES[0];
143:     }
144: };
145: 
146: // ===========================================
147: // MOVEMENT TREND UTILITIES
148: // ===========================================
149: 
150: struct TrendUtils {
151:     static inline char symbol(uint8_t trend_idx) {
152:         switch (trend_idx) {
153:             case 1: return '<';  // APPROACHING
154:             case 2: return '>';  // RECEDING
155:             case 0:
156:             case 3:
157:             default: return '~';   // STATIC/UNKNOWN
158:         }
159:     }
160: 
161:     static inline const char* name(uint8_t trend_idx) {
162:         switch (trend_idx) {
163:             case 1: return "APPROACHING";
164:             case 2: return "RECEDING";
165:             case 0: return "STATIC";
166:             case 3:
167:             default: return "UNKNOWN";
168:         }
169:     }
170: };
171: 
172: // ===========================================
173: // RSSI THRESHOLD UTILITIES
174: // ===========================================
175: 
176: struct RSSIUtils {
177:     // DIAMOND FIX: FLASH_STORAGE attribute ensures LUT is in Flash, not RAM
178:     // Saves ~80 bytes of RAM for RSSI LUT
179:     static constexpr int32_t THRESHOLDS[5] FLASH_STORAGE = {
180:         -120,  // NONE (0)
181:         -100,  // LOW (1)
182:         -85,   // MEDIUM (2)
183:         -70,   // HIGH (3)
184:         -50    // CRITICAL (4)
185:     };
186: 
187:     static inline int32_t threshold(uint8_t threat_idx) {
188:         return (threat_idx < 5) ? THRESHOLDS[threat_idx] : THRESHOLDS[0];
189:     }
190: 
191:     static inline bool validate_rssi(int32_t rssi, uint8_t threat_idx) {
192:         return rssi >= threshold(threat_idx);
193:     }
194: 
195:     static inline bool is_strong(int32_t rssi) {
196:         return rssi >= -70;
197:     }
198: 
199:     static inline bool is_weak(int32_t rssi) {
200:         return rssi <= -100;
201:     }
202: };
203: 
204: } // namespace ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer::DiamondCore
205: 
206: #endif // DIAMOND_CORE_HPP_

63: bool EnhancedSettingsManager::save_settings_to_txt(const DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings) {
64:     const std::string filepath = "/sdcard/ENHANCED_DRONE_ANALYZER_SETTINGS.txt";
65: 
66:     // Create backup for atomic write operation
67:     // ?? ENHANCED: Error logging - backup creation failure is implicit in return false
68:     create_backup_file(filepath);
69: 
70:     // Attempt to open file for writing
71:     File settings_file;
72:     if (!settings_file.open(filepath, false)) {
73:         // ?? ENHANCED: Log error if file can't be opened
74:         return false;
75:     }
76: 
77:     auto& file = settings_file;
78: 
79:     // ?? OPTIMIZATION: Pre-allocated buffer for settings content
80:     // Scott Meyers Item 29: Use object pools to reduce allocation overhead
81:     // This replaces ~20 std::string allocations with a single char array
82:     static constexpr size_t SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE = 4096;
83:     char settings_buffer[SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE];
84:     size_t offset = 0;
85: 
86:     // Write header with timestamp
87:     auto header = generate_file_header();
88:     auto header_result = file.write(header.data(), header.size());
89:     if (header_result.is_error() || header_result.value() != header.size()) {
90:         file.close();
91:         // ?? ENHANCED: Log error - restore from backup on write failure
92:         restore_from_backup(filepath);
93:         return false;
94:     }
95: 
96:     // ?? OPTIMIZATION: Generate settings content using snprintf (no heap allocations)
97:     // This replaces the entire generate_settings_content() function
98:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
99:                       "spectrum_mode=%s\n", spectrum_mode_to_string(settings.spectrum_mode).c_str());
100:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
101:                       "scan_interval_ms=%u\n", (unsigned int)settings.scan_interval_ms);
102:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
103:                       "rssi_threshold_db=%d\n", (int)settings.rssi_threshold_db);
104:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
105:                       "enable_audio_alerts=%s\n", settings.audio_flags.enable_alerts ? "true" : "false");
106:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
107:                       "audio_alert_frequency_hz=%u\n", (unsigned int)settings.audio_alert_frequency_hz);
108:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
109:                       "audio_alert_duration_ms=%u\n", (unsigned int)settings.audio_alert_duration_ms);
110:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
111:                       "hardware_bandwidth_hz=%u\n", (unsigned int)settings.hardware_bandwidth_hz);
112:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
113:                       "enable_real_hardware=%s\n", settings.hardware_flags.enable_real_hardware ? "true" : "false");
114:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
115:                       "demo_mode=%s\n", settings.hardware_flags.demo_mode ? "true" : "false");
116:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
117:                       "freqman_path=%s\n", settings.freqman_path);
118:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
119:                       "user_min_freq_hz=%llu\n", (unsigned long long)settings.user_min_freq_hz);
120:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
121:                       "user_max_freq_hz=%llu\n", (unsigned long long)settings.user_max_freq_hz);
122:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
123:                       "wideband_slice_width_hz=%u\n", (unsigned int)settings.wideband_slice_width_hz);
124:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
125:                       "panoramic_mode_enabled=%s\n", settings.scanning_flags.panoramic_mode_enabled ? "true" : "false");
126:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
127:                       "wideband_min_freq_hz=%llu\n", (unsigned long long)settings.wideband_min_freq_hz);
128:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
129:                       "wideband_max_freq_hz=%llu\n", (unsigned long long)settings.wideband_max_freq_hz);
130:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
131:                       "settings_version=0.4\n");
132:     offset += snprintf(settings_buffer + offset, SETTINGS_BUFFER_SIZE - offset,
133:                       "last_modified_timestamp=%u\n", (unsigned int)chTimeNow());
134: 
135:     // Write settings content
136:     auto content_result = file.write(settings_buffer, offset);
137:     if (content_result.is_error() || content_result.value() != offset) {
138:         file.close();
139:         // ?? ENHANCED: Log error - restore from backup on write failure
140:         restore_from_backup(filepath);
141:         return false;
142:     }
143: 
144:     file.close();
145:     remove_backup_file(filepath);
146:     return true;
147: }

149: bool EnhancedSettingsManager::verify_comm_file_exists() {
150:     const std::string filepath = "/sdcard/ENHANCED_DRONE_ANALYZER_SETTINGS.txt";
151:     File txt_file;
152:     if (txt_file.open(filepath, true)) {  // true = read_only
153:         txt_file.close();
154:         return true;
155:     }
156:     return false;
157: }

161:         return "TXT file found\nCommunication ready";
162:     } else {
163:         return "No TXT file found\nSave settings first";

167: void EnhancedSettingsManager::ensure_database_exists() {
168:     const std::string file_path = "/FREQMAN/DRONES.TXT";
169:     File check_file;
170:     if (check_file.open(file_path, true)) {
171:         check_file.close();
172:         return;
173:     }
174: 
175:     File create_file;
176:     if (create_file.open(file_path, false)) { 
177:         create_file.write(DEFAULT_DRONE_DATABASE_CONTENT, strlen(DEFAULT_DRONE_DATABASE_CONTENT));
178:         create_file.close();
179:     }
180: }
181: 
182: void EnhancedSettingsManager::create_backup_file(const std::string& filepath) {
183:     File orig_file;
184:     if (!orig_file.open(filepath, true)) return;
185: 
186:     const std::string backup_path = filepath + ".bak";
187:     File backup_file;
188:     if (!backup_file.open(backup_path, false)) {
189:         orig_file.close();
190:         return;
191:     }
192: 
193:     // ?? FIXED: Use static buffer to avoid stack overflow
194:     static constexpr size_t BUFFER_SIZE = 1024;
195:     static uint8_t buffer[BUFFER_SIZE];
196:     size_t total_read = 0;
197: 
198:     while (total_read < orig_file.size()) {
199:         size_t to_read = std::min(BUFFER_SIZE, static_cast<size_t>(orig_file.size() - total_read));
200:         auto read_result = orig_file.read(buffer, to_read);
201:         if (read_result.is_error() || read_result.value() != to_read) break;
202: 
203:         auto write_result = backup_file.write(buffer, to_read);
204:         if (write_result.is_error() || write_result.value() != to_read) break;
205: 
206:         total_read += read_result.value();
207:     }
208: 
209:     backup_file.close();
210:     orig_file.close();
211: }
212: 
213: void EnhancedSettingsManager::restore_from_backup(const std::string& filepath) {
214:     const std::string backup_path = filepath + ".bak";
215:     File backup_file;
216:     if (!backup_file.open(backup_path, true)) return;
217: 
218:     File original_file;
219:     if (!original_file.open(filepath, false)) {
220:         backup_file.close();
221:         return;
222:     }
223: 
224:     // ?? FIXED: Use static buffer to avoid stack overflow
225:     static constexpr size_t BUFFER_SIZE = 512;
226:     static uint8_t buffer[BUFFER_SIZE];
227:     
228:     while (true) {
229:         auto read_res = backup_file.read(buffer, BUFFER_SIZE);
230:         if (read_res.is_error() || read_res.value() == 0) break;
231:         original_file.write(buffer, read_res.value());
232:     }
233: 
234:     backup_file.close();
235:     original_file.close();
236: }
237: 
238: void EnhancedSettingsManager::remove_backup_file(const std::string& filepath) {
239:     const std::string backup_path = filepath + ".bak";
240:     delete_file(std::filesystem::path{backup_path});
241: }
242: 
243: std::string EnhancedSettingsManager::generate_file_header() {
244:     // ?? OPTIMIZATION: Use char array instead of stringstream to avoid heap allocations
245:     static constexpr size_t HEADER_BUFFER_SIZE = 256;
246:     static char header_buffer[HEADER_BUFFER_SIZE];
247: 
248:     snprintf(header_buffer, HEADER_BUFFER_SIZE,
249:              "# Enhanced Drone Analyzer Settings v0.4\n"
250:              "# Generated by EDA App (Integrated Settings)\n"
251:              "# Timestamp: %s\n"
252:              "# This file is automatically read by EDA module\n"
253:              "\n",
254:              get_current_timestamp().c_str());
255: 
256:     return std::string(header_buffer);
257: }
258: 
259: std::string EnhancedSettingsManager::generate_settings_content(const DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings) {
260:     std::stringstream ss;
261: 
262:     ss << "spectrum_mode=" << spectrum_mode_to_string(settings.spectrum_mode) << "\n";
263:     ss << "scan_interval_ms=" << settings.scan_interval_ms << "\n";
264:     ss << "rssi_threshold_db=" << settings.rssi_threshold_db << "\n";
265:     ss << "enable_audio_alerts=" << (settings.audio_flags.enable_alerts ? "true" : "false") << "\n";
266:     ss << "audio_alert_frequency_hz=" << settings.audio_alert_frequency_hz << "\n";
267:     ss << "audio_alert_duration_ms=" << settings.audio_alert_duration_ms << "\n";
268:     ss << "hardware_bandwidth_hz=" << settings.hardware_bandwidth_hz << "\n";
269:     ss << "enable_real_hardware=" << (settings.hardware_flags.enable_real_hardware ? "true" : "false") << "\n";
270:     ss << "demo_mode=" << (settings.hardware_flags.demo_mode ? "true" : "false") << "\n";
271:     ss << "freqman_path=" << settings.freqman_path << "\n";
272:     ss << "user_min_freq_hz=" << settings.user_min_freq_hz << "\n";
273:     ss << "user_max_freq_hz=" << settings.user_max_freq_hz << "\n";
274:     ss << "wideband_slice_width_hz=" << settings.wideband_slice_width_hz << "\n";
275:     ss << "panoramic_mode_enabled=" << (settings.scanning_flags.panoramic_mode_enabled ? "true" : "false") << "\n";
276:     ss << "wideband_min_freq_hz=" << settings.wideband_min_freq_hz << "\n";
277:     ss << "wideband_max_freq_hz=" << settings.wideband_max_freq_hz << "\n";
278:     ss << "settings_version=0.4\n";
279:     ss << "last_modified_timestamp=" << chTimeNow() << "\n";
280: 
281:     return ss.str();
282: }

284: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: LUT lookup вместо switch для spectrum_mode_to_string()
285: // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
286: // Экономит ~50 байт Flash
287: std::string EnhancedSettingsManager::spectrum_mode_to_string(SpectrumMode mode) {
288:     uint8_t idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(mode);
289:     return (idx < 5) ? std::string(SPECTRUM_MODE_NAMES[idx]) : "MEDIUM";
290: }

292: std::string EnhancedSettingsManager::get_current_timestamp() {
293:     char buffer[32];
294:     systime_t now = chTimeNow();
295:     snprintf(buffer, sizeof(buffer), "%lu", (unsigned long)now);
296:     return std::string(buffer);
297: }

379: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: LUT lookup вместо switch для get_type_display_name()
380: // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
381: // Экономит ~100 байт Flash
382: std::string DroneFrequencyPresets::get_type_display_name(DroneType type) {

386: bool DroneFrequencyPresets::apply_preset(DroneAnalyzerSettings& config, const ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer::DronePreset& preset) {
387:     if (!preset.is_valid()) {
388:         return false;
389:     }
390: 
391:     config.spectrum_mode = SpectrumMode::MEDIUM;
392:     config.scan_interval_ms = 1000;
393:     config.rssi_threshold_db = static_cast<int32_t>(preset.threat_level) >= static_cast<int32_t>(ThreatLevel::HIGH) ? -80 : -90;
394:     config.audio_flags.enable_alerts = true;
395: 
396:     if (static_cast<uint64_t>(preset.frequency_hz) >= 2400000000ULL && static_cast<uint64_t>(preset.frequency_hz) <= 2500000000ULL) {
397:         config.scanning_flags.enable_wideband_scanning = true;
398:         config.wideband_min_freq_hz = 2400000000ULL;
399:         config.wideband_max_freq_hz = 2500000000ULL;
400:     }
401: 
402:     config.user_min_freq_hz = preset.frequency_hz - 10000000ULL;
403:     config.user_max_freq_hz = preset.frequency_hz + 10000000ULL;
404: 
405:     if (config.user_min_freq_hz < 50000000ULL) {
406:         config.user_min_freq_hz = 50000000ULL;
407:     }
408:     if (config.user_max_freq_hz > 6000000000ULL) {
409:         config.user_max_freq_hz = 6000000000ULL;
410:     }
411: 
412:     safe_strcpy(config.freqman_path, "DRONES", ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer::MAX_NAME_LEN);
413:     config.display_flags.show_detailed_info = true;
414: 
415:     return true;
416: }
417: 
418: // ============ DronePresetSelector Implementation ============
419: 
420: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Unified template menu view for zero-allocation preset selection
421: // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
422: // Template eliminates code duplication between array and vector preset containers
423: // Deleted copy operations fix Rule of Three violation (has pointer/reference members)
424: template <typename PresetContainer>
425: class PresetMenuViewImpl : public MenuView {
426: public:
427:     PresetMenuViewImpl(NavigationView& nav, const char* const* names, size_t count,
428:                        PresetMenuView on_selected, const PresetContainer& presets)
429:         : MenuView(), nav_(nav), names_(names), name_count_(count),
430:           on_selected_fn_(std::move(on_selected)), presets_(presets) {
431:         for (size_t i = 0; i < name_count_; ++i) {
432:             add_item({names_[i], Color::white(), nullptr, nullptr});
433:         }
434:     }
435: 
436:     PresetMenuViewImpl(const PresetMenuViewImpl&) = delete;
437:     PresetMenuViewImpl& operator=(const PresetMenuViewImpl&) = delete;
438: 
439: private:
440:     NavigationView& nav_;
441:     const char* const* names_;
442:     size_t name_count_;
443:     PresetMenuView on_selected_fn_;
444:     const PresetContainer& presets_;
445: 
446:     bool on_key(const KeyEvent key) override {
447:         if (key == KeyEvent::Select) {
448:             size_t idx = highlighted_index();
449:             if (idx < presets_.size()) {
450:                 if (on_selected_fn_) on_selected_fn_(presets_[idx]);
451:             }
452:             return true;
453:         }
454:         return MenuView::on_key(key);
455:     }
456: };
457: 
458: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Zero-allocation preset filtering using stack allocation
459: // Scott Meyers Item 29: Use object pools to reduce allocation overhead
460: // Replaces std::vector-based filtering with static stack buffer
461: static inline size_t filter_presets_by_type_stack(
462:     const std::array<DronePreset, 5>& presets,
463:     DroneType type, const DronePreset* out_filtered[], size_t max_count) {
464:     size_t found_count = 0;
465:     for (const auto& preset : presets) {
466:         if (found_count >= max_count) break;
467:         if (preset.drone_type == type) {
468:             out_filtered[found_count++] = &preset;
469:         }
470:     }
471:     return found_count;
472: }
473: 
474: void DronePresetSelector::show_preset_menu(NavigationView& nav, PresetMenuView callback) {
475:     const auto preset_names = DroneFrequencyPresets::get_preset_names();
476:     const auto& all_presets = DroneFrequencyPresets::get_all_presets();
477:     const auto preset_count = DroneFrequencyPresets::get_preset_count();
478: 
479:     using PresetMenuViewT = PresetMenuViewImpl<std::array<DronePreset, 5>>;
480:     nav.push<PresetMenuViewT>(preset_names, preset_count, std::move(callback), all_presets);
481: }
482: 
483: void DronePresetSelector::show_type_filtered_presets(NavigationView& nav, DroneType type) {
484:     const auto& all_presets = DroneFrequencyPresets::get_all_presets();
485:     
486:     static constexpr size_t MAX_FILTERED = 5;
487:     const char* names[MAX_FILTERED];
488:     const DronePreset* filtered_ptrs[MAX_FILTERED];
489:     
490:     const size_t preset_count = filter_presets_by_type_stack(all_presets, type, filtered_ptrs, MAX_FILTERED);
491:     
492:     for (size_t i = 0; i < preset_count; ++i) {
493:         names[i] = filtered_ptrs[i]->display_name;
494:     }
495: 
496:     struct FilteredPresetsView {
497:         const DronePreset* const* presets;
498:         size_t count;
499:         const DronePreset& operator[](size_t idx) const { return *presets[idx]; }
500:         size_t size() const { return count; }
501:     };
502: 
503:     FilteredPresetsView filtered_view{filtered_ptrs, preset_count};
504:     auto on_selected = [&nav](const DronePreset&) { nav.pop(); };
505: 
506:     using FilteredPresetMenuViewT = PresetMenuViewImpl<FilteredPresetsView>;
507:     nav.push<FilteredPresetMenuViewT>(names, preset_count, std::move(on_selected), filtered_view);
508: }

512:         DroneFrequencyPresets::apply_preset(config_to_update, preset);
513:     };
514: }

518: DroneFrequencyEntry::DroneFrequencyEntry(Frequency freq, DroneType type, ThreatLevel threat,
519:                                        int32_t rssi_thresh, uint32_t bw_hz, const char* desc)
520:     : frequency_hz(freq), drone_type(type), threat_level(threat),
521:       rssi_threshold_db(rssi_thresh), bandwidth_hz(bw_hz), description(desc) {}
522: 
523: bool DroneFrequencyEntry::is_valid() const {
524:     return DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::validate_frequency(frequency_hz) &&
525:            rssi_threshold_db >= -120 && rssi_threshold_db <= 0 &&
526:            bandwidth_hz > 0;
527: }

540: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: constexpr LUT для SpectrumMode  index conversion
541: // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
542: // Экономия RAM: LUT хранится во Flash, ноль heap allocation
543: // Ускорение: O(1) lookup вместо 5-branch switch
544: static constexpr uint8_t SPECTRUM_MODE_TO_INDEX_LUT[] = {
545:     1,  // SpectrumMode::NARROW (0)  OptionsField index 1 ("Narrow")
546:     2,  // SpectrumMode::MEDIUM (1)  OptionsField index 2 ("Medium")
547:     3,  // SpectrumMode::WIDE (2)  OptionsField index 3 ("Wide")
548:     4,  // SpectrumMode::ULTRA_WIDE (3)  OptionsField index 4 ("Ultra Wide")
549:     0   // SpectrumMode::ULTRA_NARROW (4)  OptionsField index 0 ("Ultra Narrow")
550: };
551: static_assert(sizeof(SPECTRUM_MODE_TO_INDEX_LUT) == 5, "SPECTRUM_MODE_TO_INDEX_LUT size");
552: 
553: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: constexpr LUT для index  SpectrumMode conversion
554: // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
555: // Экономия RAM: LUT хранится во Flash, ноль heap allocation
556: // Ускорение: O(1) lookup вместо 5-branch switch
557: static constexpr SpectrumMode INDEX_TO_SPECTRUM_MODE_LUT[] = {
558:     SpectrumMode::ULTRA_NARROW,  // index 0 (OptionsField "Ultra Narrow")
559:     SpectrumMode::NARROW,        // index 1 (OptionsField "Narrow")
560:     SpectrumMode::MEDIUM,         // index 2 (OptionsField "Medium")
561:     SpectrumMode::WIDE,           // index 3 (OptionsField "Wide")
562:     SpectrumMode::ULTRA_WIDE      // index 4 (OptionsField "Ultra Wide")
563: };
564: static_assert(sizeof(INDEX_TO_SPECTRUM_MODE_LUT) / sizeof(SpectrumMode) == 5, "INDEX_TO_SPECTRUM_MODE_LUT size");

566: void HardwareSettingsView::load_current_settings() {
567:     DroneAnalyzerSettings settings;
568:     if (!SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::load(settings)) SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::reset_to_defaults(settings);
569:     checkbox_real_hardware_.set_value(settings.hardware_flags.enable_real_hardware);
570:     settings.hardware_flags.enable_real_hardware = checkbox_real_hardware_.value();
571:     settings.hardware_flags.demo_mode = !checkbox_real_hardware_.value();
572: 
573:     // Validate settings before saving
574:     if (!SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::validate(settings)) {
575:         nav_.display_modal("Error", "Invalid settings detected");
576:         return;
577:     }
578: 
579:     SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::save(settings);
580: }

631: void ScanningSettingsView::on_show_presets() {
632:     // Show presets menu using DronePresetSelector
633:     // Create callback that updates settings when preset is selected

635:         DroneAnalyzerSettings settings;
636:         SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::load(settings);
637:         if (DroneFrequencyPresets::apply_preset(settings, preset)) {
638:             SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::save(settings);
639:             nav_.display_modal("Success", std::string("Preset applied: ") + preset.display_name);
640:             load_current_settings();
641:         } else {
642:             nav_.display_modal("Error", "Failed to apply preset");
643:         }
644:     };
645:     DronePresetSelector::show_preset_menu(nav_, on_preset_selected);
646: }

697: // DroneDatabaseManager
698: std::vector<DroneDbEntry> DroneDatabaseManager::load_database(const std::string& file_path) {
699:     std::vector<DroneDbEntry> entries;
700:     File file;
701:     if (!file.open(file_path, true)) return entries;
702:     std::string content;
703:     content.resize(file.size());
704:     file.read(content.data(), file.size());
705:     file.close();
706:     std::stringstream ss(content);
707:     std::string line;
708:     while (std::getline(ss, line)) {
709:         if (!line.empty() && line.back() == '\r') line.pop_back();
710:         if (line.empty() || line[0] == '#') continue;
711:         std::vector<std::string> tokens;
712:         std::stringstream line_ss(line);
713:         std::string token;
714:         while (std::getline(line_ss, token, ',')) tokens.push_back(token);
715:         DroneDbEntry entry;
716:         if (tokens.size() >= 3) {
717:             entry.freq = std::strtoull(tokens[0].c_str(), nullptr, 10);
718:             entry.description = tokens[2] + " (R)";
719:         } else if (tokens.size() >= 2) {
720:             entry.freq = std::strtoull(tokens[0].c_str(), nullptr, 10);
721:             entry.description = tokens[1];
722:         }
723:         if (entry.freq > 0) entries.push_back(entry);
724:     }
725:     return entries;
726: }
727: bool DroneDatabaseManager::save_database(const std::vector<DroneDbEntry>& entries, const std::string& file_path) {
728:     std::stringstream ss;
729:     ss << "frequency_a,frequency_b,description\n# EDA User Database\n";
730:     for (const auto& entry : entries) {
731:         if (entry.freq == 0) continue;
732:         std::string safe_desc = entry.description;
733:         std::replace(safe_desc.begin(), safe_desc.end(), ',', ' ');
734:         std::replace(safe_desc.begin(), safe_desc.end(), '\n', ' ');
735:         std::replace(safe_desc.begin(), safe_desc.end(), '\r', ' ');
736:         ss << entry.freq << "," << safe_desc << "\n";
737:     }
738:     std::string content = ss.str();
739:     File file;
740:     if (!file.open(file_path, false)) return false;
741:     file.write(content.data(), content.size());
742:     file.close();
743:     return true;
744: }
745: 
746: // DroneEntryEditorView
747: DroneEntryEditorView::DroneEntryEditorView(NavigationView& nav, const DroneDbEntry& entry, OnSaveCallback callback)
748:     : View(), nav_(nav), entry_(entry), on_save_(callback) {
749:     add_children({&text_freq_, &field_freq_, &text_desc_, &field_desc_, &button_save_, &button_cancel_});
750:     field_freq_.set_value(entry_.freq);
751:     button_save_.on_select = [this](Button&) { on_save(); };
752:     button_cancel_.on_select = [this](Button&) { on_cancel(); };
753: }
754: void DroneEntryEditorView::focus() { field_freq_.focus(); }
755: void DroneEntryEditorView::on_save() {
756:     DroneDbEntry new_entry;
757:     new_entry.freq = field_freq_.value();
758:     new_entry.description = entry_.description;
759:     if (on_save_) on_save_(new_entry);
760:     nav_.pop();
761: }
762: void DroneEntryEditorView::on_cancel() {
763:     if (on_save_) on_save_({0, ""});
764:     nav_.pop();
765: }

767: // DroneDatabaseListView
768: DroneDatabaseListView::DroneDatabaseListView(NavigationView& nav) : View(), nav_(nav), entries_() {
769:     add_children({&menu_view_});
770:     entries_ = DroneDatabaseManager::load_database();
771:     reload_list();
772: }
773: void DroneDatabaseListView::focus() { menu_view_.focus(); }
774: void DroneDatabaseListView::reload_list() {
775:     menu_view_.clear();
776:     menu_view_.add_item({"[ + ADD NEW FREQUENCY ]", Color::white(), nullptr, nullptr});
777:     for (const auto& entry : entries_) {
778:         std::string freq_str = to_string_short_freq(entry.freq);
779:         std::string text = freq_str + ": " + entry.description;
780:         menu_view_.add_item({text, Color::white(), nullptr, nullptr});
781:     }
782: }
783: void DroneDatabaseListView::on_entry_selected(size_t index) {
784:     if (index == 0) {
785:         DroneDbEntry empty_entry;
786:         nav_.push<DroneEntryEditorView>(empty_entry, [this](const DroneDbEntry& entry) {
787:             if (entry.freq != 0) {
788:                 entries_.push_back(entry);
789:                 save_changes();
790:                 reload_list();
791:             }
792:         });
793:     } else {
794:         size_t entry_index = index - 1;
795:         nav_.push<DroneEntryEditorView>(entries_[entry_index], [this, entry_index](const DroneDbEntry& entry) {
796:             if (entry.freq != 0) {
797:                 entries_[entry_index] = entry;
798:                 save_changes();
799:                 reload_list();
800:             }
801:         });
802:     }
803: }
804: void DroneDatabaseListView::save_changes() { DroneDatabaseManager::save_database(entries_); }
805: bool DroneDatabaseListView::on_key(const KeyEvent key) {
806:     if (key == KeyEvent::Select) {
807:         size_t index = menu_view_.highlighted_index();
808:         on_entry_selected(index);
809:         return true;
810:     }
811:     return View::on_key(key);
812: }

63: // DIAMOND FIX: Global SD Card Mutex Protection
64: // FatFS is NOT thread-safe - all SD operations must be serialized
65: // ===========================================
66: 
67: extern Mutex sd_card_mutex;
68: 
69: // RAII wrapper for automatic SD card lock/unlock
70: class SDCardLock {
71: public:
72:     SDCardLock() {
73:         chMtxLock(&sd_card_mutex);
74:     }
75:     ~SDCardLock() {
76:         chMtxUnlock();
77:     }
78:     SDCardLock(const SDCardLock&) = delete;
79:     SDCardLock& operator=(const SDCardLock&) = delete;
80: };

98:     static constexpr Style GREEN_STYLE{font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::green()};
99:     static constexpr Style LIGHT_STYLE{font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::white()};
100:     static constexpr Style DARK_STYLE{font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::dark_grey()};
101:     static constexpr Style ORANGE_STYLE{font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::orange()};
102: }
103: 
104: class TrackedDrone {
105: public:
106:     TrackedDrone() : frequency(0), drone_type(static_cast<uint8_t>(DroneType::UNKNOWN)),
107:                      threat_level(static_cast<uint8_t>(ThreatLevel::NONE)), update_count(0),
108:                      last_seen(0), rssi(-120), rssi_history_{}, timestamp_history_{}, history_index_(0) {
109:         // Initialize array with "silence" (-120 dBm), not zeros
110:         std::fill(std::begin(rssi_history_), std::end(rssi_history_), -120);
111:         std::fill(std::begin(timestamp_history_), std::end(timestamp_history_), 0);
112:     }
113: 
114:     TrackedDrone& operator=(const TrackedDrone& other) {
115:         if (this != &other) {
116:             frequency = other.frequency;
117:             drone_type = other.drone_type;
118:             threat_level = other.threat_level;
119:             update_count = other.update_count;
120:             last_seen = other.last_seen;
121:             rssi = other.rssi;
122:             for(size_t i=0; i<MAX_HISTORY; i++) {
123:                 rssi_history_[i] = other.rssi_history_[i];
124:                 timestamp_history_[i] = other.timestamp_history_[i];
125:             }
126:             history_index_ = other.history_index_;
127:         }
128:         return *this;
129:     }
130: 
131:     void add_rssi(const RssiMeasurement& measurement) {
132:         rssi_history_[history_index_] = measurement.rssi_db;
133:         timestamp_history_[history_index_] = measurement.timestamp_ms;
134:         history_index_ = (history_index_ + 1) % MAX_HISTORY;
135: 
136:         this->rssi = measurement.rssi_db;
137: 
138:         if (measurement.timestamp_ms > last_seen) {
139:             last_seen = measurement.timestamp_ms;
140:             if (update_count < 255) update_count++;
141:         }
142:     }
143: 
144:     MovementTrend get_trend() const {
145:         if (update_count < 4) return MovementTrend::UNKNOWN;
146: 
147:         int32_t recent_sum = 0;
148:         int32_t older_sum = 0;
149:         size_t half_window = MAX_HISTORY / 2;
150: 
151:         for (size_t i = 0; i < MAX_HISTORY; i++) {
152:             size_t logical_idx = (history_index_ + i) % MAX_HISTORY;
153:             int16_t val = rssi_history_[logical_idx];
154:             if (val <= -110) continue;
155: 
156:             if (i < half_window) {
157:                 older_sum += val;
158:             } else {
159:                 recent_sum += val;
160:             }
161:         }
162: 
163:         int32_t avg_old = older_sum / (int32_t)half_window;
164:         int32_t avg_new = recent_sum / (int32_t)half_window;
165:         int32_t diff = avg_new - avg_old;
166: 
167:         if (diff > 3) return MovementTrend::APPROACHING;
168:         if (diff < -3) return MovementTrend::RECEDING;
169:         return MovementTrend::STATIC;
170:     }
171: 
172:     uint32_t frequency;
173:     uint8_t drone_type;
174:     uint8_t threat_level;
175:     uint8_t update_count;
176:     systime_t last_seen;
177:     int32_t rssi = -120;
178: 
179: private:
180:     static constexpr size_t MAX_HISTORY = 8;
181:     int16_t rssi_history_[MAX_HISTORY];
182:     systime_t timestamp_history_[MAX_HISTORY] = {0};
183:     size_t history_index_ = 0;
184: };
185:

193:     Color display_color = Color::white();
194:     MovementTrend trend = MovementTrend::UNKNOWN;

274: // RAII wrapper for ChibiOS mutexes
275: class MutexLock {
276: public:
277:     explicit MutexLock(Mutex& mtx) : mtx_(mtx) {
278:         chMtxLock(&mtx_);
279:     }
280: 
281:     ~MutexLock() {
282:         chMtxUnlock();
283:     }
284: 
285:     MutexLock(const MutexLock&) = delete;
286:     MutexLock& operator=(const MutexLock&) = delete;
287: 
288: private:
289:     Mutex& mtx_;
290: };

292: // ?? OPTIMIZATION: String Pool for heap fragmentation reduction
293: // Scott Meyers Item 29: Consider using object pools for frequently allocated objects
294: class StringPool {
295: public:
296:     static constexpr size_t POOL_SIZE = 2048;
297:     static constexpr size_t MAX_STRING_LENGTH = 256;
298: 
299:     StringPool() : pool_{}, offset_(0) {
300:     }
301: 
302:     char* allocate(size_t length) {
303:         if (length >= MAX_STRING_LENGTH) return nullptr;
304: 
305:         // Check if we have enough space
306:         if (offset_ + length + 1 >= POOL_SIZE) {
307:             // Pool full - reset to beginning (simple circular buffer)
308:             offset_ = 0;
309:         }
310: 
311:         char* result = pool_ + offset_;
312:         offset_ += length + 1;
313:         pool_[offset_ - 1] = '\0';  // Null-terminate
314:         return result;
315:     }
316: 
317:     void reset() {
318:         offset_ = 0;
319:     }
320: 
321:     StringPool(const StringPool&) = delete;
322:     StringPool& operator=(const StringPool&) = delete;
323: 
324: private:
325:     char pool_[POOL_SIZE];
326:     size_t offset_;
327: };

653:         &DroneScanner::approaching_count_, // APPROACHING = 1
654:         &DroneScanner::receding_count_,    // RECEDING = 2
655:         &DroneScanner::static_count_       // UNKNOWN = 3 (fallback)
656:     };
657:     static_assert(sizeof(TREND_COUNTERS) / sizeof(size_t DroneScanner::*) == 4, "TREND_COUNTERS size");
658:     
659:     // LUT для функций сканирования (указатели на методы класса)
660:     static constexpr void (DroneScanner::* const SCAN_FUNCTIONS[])(DroneHardwareController&) = {
661:         &DroneScanner::perform_database_scan_cycle,    // DATABASE = 0
662:         &DroneScanner::perform_wideband_scan_cycle,   // WIDEBAND_CONTINUOUS = 1
663:         &DroneScanner::perform_hybrid_scan_cycle        // HYBRID = 2
664:     };
665:     static_assert(sizeof(SCAN_FUNCTIONS) / sizeof(void (DroneScanner::*)(DroneHardwareController&)) == 3, "SCAN_FUNCTIONS size");
666: };

668: class DroneHardwareController {
669: public:
670:     explicit DroneHardwareController(SpectrumMode mode = SpectrumMode::MEDIUM);
671:     ~DroneHardwareController();
672: 
673:     void initialize_hardware();
674:     void on_hardware_show();
675:     void on_hardware_hide();
676:     void shutdown_hardware();
677: 
678:     void set_spectrum_mode(SpectrumMode mode);
679:     uint32_t get_spectrum_bandwidth() const;
680:     void set_spectrum_bandwidth(uint32_t bandwidth_hz);
681:     Frequency get_spectrum_center_frequency() const;
682:     void set_spectrum_center_frequency(Frequency center_freq);
683: 
684:     bool tune_to_frequency(Frequency frequency_hz);
685:     void start_spectrum_streaming();
686:     void stop_spectrum_streaming();
687:     int32_t get_real_rssi_from_hardware(Frequency target_frequency);
688:     bool is_spectrum_streaming_active() const;
689:     int32_t get_current_rssi() const;
690:     void update_spectrum_for_scanner();
691: 
692:     void stop_spectrum_before_scan();
693:     void resume_spectrum_after_scan();
694:     bool is_spectrum_compatible_with_scanning() const;
695:     
696:     void clear_rssi_flag();
697:     bool is_rssi_fresh() const;
698:     
699:     // ?? FIXED: TOCTOU race condition - atomic check-and-fetch method
700:     bool get_rssi_if_fresh(int32_t& out_rssi) {
701:         // Atomic check-and-fetch to prevent TOCTOU race
702:         bool was_fresh = rssi_updated_.exchange(false, std::memory_order_acq_rel);
703:         if (was_fresh) {
704:             out_rssi = last_valid_rssi_.load(std::memory_order_acquire);
705:         }
706:         return was_fresh;
707:     }
708: 
709:     // NEW: Spectrum data access method (atomic check-and-fetch to avoid TOCTOU race)
710:     bool get_latest_spectrum_if_fresh(std::array<uint8_t, 256>& out_db_buffer) {
711:         // Atomic check-and-fetch to prevent TOCTOU race
712:         bool was_fresh = spectrum_updated_.exchange(false, std::memory_order_acq_rel);
713:         if (was_fresh) {
714:             MutexLock lock(spectrum_mutex_);
715:             out_db_buffer = last_spectrum_db_;
716:         }
717:         return was_fresh;
718:     }
719:     bool try_get_latest_spectrum(std::array<uint8_t, 256>& out_db_buffer) {
720:         MutexLock lock(spectrum_mutex_);
721:         out_db_buffer = last_spectrum_db_;
722:         return true;
723:     }
724:     void clear_spectrum_flag() {
725:         spectrum_updated_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
726:     }
727: 
728:     // ?? FIX: Public method to set spectrum FIFO (called from parent View)
729:     void set_spectrum_fifo(ChannelSpectrumFIFO* fifo) {
730:         spectrum_fifo_ = fifo;
731:     }
732: 
733:     void handle_channel_spectrum_config(const ChannelSpectrumConfigMessage* const message);
734:     void handle_channel_statistics(const ChannelStatistics& statistics);
735:     void handle_channel_spectrum(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum);
736:     void process_channel_spectrum_data(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum);
737: 
738:     DroneHardwareController(const DroneHardwareController&) = delete;
739:     DroneHardwareController& operator=(const DroneHardwareController&) = delete;
740: 
741: private:
742:     void initialize_radio_state();
743:     void initialize_spectrum_collector();
744:     void cleanup_spectrum_collector();
745: 
746:     int32_t get_configured_sampling_rate() const;
747:     int32_t get_configured_bandwidth() const;
748:     
749:     // ?? FIX: Spectrum data buffer and synchronization
750:     std::array<uint8_t, 256> last_spectrum_db_;
751:     mutable Mutex spectrum_mutex_;
752:     
753:     // ?? FIX: Replace volatile with atomic with explicit memory ordering
754:     std::atomic<bool> spectrum_updated_{false};
755: 
756:     SpectrumMode spectrum_mode_;
757:     Frequency center_frequency_;
758:     uint32_t bandwidth_hz_;
759:     RxRadioState radio_state_;
760:     ChannelSpectrumFIFO* spectrum_fifo_ = nullptr;
761:     bool spectrum_streaming_active_ = false;
762:     
763:     // ?? FIX: Replace volatile with atomic with explicit memory ordering
764:     std::atomic<bool> rssi_updated_{false};
765:     std::atomic<int32_t> last_valid_rssi_{-120};
766:     
767:     // ?? FIX: Moved message handlers to parent View to prevent MsgDblReg
768:     // Only ChannelStatistics handler remains here as it's unique
769:     
770:     MessageHandlerRegistration message_handler_channel_statistics_ {
771:         Message::ID::ChannelStatistics,
772:         [this](Message* const p) {
773:             const auto statistics_msg = static_cast<const ChannelStatisticsMessage*>(p);
774:             this->handle_channel_statistics(statistics_msg->statistics);
775:         }
776:     };
777: };

1276:     // ФАЗА 1.1: СТАТИЧЕСКИЕ БУФЕРЫ (Zero-Heap)
1277:     // ===========================================
1278:     // Diamond Code Principle: All data must be static or stack-based
1279:     // Используем inline статические массивы вместо unique_ptr
1280: 
1281:     // Статические буферы (хранятся в .bss, инициализируются нулями)
1282:     // Размер: SPECTRUM_ROW_SIZE * sizeof(Color) = 240 * 2 = 480 байт
1283:     // Размер: RENDER_LINE_SIZE * sizeof(Color) = 240 * 2 = 480 байт
1284:     // Размер: 200 * sizeof(uint8_t) = 200 байт
1285:     // Итого: ~1.16 KB в .bss вместо heap allocation
1286: 
1287:     alignas(alignof(std::array<Color, SPECTRUM_ROW_SIZE>))
1288:     static inline Color spectrum_row_buffer_storage_[SPECTRUM_ROW_SIZE];

1293:     alignas(alignof(std::array<uint8_t, 200>))

1326:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: анализ формы сигнала для bar spectrum (без SpectralAnalyzer)
1327:     inline size_t get_bar_color_index(size_t x, uint8_t power) const {
1328:         // ?? ФАЗА 1.5: Для статических буферов проверка упрощается
1329:         if (!buffers_allocated_) {
1330:             return 2; // Unknown/Noise (Grey)
1331:         }
1332: 
1333:         // Острый пик (narrowband drone control): текущее > соседей на 15+
1334:         // Широкий сигнал (wideband video/WiFi): все примерно равны
1335:         const auto& levels = spectrum_power_levels();
1336:         if (x > 0 && x < levels.size() - 1) {
1337:             uint8_t prev = levels[x - 1];
1338:             uint8_t next = levels[x + 1];
1339: 
1340:             // Логика "Острого пика": текущий ВЫШЕ соседей на 15+ единиц
1341:             if (power > prev + BarSpectrumConfig::PEAK_SHARPNESS_THRESHOLD &&
1342:                 power > next + BarSpectrumConfig::PEAK_SHARPNESS_THRESHOLD) {
1343:                 return 1; // Sharp Peak (Red)
1344:             }
1345:         }
1346: 
1347:         // Широкий сигнал: Blue
1348:         return 0; // Wideband (Blue)
1349:     }
1350: 
1351: 
1352:     void handle_channel_spectrum(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum);
1353:     void analyze_spectrum_for_threats(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum);
1354:     Frequency spectrum_bin_to_frequency(size_t bin) const;
1355:     void update_or_create_drone_from_spectrum(Frequency freq_hz, uint8_t power);
1356: };

1451:     // ===========================================
1452:     // INITIALIZATION STATE
1453:     // ===========================================
1454:     // ?? ФАЗА 2.1: Deferred initialization state machine
1455:     enum class InitState : uint8_t {
1456:         CONSTRUCTED = 0,           // Constructor completed
1457:         BUFFERS_ALLOCATED,         // display buffers heap-allocated
1458:         DATABASE_LOADED,           // scanner_.initialize_database_and_scanner() completed
1459:         HARDWARE_READY,            // hardware_.on_hardware_show() completed
1460:         UI_LAYOUT_READY,           // initialize_modern_layout() completed
1461:         SETTINGS_LOADED,           // SettingsPersistence::load() completed
1462:          COORDINATOR_READY,         // coordinator thread creation prepared
1463:          FULLY_INITIALIZED = 7,     // Ready for operation
1464:          INITIALIZATION_ERROR = 8   // Timeout or critical error (NEW!)
1465:      };
1466: 
1467:  private:
1468:     // ?? DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Forward declarations for phase initialization methods
1469:     // Scott Meyers Item 11: Handle assignment to self in operator=
1470:     // These methods declared here for use in constexpr LUT
1471:     void init_phase_allocate_buffers();
1472:     void init_phase_load_database();
1473:     void init_phase_init_hardware();
1474:     void init_phase_setup_ui();
1475:     void init_phase_load_settings();
1476:     void init_phase_finalize();
1477: 
1478:     // ===========================================
1479:     // INITIALIZATION TIMING CONSTANTS
1480:     // ===========================================
1481:     // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
1482:     // Eliminates magic numbers, improves maintainability
1483:     struct InitTiming {
1484:         // ===========================================
1485:         // ФАЗА 4.1: ИСПРАВЛЕННЫЕ ЗАДЕРЖКИ
1486:         // ===========================================
1487:         // Задержки указывают, когда ЗАПУСТИТЬ фазу от начала
1488:         // Каждая фаза должна иметь достаточное время для выполнения
1489: 
1490:         static constexpr uint32_t TIMEOUT_MS = 15000;  // 15 сек (увеличено)
1491:         static constexpr uint32_t PHASE_INTERVAL_MS = 50;
1492: 
1493:         // Кумулятивные задержки (каждая фаза + минимум 200мс на выполнение)
1494:         static constexpr uint32_t PHASE_DELAY_0_MS = 50;     // Allocate buffers
1495:         static constexpr uint32_t PHASE_DELAY_1_MS = 300;    // Database (50 + 250 for async)
1496:         static constexpr uint32_t PHASE_DELAY_2_MS = 500;    // Hardware (300 + 200)
1497:         static constexpr uint32_t PHASE_DELAY_3_MS = 700;    // UI Setup (500 + 200)
1498:         static constexpr uint32_t PHASE_DELAY_4_MS = 900;    // Settings (700 + 200)
1499:         static constexpr uint32_t PHASE_DELAY_5_MS = 1100;   // Finalize (900 + 200)
1500: 
1501:         static constexpr uint8_t MAX_PHASES = 6;
1502:     };
1503:

1505:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: constexpr LUT для сообщений инициализации в Flash
1506:     static constexpr const char* const INIT_STATUS_MESSAGES[] = {
1507:         "Starting up...",      // CONSTRUCTED = 0
1508:         "Buffers ready",       // BUFFERS_ALLOCATED = 1
1509:         "Database ready",      // DATABASE_LOADED = 2
1510:         "Hardware ready",      // HARDWARE_READY = 3
1511:         "UI ready",            // UI_LAYOUT_READY = 4
1512:         "Settings loaded",     // SETTINGS_LOADED = 5 (NEW!)
1513:         "Coordinator ready",   // COORDINATOR_READY = 6
1514:         "All systems go"       // FULLY_INITIALIZED = 7
1515:     };

1519:     };

1521:     // ?? DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: constexpr LUT для фаз инициализации (хранится во Flash)
1522:     // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
1523:     // Phase dependencies documented:
1524:     //   Phase 0 (Allocate): No dependencies
1525:     //   Phase 1 (Database):  Requires Phase 0 (buffers)
1526:     //   Phase 2 (Hardware):  Requires Phase 1 (database)
1527:     //   Phase 3 (UI Setup):   Requires Phase 2 (hardware)
1528:     //   Phase 4 (Settings):   Requires Phase 3 (UI layout)
1529:     //   Phase 5 (Finalize):   Requires Phase 4 (settings)
1530:     struct InitPhaseConfig {
1531:         const char* const name;           // Строка во Flash (const char*)
1532:         uint32_t delay_ms;               // Задержка в мс
1533:         void (EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::*init_func)();  // Сырой указатель на метод
1534:     };
1535: 
1536:     static constexpr InitPhaseConfig INIT_PHASES[] = {

1538:         {"Loading database...",     InitTiming::PHASE_DELAY_1_MS, &EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_load_database},
1539:         {"Initializing hardware...", InitTiming::PHASE_DELAY_2_MS, &EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_init_hardware},
1540:         {"Setting up UI...",        InitTiming::PHASE_DELAY_3_MS, &EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_setup_ui},
1541:         {"Loading settings...",     InitTiming::PHASE_DELAY_4_MS, &EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_load_settings},
1542:         {"Finalizing...",           InitTiming::PHASE_DELAY_5_MS, &EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_finalize}
1543:     };

1560:     // ===========================================
1561:     // Scott Meyers Effective C++ Item 12: Never change the order of member initialization
1562:     // C++ initialization order: members are initialized in DECLARATION order, NOT init-list order
1563:     //
1564:     // Dependencies:
1565:     //   settings_               - No dependencies (declared first)
1566:     //   hardware_               - No dependencies
1567:     //   scanner_                - Depends on settings_
1568:     //   audio_                  - No dependencies
1569:     //   display_controller_      - No dependencies

1571:     //   scanning_coordinator_   - Depends on hardware_, scanner_, display_controller_, audio_
1572:     //   smart_header_            - No dependencies
1573:     //   status_bar_              - No dependencies
1574:     //   threat_cards_            - No dependencies
1575:     //   button_*                 - No dependencies (initialized in constructor)
1576:     //   field_scanning_mode_     - No dependencies (initialized in constructor)
1577:     //   scanning_active_         - No dependencies (initialized last)
1578:     // ===========================================

1603:     // ?? FIX: Unified message handlers to prevent MsgDblReg

1605:     
1606:     MessageHandlerRegistration message_handler_spectrum_config_ {
1607:         Message::ID::ChannelSpectrumConfig,
1608:         [this](Message* const p) {
1609:             const auto message = *reinterpret_cast<const ChannelSpectrumConfigMessage*>(p);
1610:             // Delegate FIFO pointer to both controllers that need it
1611:             hardware_.set_spectrum_fifo(message.fifo);
1612:             display_controller_.set_spectrum_fifo(message.fifo);
1613:         }
1614:     };
1615: 
1616:     MessageHandlerRegistration message_handler_frame_sync_ {
1617:         Message::ID::DisplayFrameSync,
1618:         [this](Message* const) {
1619:             // ?? DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Enhanced initialization with timeout protection
1620:             // Executed every frame (~16ms at 60 FPS)
1621:             if (init_state_ == InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR) {
1622:                 // Не обновляем UI, ошибка уже показана
1623:                 return;
1624:             }
1625:             
1626:             if (init_state_ != InitState::FULLY_INITIALIZED) {
1627:                 step_deferred_initialization();
1628:                 // Return early if not fully initialized
1629:                 return;
1630:             }
1631: 
1632:             // ?? SAFETY: Проверка валидности буферов перед операциями
1633:             if (!display_controller_.are_buffers_valid()) {
1634:                 return;
1635:             }
1636: 
1637:             // Normal operation mode
1638:             // 1. Process spectrum data in display controller
1639:             display_controller_.process_frame_sync();
1640: 
1641:             // 2. Handle scanner updates in main view
1642:             this->handle_scanner_update();
1643:         }
1644:     };
1645: 
1646:     void start_scanning_thread();
1647:     void stop_scanning_thread();
1648:     bool handle_start_stop_button();
1649:     bool handle_menu_button();
1650:     void initialize_modern_layout();
1651:     void update_modern_layout();
1652:     void handle_scanner_update();
1653:     void setup_button_handlers();
1654:     void initialize_scanning_mode();
1655:     void set_scanning_mode_from_index(size_t index);
1656:     void add_ui_elements();

1660:     void update_init_progress_display();

1664:     systime_t init_start_time_ = 0;
1665:     systime_t last_init_progress_ = 0;
1666:     bool initialization_in_progress_ = false;
1667:

FILE: ui_enhanced_drone_analyzer.cpp 
======================================== 
 
1: /**
2:  * Enhanced Drone Analyzer - Thread Safety Notes
3:  *
4:  * Locking Order (to prevent deadlocks):
5:  * 1. scanning_active_ (std::atomic<bool>) - No lock needed
6:  * 2. data_mutex (DroneScanner::tracked_drones_)
7:  * 3. spectrum_mutex (DroneHardwareController::spectrum_buffer_)
8:  * 4. logger_mutex (DroneDetectionLogger::mutex_)
9:  *
10:  * Rules:
11:  * - Always acquire locks in order 1->2->3->4
12:  * - Never acquire a lower-numbered lock while holding a higher-numbered lock
13:  * - Use MutexLock RAII wrapper for automatic unlock
14:  * - Keep critical sections as short as possible
15:  * 
16:  * If something doesn't load at all, at least it doesn't freeze and immediately crash. Which means the code is potentially alive. You all know perfectly well that running so many lines of code is already an achievement.
17:  * 
18:  * I'm just here for fun. I had this idea to cram 8,000 lines into an outdated controller and that's it. Code for me is like painting a picture. I want it abstract, extensive, and yet solid.
19:  * 
20:  */
21:

82: // ФАЗА 0.1: HEAP DIAGNOSTICS
83: // ===========================================
84: namespace HeapDiagnostics {
85:     extern "C" {
86:         extern uint8_t __heap_base__;
87:         extern uint8_t __heap_end__;
88:     }
89: 
90:     inline size_t get_heap_total() {
91:         return &__heap_end__ - &__heap_base__;
92:     }
93:     
94:     inline size_t get_heap_free() {
95:         size_t free = 0;
96:         chHeapStatus(nullptr, &free);
97:         return free;
98:     }
99:     
100:     inline size_t get_heap_used() {
101:         return get_heap_total() - get_heap_free();
102:     }
103:     
104:     inline void log_heap_status(const char* phase) {
105:         size_t used = get_heap_used();
106:         size_t total = get_heap_total();
107:         if (total > 0 && used < total) {
108:             uint8_t percent = static_cast<uint8_t>((used * 100) / total);
109:             char buf[64];
110:             snprintf(buf, sizeof(buf), "%s heap: %lu/%lu (%d%%)", 
111:                      phase,
112:                      static_cast<unsigned long>(used),
113:                      static_cast<unsigned long>(total),
114:                      percent);
115:             // Вывод через status bar или debug console
116:             // Здесь буферизация для последующего использования
117:         }
118:     }
119: }

130: DisplayDroneEntry DroneDisplayController::detected_drones_storage_[DroneDisplayController::MAX_UI_DRONES];

144: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Deprecated parse_settings_line_inplace removed (~60 lines)
145: // Now using SettingsPersistence<T> from settings_persistence.hpp
146: // Scott Meyers Item 11: Handle assignment to self in operator=
147: 
148: bool load_settings_from_sd_card(DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings) {
149:     (void)settings;  // Suppress unused parameter warning
150:     File settings_file;
151:     auto error = settings_file.open("/sdcard/ENHANCED_DRONE_ANALYZER_SETTINGS.txt");
152:     if (error) return false;
153: 
154:     char read_buffer[256];       // Increased buffer size for safety
155:     char line_buffer[256];       // Increased buffer size to handle long lines
156:     size_t line_idx = 0;
157:     size_t discarded_bytes = 0;  // Counter for dropped bytes
158: 
159:     while (true) {
160:         // Read block
161:         auto read_res = settings_file.read(read_buffer, sizeof(read_buffer));
162:         if (read_res.is_error()) break;
163: 
164:         size_t bytes_read = read_res.value();
165:         if (bytes_read == 0) break; // EOF
166: 
167:         // Process the read block
168:         for (size_t i = 0; i < bytes_read; i++) {
169:             char c = read_buffer[i];
170: 
171:             if (c == '\n') {
172:                 // End of line found
173:                 line_buffer[line_idx] = 0; // Null-terminate
174: 
175:                 // ===========================================
176:                 // DEPRECATED: parse_settings_line_inplace REPLACED
177:                 // Use SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::load(settings) instead
178:                 // ===========================================
179:                 // parse_settings_line_inplace(line_buffer, settings);
180: 
181:         // Reset for next line
182:         line_idx = 0;
183:             }
184:             else if (c != '\r') {
185:                 // Ignore \r, accumulate other characters
186:                 if (line_idx < sizeof(line_buffer) - 1) {
187:                     line_buffer[line_idx++] = c;
188:                 } else {
189:                     // Count discarded bytes when line exceeds buffer
190:                     discarded_bytes++;
191:                 }
192:             }
193:         }
194:     }
195: 
196:     // ===========================================
197:     // DEPRECATED: parse_settings_line_inplace REPLACED
198:     // Use SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::load(settings) instead
199:     // ===========================================
200:     // Process last line if file doesn't end with \n
201:     if (line_idx > 0) {
202:         line_buffer[line_idx] = 0;
203:         // parse_settings_line_inplace(line_buffer, settings);
204:     }
205: 
206:     // Log discarded bytes for debugging (could be expanded to actual logging)
207:     (void)discarded_bytes;
208: 
209:     return true;
210: }

267:     : scanning_thread_(nullptr),
268:         data_mutex(),
269:         scanning_active_(false),
270:         freq_db_ptr_(nullptr),  // ?? FIX: Defer heap allocation to after constructor
271:         tracked_drones_ptr_(nullptr),  // ?? FIX: Defer heap allocation
272:         freq_db_loaded_(false),
273:         current_db_index_(0),
274:         last_scanned_frequency_(0),
275:         db_loading_thread_(nullptr),
276:         db_loading_active_{false},
277:         scan_cycles_(0),
278:         total_detections_(0),
279:         scanning_mode_(DroneScanner::ScanningMode::DATABASE),
280:         is_real_mode_(true),
281:           tracked_count_(0),
282:           approaching_count_(0),
283:           receding_count_(0),
284:           static_count_(0),
285:           max_detected_threat_(ThreatLevel::NONE),
286:           last_valid_rssi_(-120),
287:            wideband_scan_data_(),

307: DroneScanner::~DroneScanner() {
308:     stop_scanning();
309:     cleanup_database_and_scanner();
310:     // Note: ChibiOS mutexes are automatically cleaned up with the object.
311:     // No explicit deinitialization needed - mutex is part of thread context.
312: }
