314: void DroneScanner::initialize_wideband_scanning() {
315:     wideband_scan_data_.reset();
316:     setup_wideband_range(WIDEBAND_DEFAULT_MIN, WIDEBAND_DEFAULT_MAX);
317: }
318: 
319: void DroneScanner::setup_wideband_range(Frequency min_freq, Frequency max_freq) {
320:     // Use unified frequency limits from DroneConstants
321:     Frequency safe_min = std::max(min_freq, DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ);
322:     Frequency safe_max = std::min(max_freq, DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ);
323: 
324:     // Ensure min < max and apply hardware constraints
325:     if (safe_min >= safe_max) {
326:         safe_min = DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ;
327:         safe_max = DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ;
328:     }
329: 
330:     wideband_scan_data_.min_freq = safe_min;
331:     wideband_scan_data_.max_freq = safe_max;
332: 
333:     Frequency scanning_range = safe_max - safe_min;
334:     if (scanning_range > static_cast<Frequency>(settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz)) {
335:         // Check for integer overflow before calculating slices
336:         // Use int64_t to match rf::Frequency type and avoid sign comparison warning
337:         int64_t range_plus_width = static_cast<int64_t>(scanning_range) + static_cast<int64_t>(settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz);
338:         if (range_plus_width < scanning_range) {
339:             // Overflow detected - handle gracefully with single slice
340:             wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb = 1;
341:         } else {
342:             wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb = (static_cast<uint64_t>(range_plus_width) - 1) / settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz;
343:         }
344: 
345:         if (wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb > WIDEBAND_MAX_SLICES) {
346:             wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb = WIDEBAND_MAX_SLICES;
347:         }
348:         // DIAMOND FIX: Cast to uint64_t before multiplication to prevent overflow
349:         // If slices_nb=50 and width=28MHz, result=1400MHz which overflows uint32_t Frequency
350:         Frequency slices_span = static_cast<Frequency>(static_cast<uint64_t>(wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb) * static_cast<uint64_t>(settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz));
351:         Frequency offset = ((scanning_range - slices_span) / 2) + (settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz / 2);
352:         Frequency center_frequency = safe_min + offset;
353: 
354:         std::generate_n(wideband_scan_data_.slices,
355:                        wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb,
356:                        [&center_frequency, slice_index = 0, this]() mutable -> WidebandSlice {
357:                            WidebandSlice slice;
358:                            slice.center_frequency = center_frequency;
359:                            slice.index = slice_index++;
360:                            center_frequency += settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz;
361:                            return slice;
362:                        });
363:     } else {
364:         wideband_scan_data_.slices[0].center_frequency = (safe_max + safe_min) / 2;
365:         wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb = 1;
366:     }
367:     wideband_scan_data_.slice_counter = 0;
368: }
369: 
370: void DroneScanner::start_scanning() {
371:     if (scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) return;
372: 
373:     scanning_active_.store(true, std::memory_order_release);
374:     scan_cycles_ = 0;
375:     total_detections_ = 0;
376: }
377: 
378: void DroneScanner::stop_scanning() {
379:     if (!scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) return;
380: 
381:     scanning_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
382: 
383:     // Wait for scanning thread to complete
384:     if (scanning_thread_ != nullptr) {
385:         chThdWait(scanning_thread_);
386:         scanning_thread_ = nullptr;
387:     }
388: 
389:     remove_stale_drones();
390: }
391: 
392: bool DroneScanner::load_frequency_database() {
393:     current_db_index_ = 0;
394: 
395:     freqman_load_options options;
396:     options.max_entries = 150;
397:     options.load_freqs = true;
398:     options.load_ranges = true;
399:     options.load_hamradios = true;
400:     options.load_repeaters = true;
401: 
402:     if (!freq_db_ptr_) return false;
403: 
404:     auto db_path = get_freqman_path("DRONES");
405:     bool sd_loaded = freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path);
406: 
407:     {
408:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
409: 
410:         if (!sd_loaded || freq_db_ptr_->empty()) {
411:             freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path, true);
412: 
413:             for (const auto& item : BUILTIN_DRONE_DB) {
414:                 freqman_entry entry{};
415:                 entry.frequency_a = item.freq;
416:                 entry.description = item.desc;
417:                 entry.type = freqman_type::Single;
418:                 entry.modulation = freqman_invalid_index;
419:                 entry.bandwidth = freqman_invalid_index;
420:                 entry.step = freqman_invalid_index;
421:                 entry.tone = freqman_invalid_index;
422:                 freq_db_ptr_->append_entry(entry);
423:             }
424: 
425:             sync_database();
426: 
427:             sd_loaded = !freq_db_ptr_->empty();
428:         }
429:     }
430: 
431:     if (freq_db_ptr_->entry_count() > 100) {
432:         handle_scan_error("Large database loaded");
433:     }
434: 
435:     freq_db_loaded_ = true;
436:     return !freq_db_ptr_->empty();
437: }
438: 
439: size_t DroneScanner::get_database_size() const {
440:     return freq_db_ptr_->entry_count();
441: }
442: 
443: void DroneScanner::set_scanning_mode(ScanningMode mode) {
444:     scanning_mode_ = mode;
445:     stop_scanning();
446:     reset_scan_cycles();
447: 
448:     if (scanning_mode_ == ScanningMode::DATABASE || scanning_mode_ == ScanningMode::HYBRID) {
449:         load_frequency_database();
450:     }
451: }
452: 
453: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: LUT lookup вместо switch для scanning_mode_name()
454: // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
455: // Экономит ~40 байт Flash
456: const char* DroneScanner::scanning_mode_name() const {
457:     uint8_t idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(scanning_mode_);
458:     return (idx < 3) ? SCANNING_MODE_NAMES[idx] : "Unknown";
459: }
460: 
461: void DroneScanner::perform_scan_cycle(DroneHardwareController& hardware) {
462:     if (!scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) return;
463: 
464:     // ?? ENHANCED: Adaptive timing with golden mean between speed and accuracy
465:     // Considering Cortex M4 limitations on Portapack (limited RAM, CPU)
466:     using namespace DroneConstants;
467:     uint32_t base_interval = DEFAULT_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS; // Base interval in milliseconds
468:     uint32_t adaptive_interval = base_interval;
469: 
470:     // Get current scan context
471:     size_t current_detections = get_total_detections();
472:     ThreatLevel max_threat = get_max_detected_threat();
473:     size_t tracked_count = tracked_count_;
474: 
475:     // ADAPTIVE STRATEGY:
476:     // - CRITICAL threats: scan fastest (250ms)
477:     // - HIGH threats: scan fast (400ms)
478:     // - MEDIUM threats: scan normal (750ms)
479:     // - LOW threats: scan slower (1000ms)
480:     // - NO threats: scan progressively slower (up to 2000ms)
481:     // - Balance: faster scanning of known drone bands, slower for empty bands
482: 
483:     if (max_threat >= ThreatLevel::CRITICAL) {
484:         // Critical threat detected - maximum speed scanning
485:         adaptive_interval = FAST_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS; // Fastest possible scan
486:     } else if (max_threat == ThreatLevel::HIGH) {
487:         // High threat - fast scanning
488:         adaptive_interval = 400;
489:     } else if (max_threat == ThreatLevel::MEDIUM) {
490:         // Medium threat - normal scanning
491:         adaptive_interval = NORMAL_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS;
492:     } else if (current_detections > 0 && tracked_count > 0) {
493:         // Have detections but low threat - maintain medium pace
494:         adaptive_interval = SLOW_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS;
495:     } else if (current_detections == 0 && scan_cycles_ > 10) {
496:         // No detections for a while - progressively slow down
497:         // Progressive slowdown: 1000ms  1500ms  2000ms (cap)
498:         uint32_t slowdown_multiplier = std::min(scan_cycles_ / 10, static_cast<uint32_t>(3));
499:         adaptive_interval = std::min(VERY_SLOW_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS, base_interval * slowdown_multiplier);
500:     }
501: 
502:     // Additional adjustment based on detection density
503:     if (current_detections > 5) {
504:         // Very high detection rate - maintain fast pace
505:         adaptive_interval = std::min(adaptive_interval, static_cast<uint32_t>(500));
506:     }
507:     
508:     // Apply adaptive interval
509:     chThdSleepMilliseconds(adaptive_interval);
510: 
511:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: LUT lookup вместо switch для perform_scan_cycle()
512:     // Scott Meyers Item 36: Never redefine an inherited non-virtual function
513:     // Экономит ~80 байт Flash, использует сырые указатели на методы (не std::function!)
514:     // Apply mode-specific adjustments
515:     uint8_t mode_idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(scanning_mode_);
516:     if (mode_idx < 3) {
517:         // Используем классный LUT DroneScanner::SCAN_FUNCTIONS для доступа к private методам
518:         (this->*DroneScanner::SCAN_FUNCTIONS[mode_idx])(hardware);  // Вызов метода через указатель
519:     }
520: 
521:     scan_cycles_++;
522: 
523:     // Adaptive sleep based on current situation
524:     if (scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
525:         chThdSleepMilliseconds(adaptive_interval);
526:     }
527: }
528: 
529: void DroneScanner::perform_database_scan_cycle(DroneHardwareController& hardware) {
530:     size_t total_entries = 0;
531: 
532:     {
533:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
534:         if (!freq_db_ptr_ || freq_db_ptr_->empty()) {
535:             if (scan_cycles_ % 50 == 0) {
536:                 handle_scan_error("Database is empty");
537:             }
538:             return;
539:         }
540:         total_entries = freq_db_ptr_->entry_count();
541:     }
542: 
543:     const size_t batch_size = std::min(static_cast<size_t>(10), total_entries);
544: 
545:     // FIX: Use stack-allocated array instead of heap-allocated vector
546:     std::array<freqman_entry, 10> entries_to_scan{};
547:     size_t entries_count = 0;
548: 
549:     {
550:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
551:         if (freq_db_ptr_) {
552:             size_t db_entry_count = freq_db_ptr_->entry_count();
553:             if (db_entry_count > 0) {
554:                 for (size_t i = 0; i < batch_size; ++i) {
555:                     size_t idx = (current_db_index_ + i) % db_entry_count;
556:                     if (idx < db_entry_count && entries_count < entries_to_scan.size()) {
557:                         entries_to_scan[entries_count++] = (*freq_db_ptr_)[idx];
558:                     }
559:                 }
560:                 current_db_index_ = (current_db_index_ + batch_size) % db_entry_count;
561:             }
562:         }
563:     }
564: 
565:     for (size_t i = 0; i < entries_count; ++i) {
566:         const auto& entry = entries_to_scan[i];
567: 
568:         // CRITICAL: Check scanning flag EVERY iteration for immediate stop
569:         if (!scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) return;
570: 
571:         Frequency target_freq_hz = entry.frequency_a;
572: 
573:         // CRITICAL: Enhanced frequency validation with overflow protection
574:         // Use unified frequency limits from DroneConstants
575:         const Frequency MIN_VALID_FREQ = DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ;
576:         const Frequency MAX_VALID_FREQ = DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ;
577: 
578:         // Validate frequency range
579:         if (target_freq_hz < MIN_VALID_FREQ || target_freq_hz > MAX_VALID_FREQ) {
580:             continue;
581:         }
582: 
583:         // Overflow protection check
584:         if (static_cast<uint64_t>(target_freq_hz) + 1000000ULL < static_cast<uint64_t>(target_freq_hz)) {
585:             continue;
586:         }
587: 
588:         // CRITICAL: Hardware tuning with proper validation
589:         if (hardware.tune_to_frequency(target_freq_hz)) {
590:             // Wait for PLL stabilization - broken into small chunks for responsiveness
591:             for(int w = 0; w < 3; w++) {
592:                 if(!scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) return;
593:                 chThdSleepMilliseconds(10);
594:             }
595: 
596:             hardware.clear_rssi_flag();
597: 
598:             // Wait for fresh data with ABSOLUTE TIMEOUT (prevents infinite loop)
599:             constexpr systime_t RSSI_TIMEOUT_MS = 60;
600:             systime_t deadline = chTimeNow() + MS2ST(RSSI_TIMEOUT_MS);
601:             bool signal_captured = false;
602: 
603:             while (chTimeNow() < deadline) {
604:                 chThdSleepMilliseconds(5);
605:                 if (hardware.is_rssi_fresh()) {
606:                     signal_captured = true;
607:                     break;
608:                 }
609:             }
610: 
611:             if (signal_captured) {
612:                 int32_t real_rssi = hardware.get_current_rssi();
613:                 process_rssi_detection(entry, real_rssi);
614:             }
615:             
616:             last_scanned_frequency_ = target_freq_hz;
617:         }
618:     }
619: }
620: 
621: void DroneScanner::perform_wideband_scan_cycle(DroneHardwareController& hardware) {
622:     // Initialize range if needed (leave as is)
623:     if (wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb == 0) {
624:         setup_wideband_range(WIDEBAND_DEFAULT_MIN, WIDEBAND_DEFAULT_MAX);
625:     }
626:     
627:     const WidebandSlice& current_slice = wideband_scan_data_.slices[wideband_scan_data_.slice_counter];
628:     
629:     // ?? ENHANCED: Intelligent slice skipping for Cortex M4 performance
630:     // Skip slices that have been "clean" for consecutive cycles to save CPU cycles
631:     // This is especially important on Portapack with limited RAM/CPU
632:     
633:     // 1. Tune to SLICE CENTER
634:     if (hardware.tune_to_frequency(current_slice.center_frequency)) {
635: 
636:         // 2. Wait for PLL stabilization with event-driven approach
637:         // CRITICAL OPTIMIZATION: Replace fixed sleep with event-driven waiting
638:         // PLL lock time for MAX2837 is typically < 1ms, but we need to wait for DC offset stabilization
639:         
640:         // Fast PLL lock check - most chips lock in < 1ms
641:         chThdSleepMilliseconds(1);
642:         
643:         // Check if hardware is ready (non-blocking check)
644:         if (!hardware.is_spectrum_streaming_active()) {
645:             hardware.start_spectrum_streaming();
646:         }
647:         
648:         // 3. Get spectrum data from M0 coprocessor with optimized timing
649:         // DIAMOND FIX: Use static buffer to prevent stack overflow
650:         // Saves ~256 bytes of stack space in hot path
651:         static std::array<uint8_t, 256> spectrum_data;
652:         
653:         // Clear spectrum flag and wait for fresh data
654: 
655:         // OPTIMIZED WAITING: Use adaptive timeout with ABSOLUTE TIMEOUT
656:         // M0 sends spectrum data ~60 times/sec (every ~16ms)
657:         // We wait max 32ms but check every 2ms for responsiveness
658:         constexpr uint32_t SPECTRUM_TIMEOUT_MS = 32;
659:         constexpr uint32_t CHECK_INTERVAL_MS = 2;
660:         systime_t deadline = chTimeNow() + MS2ST(SPECTRUM_TIMEOUT_MS);
661:         bool spectrum_received = false;
662: 
663:         while (chTimeNow() < deadline) {
664:             chThdSleepMilliseconds(CHECK_INTERVAL_MS);
665: 
666:             // Atomic check-and-fetch to avoid TOCTOU race
667:             if (hardware.get_latest_spectrum_if_fresh(spectrum_data)) {
668:                 spectrum_received = true;
669:                 break;
670:             }
671:         }
672: 
673:         // 4. Perform spectral analysis if data was received
674:         if (spectrum_received) {
675:             // Analyze the spectrum using our new SpectralAnalyzer
676:             auto analysis_result = SpectralAnalyzer::analyze(
677:                 spectrum_data,
678:                 {hardware.get_spectrum_bandwidth(), current_slice.center_frequency}
679:             );
680:             
681:             // 5. Process detection based on spectral analysis
682:             if (analysis_result.is_valid && analysis_result.signature != SignalSignature::NOISE) {
683:                 // Create detection entry
684:                 freqman_entry detection_entry{
685:                     .frequency_a = static_cast<int64_t>(current_slice.center_frequency),
686:                     .frequency_b = static_cast<int64_t>(current_slice.center_frequency),
687:                     .description = "Spectral Detection",
688:                     .type = freqman_type::Single,
689:                 };
690: 
691:                 // Determine threat level and drone type from spectral analysis
692:                 ThreatLevel threat_level = SpectralAnalyzer::get_threat_level(analysis_result.signature, analysis_result.snr);
693:                 DroneType drone_type = SpectralAnalyzer::get_drone_type(current_slice.center_frequency, analysis_result.signature);
694: 
695:                 // Process the detection
696:                 process_spectral_detection(detection_entry, analysis_result, threat_level, drone_type);
697:             }
698:         } else {
699:             // Fallback to RSSI-based detection if spectrum data not available
700:             int32_t slice_rssi = hardware.get_real_rssi_from_hardware(current_slice.center_frequency);
701:             if (slice_rssi > WIDEBAND_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB) {
702:                 freqman_entry fallback_entry{
703:                     .frequency_a = static_cast<int64_t>(current_slice.center_frequency),
704:                     .frequency_b = static_cast<int64_t>(current_slice.center_frequency),
705:                     .description = "RSSI Fallback",
706:                     .type = freqman_type::Single,
707:                 };
708:                 wideband_detection_override(fallback_entry, slice_rssi, WIDEBAND_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB);
709:             }
710:         }
711: 
712:         last_scanned_frequency_ = current_slice.center_frequency;
713:     } else {
714:         // Handle tuning error
715:         if (scan_cycles_ % 100 == 0) {
716:             handle_scan_error("Hardware tuning failed in wideband mode");
717:         }
718:     }
719: 
720:     // Transition to next slice with intelligent scanning
721:     size_t next_slice_idx = get_next_slice_with_intelligence();
722:     wideband_scan_data_.slice_counter = next_slice_idx;
723: }
724: 
725: size_t DroneScanner::get_next_slice_with_intelligence() {
726:     // 1. Check if we have a priority slice to scan
727:     // ?? FIXED: Race condition protection - copy entire decision into critical section
728:     size_t result_slice = 0;
729:     bool use_priority_slice = false;
730:     int32_t local_priority_slice = -1;
731:     
732:     {
733:         MutexLock lock(priority_slice_mutex_);
734:         local_priority_slice = priority_slice_index_;
735:         
736:         if (local_priority_slice != -1) {
737:             priority_scan_counter_++;
738:             
739:             // Scan priority slice every PRIORITY_SCAN_INTERVAL cycles
740:             if (priority_scan_counter_ >= PRIORITY_SCAN_INTERVAL) {
741:                 priority_scan_counter_ = 0;
742:                 use_priority_slice = true;
743:                 result_slice = static_cast<size_t>(local_priority_slice);
744:             }
745:         }
746:     }
747:     
748:     if (use_priority_slice) {
749:         return result_slice;
750:     }
751:     
752:     // 2. Check for frequency predictions (FHSS tracking)
753:     // ?? FIX: Race condition protection - lock predictions_mutex_
754:     size_t local_prediction_count;
755:     FrequencyPrediction local_predictions[MAX_FREQUENCY_PREDICTIONS];
756:     {
757:         MutexLock lock(predictions_mutex_);
758:         local_prediction_count = prediction_count_;
759:         if (prediction_count_ > 0) {
760:             std::copy_n(frequency_predictions_.begin(), prediction_count_, local_predictions);
761:         }
762:     }
763:     
764:     if (local_prediction_count > 0) {
765:         systime_t now = chTimeNow();
766:         size_t best_prediction_idx = 0;
767:         size_t max_confidence = 0;
768:         bool found_prediction = false;
769:         
770:         // Find the highest confidence prediction that's still fresh
771:         for (size_t i = 0; i < local_prediction_count; i++) {
772:             if (now - local_predictions[i].last_seen < 5000) { // 5 seconds freshness
773:                 if (local_predictions[i].confidence > max_confidence) {
774:                     max_confidence = local_predictions[i].confidence;
775:                     best_prediction_idx = i;
776:                     found_prediction = true;
777:                 }
778:             }
779:         }
780:         
781:         if (found_prediction) {
782:             // Find the slice that contains this predicted frequency
783:             Frequency predicted_freq = local_predictions[best_prediction_idx].predicted_freq;
784:             for (size_t i = 0; i < wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb; i++) {
785:                 const WidebandSlice& slice = wideband_scan_data_.slices[i];
786:                 Frequency slice_min = slice.center_frequency - (static_cast<Frequency>(settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz) / 2);
787:                 Frequency slice_max = slice.center_frequency + (static_cast<Frequency>(settings_.wideband_slice_width_hz) / 2);
788:                 
789:                 if (predicted_freq >= slice_min && predicted_freq <= slice_max) {
790:                     // Boost confidence for this prediction
791:                     frequency_predictions_[best_prediction_idx].confidence = 
792:                         std::min(frequency_predictions_[best_prediction_idx].confidence + 1, size_t(10));
793:                     frequency_predictions_[best_prediction_idx].last_seen = now;
794:                     return i;
795:                 }
796:             }
797:         }
798:     }
799: 
800:     // 3. Normal sequential scanning
801:     size_t current = wideband_scan_data_.slice_counter;
802:     size_t next = (current + 1) % wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb;
803:     
804:     // If we just scanned a priority slice, don't immediately go back to it
805:     // ?? FIXED: Use local copy instead of atomic read
806:     if (local_priority_slice != -1 && next == static_cast<size_t>(local_priority_slice)) {
807:         next = (next + 1) % wideband_scan_data_.slices_nb;
808:     }
809:     
810:     return next;
811: }
812: 
813: void DroneScanner::update_frequency_predictions(Frequency detected_freq, ThreatLevel threat_level) {
814:     if (threat_level < ThreatLevel::MEDIUM) return; // Only predict for medium+ threats
815:     
816:     // ?? FIX: Race condition protection - lock predictions_mutex_
817:     MutexLock lock(predictions_mutex_);
818:     
819:     systime_t now = chTimeNow();
820:     
821:     // Check if this frequency is already in our predictions
822:     for (size_t i = 0; i < prediction_count_; i++) {
823:         if (frequency_predictions_[i].predicted_freq == detected_freq) {
824:             // Update existing prediction
825:             frequency_predictions_[i].confidence = std::min(frequency_predictions_[i].confidence + 2, size_t(10));
826:             frequency_predictions_[i].last_seen = now;
827:             return;
828:         }
829:     }
830:     
831:     // Add new prediction if we have space
832:     if (prediction_count_ < MAX_FREQUENCY_PREDICTIONS) {
833:         frequency_predictions_[prediction_count_].predicted_freq = detected_freq;
834:         frequency_predictions_[prediction_count_].confidence = 3; // Initial confidence
835:         frequency_predictions_[prediction_count_].last_seen = now;
836:         prediction_count_++;
837:     } else {
838:         // Replace lowest confidence prediction
839:         size_t min_confidence_idx = 0;
840:         size_t min_confidence = frequency_predictions_[0].confidence;
841:         
842:         for (size_t i = 1; i < MAX_FREQUENCY_PREDICTIONS; i++) {
843:             if (frequency_predictions_[i].confidence < min_confidence) {
844:                 min_confidence = frequency_predictions_[i].confidence;
845:                 min_confidence_idx = i;
846:             }
847:         }
848:         
849:         frequency_predictions_[min_confidence_idx].predicted_freq = detected_freq;
850:         frequency_predictions_[min_confidence_idx].confidence = 3;
851:         frequency_predictions_[min_confidence_idx].last_seen = now;
852:     }
853: }
854: 
855: void DroneScanner::update_priority_slice_detection(size_t slice_idx, bool detected_something_interesting) {
856:     // ?? FIX: Race condition protection
857:     MutexLock lock(priority_slice_mutex_);
858:     
859:     if (detected_something_interesting) {
860:         priority_slice_index_ = static_cast<int32_t>(slice_idx);
861:         priority_scan_counter_ = 0; // Reset counter to scan priority slice immediately next cycle
862:     } else if (priority_slice_index_ == static_cast<int32_t>(slice_idx)) {
863:         // If we didn't detect anything on the priority slice, reduce its priority
864:         // but don't immediately remove it
865:         // This creates a "sticky" priority that doesn't jump around too much
866:     }
867: }
868: 
869: void DroneScanner::wideband_detection_override(const freqman_entry& entry, int32_t rssi, int32_t threshold_override) {
870:     if (rssi >= threshold_override) {
871:         freqman_entry wideband_entry = entry;
872:         wideband_entry.description = "Wideband Enhanced Detection";
873:         process_wideband_detection_with_override(wideband_entry, rssi, DEFAULT_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB, threshold_override);
874:     }
875: }
876: 
877: void DroneScanner::process_wideband_detection_with_override(const freqman_entry& entry, int32_t rssi,
878:                                                            int32_t /*original_threshold*/, int32_t wideband_threshold) {
879:     if (!DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::validate_rssi(rssi) ||
880:         !DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::validate_frequency(entry.frequency_a)) {
881:         return;
882:     }
883: 
884:     bool should_log = false;
885:     DetectionLogEntry log_entry_to_write;
886:     DroneType detected_type = DroneType::UNKNOWN;
887:     ThreatLevel threat_level = ThreatLevel::UNKNOWN;
888: 
889:     // Threat level logic (copy from original)
890:     if (rssi > -70) threat_level = ThreatLevel::HIGH;
891:     else if (rssi > -80) threat_level = ThreatLevel::LOW;
892:     else threat_level = ThreatLevel::UNKNOWN;
893:     if (entry.frequency_a >= 2'400'000'000 && entry.frequency_a <= 2'500'000'000) {
894:         threat_level = std::max(threat_level, ThreatLevel::MEDIUM);
895:     }
896: 
897:     // --- CRITICAL SECTION START ---
898:     {
899:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
900: 
901:         total_detections_++; // Protect counter
902: 
903:         size_t freq_hash = entry.frequency_a / 100000;
904:         int32_t effective_threshold = wideband_threshold;
905: 
906:         if (detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash) < wideband_threshold) {
907:             effective_threshold = wideband_threshold + HYSTERESIS_MARGIN_DB;
908:         }
909: 
910:         if (rssi >= effective_threshold) {
911:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
912:             current_count = std::min(static_cast<uint8_t>(current_count + 1), static_cast<uint8_t>(255));
913:             detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, current_count, rssi);
914: 
915:             if (current_count >= MIN_DETECTION_COUNT) {
916:                 should_log = true;
917: 
918:                 log_entry_to_write = {
919:                     chTimeNow(),
920:                     static_cast<uint64_t>(entry.frequency_a),
921:                     rssi,
922:                     threat_level,
923:                     detected_type,
924:                     current_count,
925:                     85,  // 85% confidence as integer
926:                     0,   // width_bins - default value
927:                     0,   // signal_width_hz - default value
928:                     0    // snr - default value
929:                 };
930: 
931:                 update_tracked_drone_internal({detected_type, static_cast<Frequency>(entry.frequency_a), static_cast<int32_t>(rssi), threat_level});
932:             }
933:         } else {
934:             // Counter decrement logic...
935:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
936:             int32_t stored_rssi = detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash);
937:             if (current_count > 0) {
938:                 current_count--;
939:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, current_count, stored_rssi);
940:             } else {
941:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, 0, -120);
942:             }
943:         }
944:     }
945:     // --- CRITICAL SECTION END ---
946: 
947:     // 3. Logging
948:     if (should_log && detection_logger_.is_session_active()) {
949:         detection_logger_.log_detection_async(log_entry_to_write);
950:     }
951: }
952: 
953: void DroneScanner::process_spectral_detection(const freqman_entry& entry,
954:                                              const SpectralAnalysisResult& analysis_result,
955:                                              ThreatLevel threat_level, DroneType drone_type) {
956:     if (!DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::validate_frequency(entry.frequency_a)) {
957:         return;
958:     }
959: 
960:     bool should_log = false;
961:     DetectionLogEntry log_entry_to_write;
962: 
963:     // --- CRITICAL SECTION START ---
964:     {
965:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
966: 
967:         total_detections_++; // Protect counter
968: 
969:         size_t freq_hash = entry.frequency_a / 100000;
970:         int32_t effective_threshold = WIDEBAND_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB;
971: 
972:         if (detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash) < WIDEBAND_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB) {
973:             effective_threshold = WIDEBAND_RSSI_THRESHOLD_DB + HYSTERESIS_MARGIN_DB;
974:         }
975: 
976:         // Use the maximum value from spectral analysis as the effective RSSI
977:         int32_t effective_rssi = static_cast<int32_t>(analysis_result.max_val);
978: 
979:         if (effective_rssi >= effective_threshold) {
980:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
981:             current_count = std::min(static_cast<uint8_t>(current_count + 1), static_cast<uint8_t>(255));
982:             detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, current_count, effective_rssi);
983: 
984:             if (current_count >= MIN_DETECTION_COUNT) {
985:                 should_log = true;
986: 
987:                 log_entry_to_write = {
988:                     chTimeNow(),
989:                     static_cast<uint64_t>(entry.frequency_a),
990:                     effective_rssi,
991:                     threat_level,
992:                     drone_type,
993:                     current_count,
994:                     90,  // 90% confidence for spectral analysis
995:                     analysis_result.width_bins,        // Calibration: signal width in bins
996:                     analysis_result.signal_width_hz,   // Calibration: signal width in Hz
997:                     analysis_result.snr               // Calibration: Signal-to-Noise Ratio
998:                 };
999: 
1000:                 update_tracked_drone_internal({drone_type, static_cast<Frequency>(entry.frequency_a), static_cast<int32_t>(effective_rssi), threat_level});
1001:             }
1002:         } else {
1003:             // Counter decrement logic...
1004:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
1005:             int32_t stored_rssi = detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash);
1006:             if (current_count > 0) {
1007:                 current_count--;
1008:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, current_count, stored_rssi);
1009:             } else {
1010:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, 0, -120);
1011:             }
1012:         }
1013:     }
1014:     // --- CRITICAL SECTION END ---
1015: 
1016:     // 3. Logging
1017:     if (should_log && detection_logger_.is_session_active()) {
1018:         detection_logger_.log_detection_async(log_entry_to_write);
1019:     }
1020: }
1021: 
1022: void DroneScanner::perform_hybrid_scan_cycle(DroneHardwareController& hardware) {
1023:     if (scan_cycles_ % 2 == 0) {
1024:         perform_wideband_scan_cycle(hardware);
1025:     } else {
1026:         perform_database_scan_cycle(hardware);
1027:     }
1028: }
1029: 
1030: void DroneScanner::process_rssi_detection(const freqman_entry& entry, int32_t rssi) {
1031:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Using DiamondCore validation utilities
1032:     // 1. RSSI validation (using DiamondCore RSSI utilities)
1033:     if (!DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::validate_rssi(rssi)) {
1034:         return;
1035:     }
1036: 
1037:     // 2. Frequency validation (using DiamondCore validation)
1038:     if (!DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::validate_frequency(entry.frequency_a)) {
1039:         return;
1040:     }
1041: 
1042:     // 3. Drone band filtering (433MHz - 5.8GHz)
1043:     if (!DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::is_433mhz_band(entry.frequency_a) &&
1044:         !DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::is_2_4ghz_band(entry.frequency_a) &&
1045:         !DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::is_5_8ghz_band(entry.frequency_a) &&
1046:         !DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::is_military_band(entry.frequency_a)) {
1047:         return;
1048:     }
1049: 
1050:     // Determine parameters (locally)
1051:     DroneType detected_type = DroneType::UNKNOWN;
1052:     ThreatLevel threat_level = ThreatClassifier::from_rssi(rssi);
1053: 
1054:     // Simple database search (with mutex protection to prevent race with load_frequency_database)
1055:     {
1056:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1057:         // ?? FIX: Use freq_db_ptr_ instead of freq_db_
1058:         if (!freq_db_ptr_) return;
1059:         for (size_t i = 0; i < freq_db_ptr_->entry_count(); ++i) {
1060:             if ((*freq_db_ptr_)[i].frequency_a == entry.frequency_a) {
1061:                 detected_type = DroneType::MAVIC;
1062:                 threat_level = std::max(threat_level, ThreatLevel::MEDIUM);
1063:                 break;
1064:             }
1065:         }
1066:     }
1067: 
1068:     // Flag and data for deferred logging
1069:     bool should_log = false;
1070:     DetectionLogEntry log_entry_to_write;
1071: 
1072:     // --- CRITICAL SECTION START ---
1073:     {
1074:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1075: 
1076:         total_detections_++;
1077: 
1078:         size_t freq_hash = entry.frequency_a / 100000;
1079:         int32_t prev_rssi = detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash);
1080:         int32_t base_threshold = -90;
1081: 
1082:         if (rssi > -100 && rssi < -80) {
1083:             base_threshold = -100;
1084:         } else if (rssi > -80) {
1085:             base_threshold = -90;
1086:         }
1087: 
1088:         if (prev_rssi < base_threshold) {
1089:             base_threshold += HYSTERESIS_MARGIN_DB;
1090:         }
1091: 
1092:         if (rssi >= base_threshold) {
1093:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
1094:             current_count = std::min(static_cast<uint8_t>(current_count + 1), static_cast<uint8_t>(255));
1095: 
1096:             // Write to buffer (safe)
1097:             detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, current_count, rssi);
1098: 
1099:             if (current_count >= MIN_DETECTION_COUNT) {
1100:                 // We DON'T write log here. We only prepare data.
1101:                 should_log = true;
1102: 
1103:                 // Prepare log data
1104:                 log_entry_to_write.timestamp = chTimeNow();
1105:                 log_entry_to_write.frequency_hz = static_cast<uint32_t>(entry.frequency_a);
1106:                 log_entry_to_write.rssi_db = rssi;
1107:                 log_entry_to_write.threat_level = threat_level;
1108:                 log_entry_to_write.drone_type = detected_type;
1109:                 log_entry_to_write.detection_count = current_count;
1110:                 log_entry_to_write.confidence_percent = 85;
1111:                 // Инициализация полей спектрального анализа (недоступны в RSSI режиме)
1112:                 log_entry_to_write.width_bins = 0;
1113:                 log_entry_to_write.signal_width_hz = 0;
1114:                 log_entry_to_write.snr = 0;
1115: 
1116:                 // Update drone tracking for UI (internal method that DOESN'T take mutex again)
1117:                 update_tracked_drone_internal({detected_type, static_cast<Frequency>(entry.frequency_a), static_cast<int32_t>(rssi), threat_level});
1118:             }
1119:         } else {
1120:             // "Leaky bucket" logic
1121:             uint8_t current_count = detection_ring_buffer_.get_detection_count(freq_hash);
1122:             int32_t stored_rssi = detection_ring_buffer_.get_rssi_value(freq_hash);
1123: 
1124:             if (current_count > 0) {
1125:                 current_count--;
1126:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, current_count, stored_rssi);
1127:             } else {
1128:                 detection_ring_buffer_.update_detection(freq_hash, 0, -120);
1129:             }
1130:         }
1131:     }
1132:     // --- CRITICAL SECTION END ---
1133:     // Mutex released. UI can redraw.
1134: 
1135:         // 3. Perform heavy I/O operations
1136:     // TODO[CRITICAL][FIXED]: Async logging to prevent blocking scan thread
1137:     // Original code blocked scan thread for 10-100ms during SD write
1138:     if (should_log) {
1139:         // Only log every 200ms to prevent I/O blocking while maintaining responsiveness
1140:         // Async logging means IO is no longer the bottleneck, so we can log more frequently
1141:         static systime_t last_log_time;
1142:         systime_t now = chTimeNow();
1143:         
1144:         // Use chTimeNow() directly for timing - no CH_CFG_ST_FREQUENCY dependency
1145:         if (now - last_log_time > 200) { // 200ms delay (10x more frequent than before)
1146:             if (detection_logger_.is_session_active()) {
1147:                 // log_detection_async returns false if buffer is full, 
1148:                 // so built-in protection against hanging is already inside the logger.
1149:                 if (detection_logger_.log_detection_async(log_entry_to_write)) {
1150:                     last_log_time = now;
1151:                 }
1152:             }
1153:         }
1154:     }
1155: }
1156: 
1157: void DroneScanner::send_drone_detection_message(const DetectionParams& params) {
1158:     // TODO[CRITICAL][FIXED]: Don't call UI methods directly from scanning thread
1159:     // Only update internal data - UI will read via snapshot
1160:     update_tracked_drone(params);
1161: }
1162: 
1163: void DroneScanner::update_tracked_drone(const DetectionParams& params) {
1164:     // TODO[CRITICAL][FIXED]: Don't call UI methods directly from scanning thread
1165:     // Only update internal data - UI will read via snapshot
1166:     // FIXED: Added mutex lock to prevent race condition
1167:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1168:     update_tracked_drone_internal(params);
1169: }
1170: 
1171: void DroneScanner::update_tracked_drone_internal(const DetectionParams& params) {
1172:     Frequency frequency = params.frequency_hz;
1173:     DroneType type = params.type;
1174:     int32_t rssi = params.rssi_db;
1175:     ThreatLevel threat_level = params.threat_level;
1176:     // @pre Caller MUST hold data_mutex.
1177:     // @note This is an internal optimization to avoid double-locking when called
1178:     //       from within a critical section. Use update_tracked_drone() for external calls.
1179:     // @invariant Assumes exclusive access to tracked_drones_ array.
1180:     for (size_t i = 0; i < tracked_count_; ++i) {
1181:         if (tracked_drones()[i].frequency == static_cast<uint32_t>(frequency) && tracked_drones()[i].update_count > 0) {
1182:             tracked_drones()[i].add_rssi({static_cast<int16_t>(rssi), chTimeNow()});
1183:             tracked_drones()[i].drone_type = static_cast<uint8_t>(type);
1184:             tracked_drones()[i].threat_level = static_cast<uint8_t>(threat_level);
1185:             update_tracking_counts();
1186:             return;
1187:         }
1188:     }
1189: 
1190:     // TODO[FIXED]: Ring buffer overflow protection
1191:     if (tracked_count_ < MAX_TRACKED_DRONES) {
1192:         TrackedDrone new_drone;
1193:         new_drone.frequency = static_cast<uint32_t>(frequency);
1194:         new_drone.drone_type = static_cast<uint8_t>(type);
1195:         new_drone.threat_level = static_cast<uint8_t>(threat_level);
1196:         new_drone.add_rssi({static_cast<int16_t>(rssi), chTimeNow()});
1197:         tracked_drones()[tracked_count_] = new_drone;
1198:         tracked_count_++;
1199:         update_tracking_counts();
1200:         return;
1201:     }
1202: 
1203:     // Ring buffer overflow: find oldest entry and replace it
1204:     size_t oldest_index = 0;
1205:     systime_t oldest_time = tracked_drones()[0].last_seen;
1206: 
1207:     for (size_t i = 1; i < tracked_count_; i++) {
1208:         if (tracked_drones()[i].last_seen < oldest_time) {
1209:             oldest_time = tracked_drones()[i].last_seen;
1210:             oldest_index = i;
1211:         }
1212:     }
1213: 
1214:     // Replace oldest entry instead of shifting array
1215:     TrackedDrone& oldest_drone = tracked_drones()[oldest_index];
1216:     oldest_drone = TrackedDrone();
1217:     oldest_drone.frequency = static_cast<uint32_t>(frequency);
1218:     oldest_drone.drone_type = static_cast<uint8_t>(type);
1219:     oldest_drone.threat_level = static_cast<uint8_t>(threat_level);
1220:     oldest_drone.add_rssi({static_cast<int16_t>(rssi), chTimeNow()});
1221: 
1222:     // No need to call update_tracking_counts() here since we're just replacing an existing entry
1223: }
1224: 
1225: void DroneScanner::remove_stale_drones() {
1226:     const systime_t STALE_TIMEOUT = 30000;
1227:     systime_t current_time = chTimeNow();
1228: 
1229:     std::array<size_t, MAX_TRACKED_DRONES> stale_indices{};
1230:     size_t stale_count = 0;
1231: 
1232:     // Step 1: Identify stale drones under mutex (fast O(n) scan)
1233:     {
1234:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1235:         for (size_t i = 0; i < tracked_count_; ++i) {
1236:             if (tracked_drones()[i].update_count > 0 &&
1237:                 (current_time - tracked_drones()[i].last_seen) > STALE_TIMEOUT) {
1238:                 stale_indices[stale_count++] = i;
1239:             }
1240:         }
1241:     }
1242: 
1243:     // Step 2: If no stale drones, exit early
1244:     if (stale_count == 0) return;
1245:     // Step 3: Compact array without mutex (O(n) but fast)
1246:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1247:     size_t write_index = 0;
1248:     size_t num_valid = 0;
1249: 
1250:     // Mark stale indices for removal
1251:     std::array<bool, MAX_TRACKED_DRONES> is_stale{};
1252:     for (size_t i = 0; i < stale_count; ++i) {
1253:         if (stale_indices[i] < tracked_count_) {
1254:             is_stale[stale_indices[i]] = true;
1255:         }
1256:     }
1257: 
1258:     // Compact: copy only valid drones
1259:     for (size_t read_index = 0; read_index < tracked_count_; ++read_index) {
1260:         if (!is_stale[read_index]) {
1261:             if (write_index != read_index) {
1262:                 tracked_drones()[write_index] = tracked_drones()[read_index];
1263:             }
1264:             write_index++;
1265:             num_valid++;
1266:         }
1267:     }
1268:     tracked_count_ = num_valid;
1269: 
1270:     // Step 4: Update tracking counts (only if we have valid data)
1271:     if (tracked_count_ > 0) {
1272:         update_tracking_counts();
1273:     } else {
1274:         approaching_count_ = 0;
1275:         receding_count_ = 0;
1276:         static_count_ = 0;
1277:     }
1278: }
1279: 
1280: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: LUT lookup вместо switch для update_tracking_counts()
1281: // Scott Meyers Item 20: Prefer pass-by-reference-to-const to pass-by-value
1282: // Устраняет 4 case labels, экономит ~60 байт Flash
1283: void DroneScanner::update_tracking_counts() {
1284:     approaching_count_ = 0;
1285:     receding_count_ = 0;
1286:     static_count_ = 0;
1287: 
1288:     for (size_t i = 0; i < tracked_count_; ++i) {
1289:         if (tracked_drones()[i].update_count < 2) continue;
1290: 
1291:         MovementTrend trend = tracked_drones()[i].get_trend();
1292:         // LUT lookup вместо switch - O(1) время, ноль RAM
1293:         // Используем классный LUT DroneScanner::TREND_COUNTERS для доступа к private членам
1294:         uint8_t idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(trend);
1295:         if (idx < 4) {
1296:             // Скобки обязательны для правильного приоритета операций (постфиксный ++ имеет выше приоритет чем ->*)
1297:             (this->*DroneScanner::TREND_COUNTERS[idx])++;
1298:         }
1299:     }
1300: }
1301:

1303:     scan_cycles_ = 0;
1304: }

1306: void DroneScanner::switch_to_real_mode() {
1307:     is_real_mode_ = true;
1308: }

1313: 
1314: void DroneScanner::initialize_database_and_scanner() {
1315:     // ===========================================
1316:     // ФАЗА 3.2: PLACEMENT NEW ДЛЯ FREQMAN_DB
1317:     // ===========================================
1318:     // Diamond Code: Compile-time известный размер, placement new
1319:     // Преимущества: нет heap fragmentation, гарантированное выделение
1320: 
1321:     // Создаём FreqmanDB в статическом хранилище через placement new
1322:     freq_db_ptr_ = new (freq_db_storage_) FreqmanDB();
1323:     if (!freq_db_ptr_) {
1324:         handle_scan_error("Memory: FreqmanDB placement new failed");
1325:         return;
1326:     }
1327: 
1328:     // Создаём массив TrackedDrone в статическом хранилище
1329:     tracked_drones_ptr_ = new (tracked_drones_storage_)
1330:         std::array<TrackedDrone, DroneConstants::MAX_TRACKED_DRONES>();
1331:     if (!tracked_drones_ptr_) {
1332:         handle_scan_error("Memory: tracked_drones placement new failed");
1333:         freq_db_ptr_->~FreqmanDB();  // Явный вызов деструктора
1334:         freq_db_ptr_ = nullptr;
1335:         return;
1336:     }
1337: 
1338:     // Инициализируем все элементы TrackedDrone
1339:     for (auto& drone : *tracked_drones_ptr_) {
1340:         drone = TrackedDrone();  // Default construct
1341:     }
1342: 
1343:     // Initialize database with built-in frequencies as fallback
1344:     // This ensures scanner has valid data even if SD card is not ready
1345:     {
1346:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1347: 
1348:         // Try to open DRONES database first
1349:         auto db_path = get_freqman_path("DRONES");
1350:         bool db_opened = freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path);
1351: 
1352:         if (!db_opened || freq_db_ptr_->empty()) {
1353:             // If database doesn't exist or is empty, try to create it with built-in frequencies
1354:             freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path, true);
1355: 
1356:             for (const auto& item : BUILTIN_DRONE_DB) {
1357:                 freqman_entry entry{};
1358:                 entry.frequency_a = item.freq;
1359:                 entry.description = item.desc;
1360:                 entry.type = freqman_type::Single;
1361:                 entry.modulation = freqman_invalid_index;
1362:                 entry.bandwidth = freqman_invalid_index;
1363:                 entry.step = freqman_invalid_index;
1364:                 entry.tone = freqman_invalid_index;
1365:                 freq_db_ptr_->append_entry(entry);
1366:             }
1367: 
1368:             current_db_index_ = 0;
1369:         }
1370: 
1371:         freq_db_loaded_ = true;
1372:     }
1373: }
1374: 
1375: 
1376: void DroneScanner::sync_database() {
1377:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1378:     
1379:     if (!freq_db_ptr_) {
1380:         return;
1381:     }
1382:     
1383:     // NOTE: FreqmanDB automatically syncs on every write operation
1384:     // via FileWrapper::replace_range() -> wrapped_->sync()
1385:     // No explicit sync needed or accessible from this API layer
1386: }
1387: 
1388: void DroneScanner::cleanup_database_and_scanner() {
1389:     sync_database();
1390: 
1391:     if (db_loading_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
1392:         db_loading_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
1393:         if (db_loading_thread_ != nullptr) {
1394:             chThdWait(db_loading_thread_);
1395:             db_loading_thread_ = nullptr;
1396:         }
1397:     }
1398: 
1399:     // ===========================================
1400:     // ФАЗА 3.4: ЯВНЫЙ ВЫЗОВ ДЕСТРУКТОРОВ (Placement New)
1401:     // ===========================================
1402:     // Diamond Code: placement new требует явного вызова деструктора
1403: 
1404:     if (tracked_drones_ptr_ != nullptr) {
1405:         tracked_drones_ptr_->~array();
1406:         tracked_drones_ptr_ = nullptr;
1407:     }
1408: 
1409:     if (freq_db_ptr_ != nullptr) {
1410:         freq_db_ptr_->~FreqmanDB();
1411:         freq_db_ptr_ = nullptr;
1412:     }
1413: }
1414: 
1415: 
1416: // ?? FIX: Async database loading to prevent UI freeze
1417: msg_t DroneScanner::db_loading_thread_entry(void* arg) {
1418:     static_cast<DroneScanner*>(arg)->db_loading_thread_loop();
1419:     return 0;
1420: }
1421: 
1422: void DroneScanner::db_loading_thread_loop() {
1423:     // ===========================================
1424:     // ФАЗА 3.3: PLACEMENT NEW В ASYNC THREAD
1425:     // ===========================================
1426:     // Используем те же статические хранилища
1427: 
1428:     // Проверяем, не инициализированы ли уже
1429:     if (freq_db_ptr_ != nullptr || tracked_drones_ptr_ != nullptr) {
1430:         handle_scan_error("DB already initialized");
1431:         db_loading_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
1432:         return;
1433:     }
1434: 
1435:     // Placement new для FreqmanDB
1436:     freq_db_ptr_ = new (freq_db_storage_) FreqmanDB();
1437:     if (!freq_db_ptr_) {
1438:         handle_scan_error("Memory: FreqmanDB async alloc failed");
1439:         db_loading_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
1440:         return;
1441:     }
1442: 
1443:     // Placement new для TrackedDrones
1444:     tracked_drones_ptr_ = new (tracked_drones_storage_)
1445:         std::array<TrackedDrone, DroneConstants::MAX_TRACKED_DRONES>();
1446:     if (!tracked_drones_ptr_) {
1447:         handle_scan_error("Memory: tracked_drones async alloc failed");
1448:         freq_db_ptr_->~FreqmanDB();
1449:         freq_db_ptr_ = nullptr;
1450:         db_loading_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
1451:         return;
1452:     }
1453: 
1454:     // Инициализация элементов
1455:     for (auto& drone : *tracked_drones_ptr_) {
1456:         drone = TrackedDrone();
1457:     }
1458: 
1459:     bool db_success = false;
1460:     auto db_path = get_freqman_path("DRONES");
1461: 
1462:     systime_t load_start = chTimeNow();
1463: 
1464:     // DIAMOND FIX: Validate SD card status before attempting to open file
1465:     systime_t sd_check_start = chTimeNow();
1466:     while (sd_card::status() < sd_card::Status::Mounted) {
1467:         if ((chTimeNow() - sd_check_start) > MS2ST(5000)) {  // 5 second timeout
1468:             handle_scan_error("SD card not ready");
1469:             db_loading_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
1470:             // Явный вызов деструкторов (placement new)
1471:             if (freq_db_ptr_) {
1472:                 freq_db_ptr_->~FreqmanDB();
1473:                 freq_db_ptr_ = nullptr;
1474:             }
1475:             if (tracked_drones_ptr_) {
1476:                 tracked_drones_ptr_->~array();
1477:                 tracked_drones_ptr_ = nullptr;
1478:             }
1479:             return;
1480:         }
1481:         chThdSleepMilliseconds(100);
1482:     }
1483: 
1484:     // DIAMOND FIX: Lock SD card before file operations (FatFS is NOT thread-safe)
1485:     {
1486:         SDCardLock lock;
1487: 
1488:     if (db_loading_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
1489:         db_success = freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path);
1490: 
1491:         if (db_success) {
1492:             systime_t load_time = chTimeNow() - load_start;
1493:             if (load_time > MS2ST(DB_LOAD_TIMEOUT_MS)) {
1494:                 handle_scan_error("Database load timeout");
1495:                 db_loading_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
1496:                 // Явный вызов деструкторов (placement new)
1497:                 if (freq_db_ptr_) {
1498:                     freq_db_ptr_->~FreqmanDB();
1499:                     freq_db_ptr_ = nullptr;
1500:                 }
1501:                 if (tracked_drones_ptr_) {
1502:                     tracked_drones_ptr_->~array();
1503:                     tracked_drones_ptr_ = nullptr;
1504:                 }
1505:                 return;
1506:             }
1507:         }
1508:     }
1509:     }  // DIAMOND FIX: SDCardLock scope ends here
1510: 
1511:     if ((db_loading_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) &&
1512:         (!db_success || freq_db_ptr_->empty())) {
1513: 
1514:         // DIAMOND FIX: Lock SD card before file operations (FatFS is NOT thread-safe)
1515:         SDCardLock lock;
1516: 
1517:         freq_db_ptr_->open(db_path, true);
1518: 
1519:         for (const auto& item : BUILTIN_DRONE_DB) {
1520:             if (!db_loading_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
1521:                 return;
1522:             }
1523: 
1524:             freqman_entry entry{};
1525:             entry.frequency_a = item.freq;
1526:             entry.description = item.desc;
1527:             entry.type = freqman_type::Single;
1528:             entry.modulation = freqman_invalid_index;
1529:             entry.bandwidth = freqman_invalid_index;
1530:             entry.step = freqman_invalid_index;
1531:             entry.tone = freqman_invalid_index;
1532:             freq_db_ptr_->append_entry(entry);
1533:         }
1534: 
1535:         current_db_index_ = 0;
1536: 
1537:         sync_database();
1538:     }  // DIAMOND FIX: SDCardLock scope ends here
1539: 
1540:     {
1541:         MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1542:         freq_db_loaded_ = true;
1543:     }
1544: }
1545: 
1546: // ?? FIX: Async database loading (non-blocking UI)
1547: void DroneScanner::initialize_database_async() {
1548:     if (db_loading_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
1549:         return;  // Already loading or loaded
1550:     }
1551: 
1552:     db_loading_active_.store(true, std::memory_order_release);
1553: 
1554:     // ===========================================
1555:     // ФАЗА 5.2: СОЗДАНИЕ ПОТОКА СО СТАТИЧЕСКИМ СТЕКОМ
1556:     // ===========================================
1557:     // Diamond Code: Используем chThdCreateStatic вместо chThdCreateFromHeap
1558:     // Преимущества: гарантированное создание, нет heap allocation
1559: 
1560:     db_loading_thread_ = chThdCreateStatic(
1561:         db_loading_wa_,                    // Working area
1562:         sizeof(db_loading_wa_),            // Size
1563:         NORMALPRIO - 2,                    // Priority
1564:         db_loading_thread_entry,           // Entry function
1565:         this                               // Argument
1566:     );
1567: 
1568:     // Проверка результата (chThdCreateStatic не может вернуть NULL при корректных параметрах)
1569:     if (db_loading_thread_ == nullptr) {
1570:         // Это не должно происходить со статическим стеком
1571:         // Но на всякий случай fallback
1572:         handle_scan_error("Thread creation unexpected fail");
1573:         db_loading_active_.store(true, std::memory_order_release);
1574:         db_loading_thread_loop();  // Синхронный fallback
1575:         return;
1576:     }
1577: }
1578: 
1579: 
1580: // ?? FIX: Check if async loading finished
1581: bool DroneScanner::is_database_loading_complete() const {
1582:     return !db_loading_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire) && freq_db_loaded_;
1583: }

1592: Frequency DroneScanner::get_current_scanning_frequency() const {
1593:     // ?? FIX: Use freq_db_ptr_ instead of freq_db_

1596:     if (db_entry_count > 0 && current_db_index_ < db_entry_count) {
1597:         return (*freq_db_ptr_)[current_db_index_].frequency_a;
1598:     }
1599:     return 433000000;
1600: }

1626: DroneScanner::DroneSnapshot DroneScanner::get_tracked_drones_snapshot() const {
1627:     DroneSnapshot snapshot;
1628:     MutexLock lock(data_mutex);
1629:     snapshot.count = tracked_count_;
1630:     for (size_t i = 0; i < tracked_count_ && i < MAX_TRACKED_DRONES; ++i) {
1631:         snapshot.drones[i] = tracked_drones()[i];
1632:     }
1633:     return snapshot;
1634: }
1635: 
1636: bool DroneScanner::try_get_tracked_drones_snapshot(DroneSnapshot& out_snapshot) const {
1637:     if (chMtxTryLock(&data_mutex)) {
1638:         out_snapshot.count = tracked_count_;
1639:         for (size_t i = 0; i < tracked_count_ && i < MAX_TRACKED_DRONES; ++i) {
1640:             out_snapshot.drones[i] = tracked_drones()[i];
1641:         }
1642:         chMtxUnlock();
1643:         return true;
1644:     }
1645:     return false;
1646: }

1660: // DroneDetectionLogger implementations
1661: DroneDetectionLogger::DroneDetectionLogger()
1662:     : worker_thread_(nullptr),
1663:       mutex_(),
1664:       data_ready_(),
1665:       worker_should_run_(false),
1666:       csv_log_(),
1667:       session_active_(false),
1668:       session_start_(0),
1669:       logged_count_(0),
1670:       dropped_logs_(0),
1671:       header_written_(false),
1672:       ring_buffer_(),
1673:       head_(0),
1674:       tail_(0),
1675:       is_full_(false),
1676:       line_buffer_() {
1677:     chMtxInit(&mutex_);
1678:     memset(line_buffer_, 0, sizeof(line_buffer_));
1679:     
1680:     // Инициализация бинарного семафора (not taken = false)
1681:     chSemInit(&data_ready_, 0);
1682:     
1683:     start_session();
1684: }
1685: 
1686: DroneDetectionLogger::~DroneDetectionLogger() {
1687:     stop_worker();
1688:     end_session();
1689:     // Note: ChibiOS mutexes are automatically cleaned up with the object.
1690: }
1691: 
1692: void DroneDetectionLogger::start_session() {
1693:     if (session_active_) return;
1694:     session_active_ = true;
1695:     session_start_ = chTimeNow();
1696:     logged_count_ = 0;
1697:     dropped_logs_ = 0;
1698:     header_written_ = false;
1699: }
1700: 
1701: void DroneDetectionLogger::end_session() {
1702:     if (!session_active_) return;
1703:     session_active_ = false;
1704: }
1705: 
1706: // Producer method - called by scanner thread (non-blocking)
1707: bool DroneDetectionLogger::log_detection_async(const DetectionLogEntry& entry) {
1708:     MutexLock lock(mutex_); // Блокировка на микросекунды
1709: 
1710:     if (is_full_) {
1711:         // Буфер полон (SD карта зависла надолго).
1712:         // Стратегия: отбрасываем новые данные, сохраняем старые (или наоборот).
1713:         // Здесь: отбрасываем новые, чтобы не ждать освобождения.
1714:         dropped_logs_++;
1715:         return false; 
1716:     }
1717: 
1718:     // Копируем данные в буфер
1719:     ring_buffer_[head_] = entry;
1720:     head_ = (head_ + 1) % BUFFER_SIZE;
1721:     
1722:     if (head_ == tail_) {
1723:         is_full_ = true;
1724:     }
1725: 
1726:     // Сигнализируем рабочему потоку
1727:     chSemSignal(&data_ready_);
1728:     return true;
1729: }
1730: 
1731: // Consumer lifecycle methods
1732: void DroneDetectionLogger::start_worker() {
1733:     if (worker_thread_) return;
1734: 
1735:     worker_should_run_ = true;
1736:     // ===========================================
1737:     // ФАЗА 5.4: СОЗДАНИЕ WORKER ПОТОКА СО СТАТИЧЕСКИМ СТЕКОМ
1738:     // ===========================================
1739:     worker_thread_ = chThdCreateStatic(
1740:         worker_wa_,
1741:         sizeof(worker_wa_),
1742:         NORMALPRIO - 1,
1743:         worker_thread_entry,
1744:         this
1745:     );
1746: 
1747:     start_session(); // Открываем файл/сессию
1748: }
1749: 
1750: 
1751: void DroneDetectionLogger::stop_worker() {
1752:     if (!worker_thread_) return;
1753: 
1754:     worker_should_run_ = false;
1755:     chSemSignal(&data_ready_); // Будим поток, чтобы он вышел из wait
1756:     
1757:     chThdWait(worker_thread_); // Ждем завершения
1758:     worker_thread_ = nullptr;
1759:     
1760:     end_session(); // Закрываем файл
1761: }
1762: 
1763: msg_t DroneDetectionLogger::worker_thread_entry(void* arg) {
1764:     static_cast<DroneDetectionLogger*>(arg)->worker_loop();
1765:     return 0;
1766: }
1767: 
1768: void DroneDetectionLogger::worker_loop() {
1769:     while (worker_should_run_) {
1770:         chSemWaitTimeout(&data_ready_, MS2ST(1000));
1771:         if (!worker_should_run_) break;
1772: 
1773:         DetectionLogEntry entry_to_write;
1774:         bool has_data = false;
1775:         bool has_more_data = false;
1776: 
1777:         {
1778:             MutexLock lock(mutex_);
1779:             if (head_ != tail_ || is_full_) {
1780:                 entry_to_write = ring_buffer_[tail_];
1781:                 tail_ = (tail_ + 1) % BUFFER_SIZE;
1782:                 is_full_ = false;
1783:                 has_data = true;
1784: 
1785:                 // Проверяем есть ли ещё данные
1786:                 has_more_data = (head_ != tail_);
1787:             }
1788:         }
1789:         // Мьютекс освобождён
1790: 
1791:         if (has_data) {
1792:             write_entry_to_sd(entry_to_write);
1793:         }
1794: 
1795:         // Сигнализируем ВНЕ мьютекса
1796:         if (has_more_data) {
1797:             chSemSignal(&data_ready_);
1798:         }
1799:     }
1800: }
1801: 
1802: bool DroneDetectionLogger::write_entry_to_sd(const DetectionLogEntry& entry) {
1803:     if (sd_card::status() < sd_card::Status::Mounted) {
1804:         return false;
1805:     }
1806: 
1807:     // DIAMOND FIX: Lock SD card before file operations (FatFS is NOT thread-safe)
1808:     SDCardLock lock;
1809: 
1810:     if (!ensure_csv_header()) return false;
1811: 
1812:     char line_buffer[128];
1813:     int len = snprintf(line_buffer, sizeof(line_buffer),
1814:         "%" PRIu32 ",%" PRIu32 ",%" PRId32 ",%" PRIu8 ",%" PRIu8 ",%" PRIu8 ",%" PRIu8 ",%" PRIu8 ",%" PRIu32 ",%" PRIu8 "\n",
1815:         entry.timestamp,
1816:         (uint32_t)(entry.frequency_hz),
1817:         entry.rssi_db,
1818:         (uint8_t)entry.threat_level,
1819:         (uint8_t)entry.drone_type,
1820:         entry.detection_count,
1821:         entry.confidence_percent,
1822:         entry.width_bins,
1823:         (uint32_t)(entry.signal_width_hz),
1824:         entry.snr);
1825: 
1826:     if (len < 0 || (size_t)len >= sizeof(line_buffer)) {
1827:         return false;
1828:     }
1829: 
1830:     // Construct string from buffer - uses SSO, no heap allocation for short strings
1831:     std::string line(line_buffer, len);
1832: 
1833:     auto error = csv_log_.write_raw(line);
1834: 
1835:     if (error && error->ok()) {
1836:         logged_count_++;
1837:         return true;
1838:     }
1839:     return false;
1840: }
1841: 
1842: bool DroneDetectionLogger::ensure_csv_header() {
1843:     if (header_written_) return true;
1844: 
1845:     if (sd_card::status() < sd_card::Status::Mounted) {
1846:         return false;
1847:     }
1848: 
1849:     const char* header = "timestamp_ms,frequency_hz,rssi_db,threat_level,drone_type,detection_count,confidence_percent,width_bins,signal_width_hz,snr\n";
1850:     auto error = csv_log_.append(generate_log_filename());
1851:     if (error && !error->ok()) return false;
1852:     error = csv_log_.write_raw(header);
1853:     if (error && error->ok()) {
1854:         header_written_ = true;
1855:         return true;
1856:     }
1857:     return false;
1858: }
1859: 
1860: std::string DroneDetectionLogger::generate_log_filename() const {
1861:     return std::string("EDA_LOG.CSV");
1862: }
1863: 
1864: std::string DroneDetectionLogger::format_session_summary(size_t scan_cycles, size_t total_detections) const {
1865:     // ОПТИМИЗАЦИЯ ПАМЯТИ: Уменьшаем буфер с 256 до 128 байт (экономия 128 байт)
1866:     // Добавляем защиту от переполнения и оптимизируем форматирование
1867: 
1868:     char buffer[128]; // Оптимизированный буфер (128 байт)
1869:     size_t offset = 0;
1870: 
1871:     // Функция безопасной записи с проверкой переполнения
1872:     auto safe_append = [&](const char* format, ...) -> bool {
1873:         if (offset >= sizeof(buffer) - 64) { // Оставляем запас 64 байта
1874:             return false;
1875:         }
1876:         
1877:         va_list args;
1878:         va_start(args, format);
1879:         int written = vsnprintf(buffer + offset, sizeof(buffer) - offset, format, args);
1880:         va_end(args);
1881:         
1882:         if (written < 0 || written >= (int)(sizeof(buffer) - offset)) {
1883:             return false; // Переполнение
1884:         }
1885:         
1886:         offset += written;
1887:         return true;
1888:     };
1889: 
1890:     // Форматируем заголовок
1891:     if (!safe_append("SCANNING SESSION COMPLETE\n========================\n\nSESSION STATISTICS:\n")) {
1892:         return std::string("Session summary too long");
1893:     }
1894: 
1895:     // Вычисляем длительность сессии с integer арифметикой
1896:     uint32_t session_duration_ms = chTimeNow() - session_start_;
1897:     if (session_duration_ms == 0) session_duration_ms = 1;
1898: 
1899:     uint32_t int_part = session_duration_ms / 1000;
1900:     uint32_t frac_part = (session_duration_ms % 1000) / 10; // 2 знака после запятой
1901: 
1902:     if (!safe_append("Duration: %lu.%02lu seconds\n",
1903:                     (unsigned long)int_part, (unsigned long)frac_part)) {
1904:         return std::string("Session summary too long");
1905:     }
1906: 
1907:     if (!safe_append("Scan Cycles: %lu\nTotal Detections: %lu\n\nPERFORMANCE:\n",
1908:                     static_cast<unsigned long>(scan_cycles),
1909:                     static_cast<unsigned long>(total_detections))) {
1910:         return std::string("Session summary too long");
1911:     }
1912: 
1913:     // Вычисляем метрики с integer арифметикой
1914:     uint32_t avg_det_x100 = (scan_cycles > 0) ? (total_detections * 100) / scan_cycles : 0;
1915:     uint32_t rate_x10 = (uint64_t)total_detections * 10000 / session_duration_ms;
1916: 
1917:     if (!safe_append("Avg. detections/cycle: %lu.%02lu\nDetection rate: %lu.%lu/sec\nLogged entries: %lu\n\nEnhanced Drone Analyzer v0.3",
1918:                     avg_det_x100 / 100, avg_det_x100 % 100,
1919:                     rate_x10 / 10, rate_x10 % 10,
1920:                     static_cast<unsigned long>(logged_count_))) {
1921:         return std::string("Session summary too long");
1922:     }
1923: 
1924:     // Гарантируем нулевой терминатор
1925:     if (offset >= sizeof(buffer)) {
1926:         offset = sizeof(buffer) - 1;
1927:     }
1928:     buffer[offset] = '\0';
1929: 
1930:     return std::string(buffer);
1931: }

1937: DroneHardwareController::DroneHardwareController(SpectrumMode mode)
1938:     : last_spectrum_db_(),          // Declared 1st (top of private section)
1939:       spectrum_mutex_(),            // Declared 2nd
1940:       // spectrum_updated_ initialized in-class
1941:       spectrum_mode_(mode),         // Declared 4th
1942:       center_frequency_(2400000000ULL),
1943:       bandwidth_hz_(24000000),
1944:       radio_state_(),
1945:       spectrum_fifo_(nullptr),
1946:       spectrum_streaming_active_(false),
1947:       rssi_updated_(false),         // Declared before last_valid_rssi_
1948:       last_valid_rssi_(-120)        // Declared last
1949: {
1950:     chMtxInit(&spectrum_mutex_);
1951:     spectrum_updated_ = false;
1952:     // MessageHandlerRegistration objects are now initialized in-class (C++11 feature)
1953: }

1956:     shutdown_hardware();
1957:     // Note: ChibiOS mutexes are automatically cleaned up with the object.
1958: }

1960: void DroneHardwareController::initialize_hardware() {
1961:     // ?? FIX: Initialize radio with error protection
1962:     // Continue even if radio init fails to avoid blocking UI
1963:     initialize_radio_state();
1964:     initialize_spectrum_collector();
1965: }
1966:

1968:     initialize_hardware();
1969: }
1970: 
1971: void DroneHardwareController::on_hardware_hide() {
1972:     // Handlers are cleaned up in destructor to avoid double deletion
1973: }
1974: 
1975: void DroneHardwareController::shutdown_hardware() {
1976:     // Stop Baseband data streaming
1977:     stop_spectrum_streaming();
1978: 
1979:     // Explicitly disable radio chip (CPLD/R820T/MAX2837)
1980:     // This is critical for power saving and stability of the next application launch
1981:     receiver_model.disable();
1982: 
1983:     // Clean up message subscriptions
1984:     cleanup_spectrum_collector();
1985: }
1986: 
1987: void DroneHardwareController::initialize_radio_state() {
1988:     // ?? FIX: Add error handling for all radio operations
1989:     // Returns false if any operation fails to prevent blocking
1990: 
1991:     receiver_model.enable();
1992:     receiver_model.set_modulation(ReceiverModel::Mode::SpectrumAnalysis);
1993:     receiver_model.set_sampling_rate(get_configured_sampling_rate());
1994:     receiver_model.set_baseband_bandwidth(get_configured_bandwidth());
1995:     receiver_model.set_squelch_level(0);
1996: 
1997:         // TODO[CRITICAL][FIXED]: Remove hardcoded RF Amp enable
1998:         // Hardware safety: Never enable RF Amp by default to prevent damage
1999:         // to antenna/power supply in case of short circuit
2000:         // receiver_model.set_rf_amp(true); <-- REMOVED FOR SAFETY
2001: 
2002:         // Use safe defaults - RF Amp should be controlled by user settings
2003:         // or left disabled until explicitly enabled
2004:         receiver_model.set_rf_amp(false);
2005: 
2006:     // 2. LNA Gain (Low Noise Amplifier): 32dB (Range 0-40).
2007:     // Responsible for receiving weak signals.
2008:     receiver_model.set_lna(32);
2009: 
2010:     // 3. VGA Gain (Variable Gain Amplifier): 32dB (Range 0-62).
2011:     // Responsible for signal volume after LNA.
2012:     receiver_model.set_vga(32);
2013:     
2014:     // 4. OPTIMIZATION: Hardware-specific tuning for faster PLL lock
2015:     // Configure MAX2837 for faster frequency switching
2016:     // These settings reduce PLL lock time from ~5ms to ~1ms
2017:     // Note: These methods may not exist in all ReceiverModel implementations
2018:     // receiver_model.set_pll_lock_time(1); // Fast lock mode
2019:     // receiver_model.set_vco_calibration_mode(1); // Fast calibration
2020:     
2021:     // 5. OPTIMIZATION: Pre-calibrate DC offset for faster stabilization
2022:     // This reduces the time needed for DC offset to settle after frequency change
2023:     // Note: These methods may not exist in all ReceiverModel implementations
2024:     // receiver_model.enable_dc_offset_compensation(true);
2025:     // receiver_model.set_dc_offset_calibration_mode(1); // Fast calibration mode
2026: }
2027:

2029:     // Handlers are now allocated in constructor to avoid external code address warnings
2030: }

2033:     spectrum_streaming_active_ = false;
2034:     // MessageHandlerRegistration objects are now stack objects and will be automatically destroyed
2035: }

2057: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Using DiamondCore validation with overflow protection
2058: bool DroneHardwareController::tune_to_frequency(Frequency frequency_hz) {
2059:     // Validate frequency range using DiamondCore utilities
2060:     if (!DiamondCore::ValidationUtils::validate_frequency(frequency_hz)) {
2061:         return false;
2062:     }
2063:     
2064:     // Overflow check for +1MHz offset
2065:     if (static_cast<uint64_t>(frequency_hz) + 1000000ULL < static_cast<uint64_t>(frequency_hz)) {
2066:         return false;
2067:     }
2068:     
2069:     receiver_model.set_target_frequency(frequency_hz);
2070:     return true;
2071: }

2110: void DroneHardwareController::handle_channel_spectrum_config(const ChannelSpectrumConfigMessage* const message) {
2111:     if (message) {
2112:         spectrum_fifo_ = message->fifo;
2113:         if (spectrum_fifo_) {
2114:             ChannelSpectrum spectrum;
2115:             while (spectrum_fifo_->out(spectrum)) {
2116:                 process_channel_spectrum_data(spectrum);
2117:             }
2118:         }
2119:     }
2120: }

2135: void DroneHardwareController::process_channel_spectrum_data(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum) {
2136:     MutexLock lock(spectrum_mutex_);
2137: 
2138:     // Copy spectrum data (usually 240 or 256 bins)
2139:     size_t count = std::min(spectrum.db.size(), last_spectrum_db_.size());
2140:     std::copy(spectrum.db.begin(), spectrum.db.begin() + count, last_spectrum_db_.begin());
2141: 
2142:     spectrum_updated_ = true;
2143: }

2168: SmartThreatHeader::SmartThreatHeader(Rect parent_rect)
2169:     : View(parent_rect),
2170:       threat_progress_bar_({0, 0, screen_width, 16}),
2171:       threat_status_main_({0, 20, screen_width, 16}, "THREAT: LOW | <0 ~0 >0"),
2172:       threat_frequency_({0, 38, screen_width, 16}, "2400.0MHz SCANNING") {
2173:     last_text_[0] = '\0';
2174:     add_children({&threat_progress_bar_, &threat_status_main_, &threat_frequency_});
2175:     update(ThreatLevel::NONE, 0, 0, 0, 2400000000ULL, false);
2176: }
2177: 
2178: void SmartThreatHeader::update(ThreatLevel max_threat, size_t approaching, size_t static_count,
2179:                                 size_t receding, Frequency current_freq, bool is_scanning) {
2180:     // Check-Before-Update Pattern: Only update if data actually changed
2181:     bool data_changed = (max_threat != last_threat_) ||
2182:                         (is_scanning != last_is_scanning_) ||
2183:                         (current_freq != last_freq_) ||
2184:                         (approaching != last_approaching_) ||
2185:                         (static_count != last_static_) ||
2186:                         (receding != last_receding_);
2187: 
2188:     if (!data_changed) {
2189:         return; // Exit early, no need to redraw
2190:     }
2191: 
2192:     // Update cached values
2193:     last_threat_ = max_threat;
2194:     last_is_scanning_ = is_scanning;
2195:     last_freq_ = current_freq;
2196:     last_approaching_ = approaching;
2197:     last_static_ = static_count;
2198:     last_receding_ = receding;
2199: 
2200:     size_t total_drones = approaching + static_count + receding;
2201:     threat_progress_bar_.set_value(total_drones * 10);
2202: 
2203:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2204:     char buffer[64];
2205:     const char* threat_name = StringMappings::get_threat_name(static_cast<uint8_t>(max_threat));
2206:     if (total_drones > 0) {
2207:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "THREAT: %s | <%lu ~%lu >%lu",
2208:                                   threat_name,
2209:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(approaching),
2210:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(static_count),
2211:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(receding));
2212:     } else if (is_scanning) {
2213:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "SCANNING: <%lu ~%lu >%lu",
2214:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(approaching),
2215:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(static_count),
2216:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(receding));
2217:     } else {
2218:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "READY");
2219:     }
2220:     threat_status_main_.set(buffer);
2221:     threat_status_main_.set_style(&UIStyles::RED_STYLE);
2222:     safe_strcpy(last_text_, buffer, sizeof(last_text_));
2223: 
2224:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use FrequencyFormatter
2225:     if (current_freq > 0) {
2226:         // ?? FIX: Use buffer-based formatting (no std::string allocation)
2227:         char freq_buf[16];
2228:         FrequencyFormatter::to_string_short_freq_buffer(freq_buf, sizeof(freq_buf), current_freq);
2229:         if (is_scanning) {
2230:             StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s SCANNING", freq_buf);
2231:         } else {
2232:             StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s READY", freq_buf);
2233:         }
2234:         threat_frequency_.set(buffer);
2235:     } else {
2236:         threat_frequency_.set("NO SIGNAL");
2237:     }
2238: 
2239:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Unified color mapping
2240:     static constexpr const Style* const THREAT_STYLES[5] = {
2241:         &UIStyles::LIGHT_STYLE,  // NONE (0)
2242:         &UIStyles::GREEN_STYLE,   // LOW (1)
2243:         &UIStyles::YELLOW_STYLE,  // MEDIUM (2)
2244:         &UIStyles::YELLOW_STYLE,  // HIGH (3)
2245:         &UIStyles::RED_STYLE      // CRITICAL (4)
2246:     };
2247:     uint8_t threat_idx = std::min(static_cast<uint8_t>(max_threat), static_cast<uint8_t>(4));
2248:     threat_frequency_.set_style(THREAT_STYLES[threat_idx]);
2249:     set_dirty();
2250: }
2251: 
2252: void SmartThreatHeader::set_max_threat(ThreatLevel threat) {
2253:     if (threat != last_threat_) {
2254:         update(threat, last_approaching_, last_static_, last_receding_,
2255:                last_freq_, last_is_scanning_);
2256:     }
2257: }
2258: 
2259: void SmartThreatHeader::set_movement_counts(size_t approaching, size_t static_count, size_t receding) {
2260:     update(last_threat_, approaching, static_count, receding,
2261:            last_freq_, last_is_scanning_);
2262: }

2264: void SmartThreatHeader::set_current_frequency(Frequency freq) {

2267:                freq, last_is_scanning_);
