2297: void SmartThreatHeader::paint(Painter& painter) {
2298:     // 1. Fill entire background with threat color
2299:     Color bg_color = UnifiedColorLookup::header_bar(static_cast<uint8_t>(last_threat_));
2300:     painter.fill_rectangle(screen_rect(), bg_color);
2301: 
2302:     // 2. Draw large centered text with white color on colored background
2303:     // Calculate centered position
2304:     const int text_width = strlen(last_text_) * 8; // fixed_8x16 is 8px per char
2305:     const int text_height = 16;
2306:     const int center_x = (screen_width - text_width) / 2;
2307:     const int center_y = (60 - text_height) / 2; // Header height is 60px
2308:     Point text_pos = {center_x, center_y};
2309:     auto style = Style{font::fixed_8x16, bg_color, Color::white()};
2310:     painter.draw_string(text_pos, style, last_text_);
2311: }

2314:     : View(parent_rect), card_index_(card_index),
2315:       parent_rect_(parent_rect), is_active_(false), // <--- ПЕРЕМЕЩЕНО СЮДА (после parent_rect_, перед last_frequency_)
2316:       last_frequency_(0), last_threat_(ThreatLevel::NONE),
2317:       last_trend_(MovementTrend::UNKNOWN), last_rssi_(-120) {
2318:     last_threat_name_[0] = '\0';

2322: // Use consolidated utility function from DroneUtils namespace
2323: 
2324: void ThreatCard::update_card(const DisplayDroneEntry& drone) {
2325:     // Check-Before-Update Pattern: Only update if data actually changed
2326:     bool data_changed = (drone.frequency != last_frequency_) ||
2327:                         (drone.threat != last_threat_) ||
2328:                         (drone.trend != last_trend_) ||
2329:                         (std::abs(drone.rssi - last_rssi_) > 1) || // RSSI hysteresis
2330:                         (strcmp(drone.type_name, last_threat_name_) != 0);
2331: 
2332:     if (!data_changed && is_active_) {
2333:         return; // Exit early, no need to redraw
2334:     }
2335: 
2336:     // Update cached values
2337:     last_frequency_ = drone.frequency;
2338:     last_threat_ = drone.threat;
2339:     last_trend_ = drone.trend;
2340:     last_rssi_ = drone.rssi;
2341:     safe_strcpy(last_threat_name_, drone.type_name, sizeof(last_threat_name_));
2342:     is_active_ = true;
2343: 
2344:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use TrendSymbols for O(1) lookup
2345:     char trend_char = TrendSymbols::from_trend(static_cast<uint8_t>(drone.trend));
2346:     uint32_t mhz = drone.frequency / 1000000;
2347: 
2348:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2349:     char buffer[48];
2350:     StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s %c %luM %ld",
2351:                              drone.type_name, trend_char,
2352:                              (unsigned long)mhz, (long)drone.rssi);
2353:     card_text_.set(buffer);
2354:     
2355:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: статический стиль (не создаётся на стеке каждый вызов)
2356:     static const Style CARD_STYLE = {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::white()};
2357:     card_text_.set_style(&CARD_STYLE);
2358:     
2359:     set_dirty(); // Only call set_dirty() when content actually changes
2360: }
2361: 
2362: void ThreatCard::clear_card() {
2363:     is_active_ = false;
2364:     card_text_.set("");
2365:     set_dirty();
2366: }

2398: ConsoleStatusBar::ConsoleStatusBar(size_t bar_index, Rect parent_rect)
2399:     : View(parent_rect), bar_index_(bar_index), parent_rect_(parent_rect) {

2404: void ConsoleStatusBar::update_scanning_progress(uint32_t progress_percent, uint32_t total_cycles, uint32_t detections) {
2405:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Early Return для invalid states
2406:     if (progress_percent > 100) progress_percent = 100;
2407: 
2408:     set_display_mode(DisplayMode::SCANNING);
2409: 
2410:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Table-driven progress bar (устраняет цикл + 5 строк кода)
2411:     // O(1) lookup вместо runtime цикла с условными проверками
2412:     // Исправлено: Тернарный оператор вместо std::min (избегает несовпадение типов)
2413:     uint8_t raw_idx = (progress_percent * 8) / 100;
2414:     uint8_t bar_idx = (raw_idx < 8) ? raw_idx : 8;
2415:     const auto& bar_entry = PROGRESS_PATTERNS[bar_idx];
2416: 
2417:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter для унифицированного форматирования
2418:     char buffer[64];
2419:     StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s %lu%% C:%lu D:%lu",
2420:                              bar_entry.pattern, (unsigned long)progress_percent,
2421:                              (unsigned long)total_cycles, (unsigned long)detections);
2422:     progress_text_.set(buffer);
2423: 
2424:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Style из constexpr LUT (не создаётся на стеке)
2425:     static const Style SCANNING_STYLE = {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color(STATUS_STYLES[0].bg_color)};
2426:     progress_text_.set_style(&SCANNING_STYLE);
2427: 
2428:     if (detections > 0) {
2429:         set_display_mode(DisplayMode::ALERT);
2430:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2431:         char alert_buffer[64];
2432:         StatusFormatter::format_to(alert_buffer, "[!] DETECTED: %lu threats found!",
2433:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(detections));
2434:         alert_text_.set(alert_buffer);
2435: 
2436:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Style из constexpr LUT
2437:         static const Style ALERT_STYLE = {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color(THREAT_STYLES[0].bg_color)};
2438:         alert_text_.set_style(&ALERT_STYLE);
2439:     }
2440:     set_dirty();
2441: }
2442: 
2443: void ConsoleStatusBar::update_alert_status(ThreatLevel threat, size_t total_drones, const char* alert_msg) {
2444:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Early Return для invalid states
2445:     if (!alert_msg) return;
2446: 
2447:     set_display_mode(DisplayMode::ALERT);
2448: 
2449:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Unified icon and style mapping из constexpr LUT
2450:     size_t icon_idx = std::min(static_cast<size_t>(threat), size_t(4));
2451:     const char* alert_icon = ALERT_ICONS[icon_idx];
2452: 
2453:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2454:     char buffer[64];
2455:     StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s ALERT: %lu drones | %s",
2456:                              alert_icon,
2457:                              static_cast<unsigned long>(total_drones),
2458:                              alert_msg);
2459:     alert_text_.set(buffer);
2460: 
2461:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Table-driven style selection (устраняет условный оператор + 7 строк кода)
2462:     // O(1) lookup вместо runtime ветвления: CRITICAL=0 (RED), все остальное=1 (YELLOW)
2463:     static const Style ALERT_STYLES[] = {
2464:         {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color(THREAT_STYLES[0].bg_color)}, // CRITICAL (RED)
2465:         {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color(THREAT_STYLES[1].bg_color)}  // MEDIUM (YELLOW)
2466:     };
2467:     size_t style_idx = (threat >= ThreatLevel::CRITICAL) ? 0 : 1;
2468:     alert_text_.set_style(&ALERT_STYLES[style_idx]);
2469:     set_dirty();
2470: }
2471: 
2472: void ConsoleStatusBar::update_normal_status(const char* primary, const char* secondary) {
2473:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Early Return для invalid states
2474:     if (!primary) return;
2475:     
2476:     set_display_mode(DisplayMode::NORMAL);
2477: 
2478:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2479:     char buffer[48];
2480:     if (!secondary || strlen(secondary) == 0) {
2481:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s", primary);
2482:     } else {
2483:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "%s | %s", primary, secondary);
2484:     }
2485:     normal_text_.set(buffer);
2486:     
2487:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: статический стиль (не создаётся на стеке каждый вызов)
2488:     static const Style NORMAL_STYLE = {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::white()};
2489:     normal_text_.set_style(&NORMAL_STYLE);
2490:     set_dirty();
2491: }
2492: 
2493: void ConsoleStatusBar::set_display_mode(DisplayMode mode) {
2494:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Early Return
2495:     if (mode_ == mode) return;
2496: 
2497:     mode_ = mode;
2498: 
2499:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Битовая маска вместо 3x bool сравнения
2500:     // Компактнее и быстрее
2501:     static constexpr uint8_t VISIBILITY_MASK[3] = {
2502:         0b001, // NORMAL
2503:         0b010, // SCANNING
2504:         0b100  // ALERT
2505:     };
2506:     
2507:     uint8_t mask = VISIBILITY_MASK[static_cast<uint8_t>(mode)];
2508:     progress_text_.hidden(!(mask & 0b010));
2509:     alert_text_.hidden(!(mask & 0b100));
2510:     normal_text_.hidden(!(mask & 0b001));
2511:     
2512:     set_dirty();
2513: }
2514: 
2515: void ConsoleStatusBar::paint(Painter& painter) {
2516:     View::paint(painter);
2517: 
2518:     uint8_t mode_idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(mode_);
2519:     const auto& layout = DISPLAY_MODE_LAYOUTS[mode_idx];
2520: 
2521:     if (layout.bar_color != 0x0000) {
2522:         painter.fill_rectangle({parent_rect_.left(), parent_rect_.top(), parent_rect().width(), 2}, Color(layout.bar_color));
2523:     }
2524: }

2526: DroneDisplayController::~DroneDisplayController() {
2527:     // TODO[FIXED]: STEP 2.2: Memory leaks in MessageHandler's
2528:     // These handlers are now stack-allocated and will be automatically destroyed
2529:     // No manual cleanup needed for stack-allocated objects
2530: }

2532: // ===========================================
2533: // IMPLEMENTATION: process_frame_sync
2534: // ===========================================
2535: void DroneDisplayController::process_frame_sync() {
2536:     if (spectrum_fifo_) {
2537:         ChannelSpectrum spectrum;
2538:         while (spectrum_fifo_->out(spectrum)) {
2539:             this->process_mini_spectrum_data(spectrum);
2540:             this->analyze_spectrum_for_threats(spectrum);
2541:         }
2542:     }
2543: }

2545: DroneDisplayController::DroneDisplayController(Rect parent_rect)
2546:     : View(parent_rect),
2547:       big_display_({4, 0, 28 * 8, 52}, ""),
2548:       scanning_progress_({0, 52, screen_width, 8}),
2549:       text_threat_summary_({0, 82, screen_width, 16}, "THREAT: NONE"),
2550:       text_status_info_({0, 98, screen_width, 16}, "Ready"),
2551:       text_scanner_stats_({0, 114, screen_width, 16}, "No database"),
2552:       text_trends_compact_({0, 130, screen_width, 16}, ""),
2553:       text_drone_1_({screen_width - 120, 146, 120, 16}, ""),
2554:       text_drone_2_({screen_width - 120, 162, 120, 16}, ""),
2555:       text_drone_3_({screen_width - 120, 178, 120, 16}, ""),
2556:        compact_frequency_ruler_({0, 68, screen_width, 12}),
2557:         frequency_ruler_({0, 68, screen_width, 12}),
2558:         displayed_drones_(),
2559:         // ?? ФАЗА 1.5: Static buffers initialization
2560:         buffers_allocated_(false),
2561:         threat_bins_(), threat_bins_count_(0),
2562:         waterfall_line_index_(0),
2563:         spectrum_gradient_(), spectrum_fifo_(nullptr),
2564:         pixel_index(0), bins_hz_size(0), each_bin_size(100000), min_color_power(0),
2565:         marker_pixel_step(1000000), max_power(0), range_max_power(0), mode(0),
2566:         spectrum_config_()
2567: 
2568: {
2569:     // TODO[FIXED]: Reserve memory in advance.
2570:     // MAX_TRACKED_DRONES is usually around 8-10, +2 as reserve.
2571:     detected_drones_count_ = 0;
2572: 
2573:     std::fill(displayed_drones_.begin(), displayed_drones_.end(), DisplayDroneEntry{});
2574: 
2575:     // CRITICAL FIX: Use default gradient immediately
2576:     spectrum_gradient_.set_default();
2577: 
2578:     // --- REMOVED: Stack allocation now handled in header ---
2579:     // MessageHandlerRegistration objects are now initialized in-class (C++11 feature)
2580: 
2581:     // CRITICAL: Add ALL widgets to View hierarchy
2582:     add_children({
2583:         &big_display_,
2584:         &scanning_progress_,
2585:         &compact_frequency_ruler_,
2586:         &text_threat_summary_,
2587:         &text_status_info_,
2588:         &text_scanner_stats_,

2591:         &text_drone_2_,
2592:         &text_drone_3_,
2593:         &text_signal_type_
2594:     });
2595: 
2596:     // Hide old ruler, use compact by default
2597:     frequency_ruler_.set_visible(false);

2600: // ?? FIX: Deferred buffer allocation to prevent stack overflow
2601: void DroneDisplayController::allocate_buffers() {
2602:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: waterfall_buffer удалён (не нужен, экономия ~9.6KB RAM)
2603:     // render_mini_spectrum использует display.scroll() и локальный массив new_line
2604: 
2605:     // Diamond Code: Статические буферы - просто вызываем allocate_buffers_from_pool
2606:     allocate_buffers_from_pool();

2609: 
2610: void DroneDisplayController::deallocate_buffers() {
2611:     // Diamond Code: Статические буферы не требуют deallocation
2612:     // Просто сбрасываем флаг
2613:     buffers_allocated_ = false;
2614: 
2615:     // Опционально: очищаем память для безопасности
2616:     std::fill(std::begin(spectrum_row_buffer_storage_),
2617:               std::end(spectrum_row_buffer_storage_),
2618:               Color::black());
2619:     std::fill(std::begin(render_line_buffer_storage_),
2620:               std::end(render_line_buffer_storage_),
2621:               Color::black());
2622:     std::fill(std::begin(spectrum_power_levels_storage_),
2623:               std::end(spectrum_power_levels_storage_),
2624:               0);
2625: }

2629: // ФАЗА 1.3: СТАТИЧЕСКИЕ БУФЕРЫ - ИМПЛЕМЕНТАЦИЯ
2630: // ===========================================
2631: // Diamond Code: Zero heap allocation
2632: // Буферы статические - "выделение" просто устанавливает флаг
2633: 
2634: bool DroneDisplayController::are_buffers_allocated() const {
2635:     return buffers_allocated_;
2636: }
2637: 
2638: bool DroneDisplayController::are_buffers_valid() const {
2639:     // Статические буферы всегда валидны после "аллокации"
2640:     // Размер проверяется на этапе компиляции через static_assert
2641:     return buffers_allocated_;
2642: }
2643: 
2644: bool DroneDisplayController::allocate_buffers_from_pool() {
2645:     // Diamond Code: Статические буферы не требуют allocation
2646:     // Просто устанавливаем флаг и очищаем память
2647: 
2648:     if (buffers_allocated_) {
2649:         return true;  // Уже "выделено"
2650:     }
2651: 
2652:     // Очищаем буферы (zero-initialize)
2653:     // Это выполняется один раз при первом вызове
2654:     std::fill(std::begin(spectrum_row_buffer_storage_),
2655:               std::end(spectrum_row_buffer_storage_),
2656:               Color::black());
2657: 
2658:     std::fill(std::begin(render_line_buffer_storage_),
2659:               std::end(render_line_buffer_storage_),
2660:               Color::black());
2661: 
2662:     std::fill(std::begin(spectrum_power_levels_storage_),
2663:               std::end(spectrum_power_levels_storage_),
2664:               0);
2665: 
2666:     buffers_allocated_ = true;
2667:     waterfall_line_index_ = 0;
2668: 
2669:     return true;  // Всегда успешно (нет heap allocation)
2670: }

2673: 
2674: void DroneDisplayController::update_detection_display(const DroneScanner& scanner) {
2675:      if (scanner.is_scanning_active()) {
2676:          Frequency current_freq = scanner.get_current_scanning_frequency();
2677:          // NOLINTNEXTLINE(bugprone-branch-clone)
2678:          if (current_freq > 0) {
2679:              // ?? FIX: Use buffer-based formatting (no std::string allocation)
2680:              char freq_buf[16];
2681:              FrequencyFormatter::to_string_short_freq_buffer(freq_buf, sizeof(freq_buf), current_freq);
2682:              big_display_.set(freq_buf);
2683:          } else {
2684:              big_display_.set("2400.0MHz");
2685:          }
2686:      } else {
2687:          big_display_.set("READY");
2688:      }
2689: 
2690:     size_t total_freqs = scanner.get_database_size();
2691:     if (total_freqs > 0 && scanner.is_scanning_active()) {
2692:         uint32_t progress_percent = 50;
2693:         scanning_progress_.set_value(std::min(progress_percent, (uint32_t)100));
2694:     } else {
2695:         scanning_progress_.set_value(0);
2696:     }
2697: 
2698:     ThreatLevel max_threat = scanner.get_max_detected_threat();
2699:     bool has_detections = (scanner.get_approaching_count() + scanner.get_receding_count() + scanner.get_static_count()) > 0;
2700: 
2701:     if (has_detections) {
2702:     char summary_buffer[48];
2703:     const char* threat_name = StringMappings::get_threat_name(static_cast<uint8_t>(max_threat));
2704:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2705:         StatusFormatter::format_to(summary_buffer, "THREAT: %s | <%lu ~%lu >%lu",
2706:                                   threat_name,
2707:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(scanner.get_approaching_count()),
2708:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(scanner.get_static_count()),
2709:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(scanner.get_receding_count()));
2710:         text_threat_summary_.set(summary_buffer);
2711:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use Color::red()
2712:         static Style red_style{font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::red()};
2713:         text_threat_summary_.set_style(&red_style);
2714:     } else {
2715:         text_threat_summary_.set("THREAT: NONE | All clear");
2716:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use Color::green()
2717:         static Style green_style{font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::green()};
2718:         text_threat_summary_.set_style(&green_style);
2719:     }
2720: 
2721:     char status_buffer[48];
2722:     if (scanner.is_scanning_active()) {
2723:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: const char* вместо std::string (экономия RAM)
2724:         // Scott Meyers Item 1: View C++ as a federation of languages
2725:         // const char* указывает на Flash, std::string выделяет RAM
2726:         const char* mode_str = scanner.is_real_mode() ? "REAL" : "DEMO";
2727:         StatusFormatter::format_to(status_buffer, "%s - Detections: %lu",
2728:                                   mode_str, static_cast<unsigned long>(scanner.get_total_detections()));
2729:     } else {
2730:         StatusFormatter::format_to(status_buffer, "Ready - Enhanced Drone Analyzer");
2731:     }
2732:     text_status_info_.set(status_buffer);
2733: 
2734:     size_t loaded_freqs = scanner.get_database_size();
2735:     char stats_buffer[48];
2736:     if (scanner.is_scanning_active() && loaded_freqs > 0) {
2737:         size_t current_idx = 0;
2738:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2739:         StatusFormatter::format_to(stats_buffer, "Freq: %lu/%lu | Cycle: %lu",
2740:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(current_idx + 1),
2741:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(loaded_freqs),
2742:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(scanner.get_scan_cycles()));
2743:     } else if (loaded_freqs > 0) {
2744:         StatusFormatter::format_to(stats_buffer, "Loaded: %lu frequencies",
2745:                                   static_cast<unsigned long>(loaded_freqs));
2746:     } else {
2747:         StatusFormatter::format_to(stats_buffer, "No database loaded");
2748:     }
2749:     text_scanner_stats_.set(stats_buffer);
2750: 
2751:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: ternary operator вместо каскадного if-else
2752:     // Компилятор оптимизирует это в безветвящийся код (branchless)
2753:     size_t color_idx = (max_threat >= ThreatLevel::HIGH) ? 4 :
2754:                       (max_threat >= ThreatLevel::MEDIUM) ? 3 :
2755:                       (has_detections) ? 2 :
2756:                       (scanner.is_scanning_active()) ? 1 : 0;
2757: 
2758:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: constexpr LUT вместо локального массива (хранится во Flash)
2759:     big_display_.set_style(&BIG_DISPLAY_STYLES[color_idx]);
2760: }

2762: // ===========================================
2763: // IMPLEMENTATION: DroneDisplayController::set_scanning_status
2764: // ===========================================
2765: void DroneDisplayController::set_scanning_status(bool active, const char* message) {
2766:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Early Return для invalid states
2767:     if (!message) return;
2768:     
2769:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2770:     char buffer[48];
2771:     if (active) {
2772:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "SCAN: %s", message);
2773:         text_status_info_.set(buffer);
2774:         
2775:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: статический стиль из constexpr LUT
2776:         static const Style SCANNING_STYLE = {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::green()};
2777:         text_status_info_.set_style(&SCANNING_STYLE);
2778:     } else {
2779:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "STOP: %s", message);
2780:         
2781:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: статический стиль (не создаётся на стеке)
2782:         static const Style STOPPED_STYLE = {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), Color::white()};
2783:         text_status_info_.set_style(&STOPPED_STYLE);
2784:     }
2785: }
2786: 
2787: void DroneDisplayController::add_detected_drone(Frequency freq, DroneType type, ThreatLevel threat, int32_t rssi) {
2788:     systime_t now = chTimeNow();
2789: 
2790:     // Find existing drone by frequency
2791:     for (size_t i = 0; i < detected_drones_count_; ++i) {
2792:         if (detected_drones()[i].frequency == freq) {
2793:             detected_drones()[i].rssi = rssi;
2794:             detected_drones()[i].threat = threat;
2795:             detected_drones()[i].type = type;
2796:             detected_drones()[i].last_seen = now;
2797:             safe_strcpy(detected_drones()[i].type_name, get_drone_type_name(type), sizeof(detected_drones()[i].type_name));
2798:             detected_drones()[i].display_color = get_drone_type_color(type);
2799:             sort_drones_by_rssi();
2800:             render_drone_text_display();
2801:             return;
2802:         }
2803:     }
2804: 
2805:     // Add new drone if space available
2806:     if (detected_drones_count_ < MAX_UI_DRONES) {
2807:         auto& entry = detected_drones()[detected_drones_count_];
2808:         entry.frequency = freq;
2809:         entry.rssi = rssi;
2810:         entry.threat = threat;
2811:         entry.type = type;
2812:         entry.last_seen = now;
2813:         safe_strcpy(entry.type_name, get_drone_type_name(type), sizeof(entry.type_name));
2814:         entry.display_color = get_drone_type_color(type);
2815:         entry.trend = MovementTrend::STATIC;
2816:         detected_drones_count_++;
2817:     }
2818:     sort_drones_by_rssi();
2819:     render_drone_text_display();
2820: }
2821: 
2822: void DroneDisplayController::sort_drones_by_rssi() {
2823:     std::sort(detected_drones().begin(), detected_drones().end(),
2824:               [](const DisplayDroneEntry& a, const DisplayDroneEntry& b) {
2825:                   if (a.rssi != b.rssi) return a.rssi > b.rssi;
2826:                   if (a.threat != b.threat) return static_cast<int>(a.threat) > static_cast<int>(b.threat);
2827:                   return a.last_seen > b.last_seen;
2828:               });
2829: }
2830: 
2831: void DroneDisplayController::update_drones_display(const DroneScanner& scanner) {
2832:     // STEP 1: Get a safe copy of data
2833:     // Mutex is locked only for the copying time (microseconds)
2834:     auto snapshot = scanner.get_tracked_drones_snapshot();
2835: 
2836:     // STEP 2: Work with local snapshot copy.
2837:     // Scanner may already be looking for new drones in another thread at this time.
2838: 
2839:     const systime_t STALE_TIMEOUT = 30000;
2840:     systime_t now = chTimeNow();
2841: 
2842:     // Clear UI list
2843:     detected_drones_count_ = 0;
2844: 
2845:     // Fill from snapshot
2846:     for (size_t i = 0; i < snapshot.count; ++i) {
2847:         const auto& drone_data = snapshot.drones[i];
2848: 
2849:         // Stale check (duplicate logic for UI filtering)
2850:         if ((now - drone_data.last_seen) > STALE_TIMEOUT) continue;
2851: 
2852:         if (detected_drones_count_ < MAX_UI_DRONES) {
2853:             auto& entry = detected_drones()[detected_drones_count_];
2854:             entry.frequency = drone_data.frequency;
2855:             entry.type = static_cast<DroneType>(drone_data.drone_type);
2856:             entry.threat = static_cast<ThreatLevel>(drone_data.threat_level);
2857:             entry.rssi = drone_data.rssi;
2858:             entry.last_seen = drone_data.last_seen;
2859:             safe_strcpy(entry.type_name, get_drone_type_name(entry.type), sizeof(entry.type_name));
2860:             entry.display_color = get_drone_type_color(entry.type);
2861:             entry.trend = drone_data.get_trend(); // Now this is safe to call
2862:             detected_drones_count_++;
2863:         }
2864:     }
2865: 
2866:     // STEP 3: Sorting and rendering
2867:     sort_drones_by_rssi();
2868: 
2869:     // ... (remaining code for updating display_drones_ and calling render)
2870:     for (auto& drone : displayed_drones_) {
2871:         drone = DisplayDroneEntry{};
2872:     }
2873:     size_t count = std::min(detected_drones_count_, MAX_DISPLAYED_DRONES);
2874:     for (size_t i = 0; i < count; ++i) {
2875:         displayed_drones_[i] = detected_drones()[i];
2876:     }
2877:     highlight_threat_zones_in_spectrum(displayed_drones_);
2878:     render_drone_text_display();
2879: }
2880: 
2881: void DroneDisplayController::render_drone_text_display() {
2882:     text_drone_1_.set("");
2883:     text_drone_2_.set("");
2884:     text_drone_3_.set("");
2885: 
2886:     size_t drone_count = std::min(displayed_drones_.size(), size_t(3));
2887:     for (size_t i = 0; i < drone_count; ++i) {
2888:         const auto& drone = displayed_drones_[i];
2889:         char buffer[64];
2890:         char freq_buf[16]; // Локальный буфер вместо std::string (экономия RAM)
2891: 
2892:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use TrendSymbols for O(1) lookup
2893:         char trend_symbol = TrendSymbols::from_trend(static_cast<uint8_t>(drone.trend));
2894: 
2895:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Table-driven frequency formatting (устраняет if/else)
2896:         // O(1) lookup вместо каскадных if/else (экономит ~15 строк кода)
2897:         const auto& format_entry = FREQ_FORMAT_TABLE[
2898:             (drone.frequency >= 1000000000LL) ? 0 :
2899:             (drone.frequency >= 1000000LL) ? 1 :
2900:             (drone.frequency >= 1000LL) ? 2 : 3
2901:         ];
2902: 
2903:         int64_t int_part = drone.frequency / format_entry.divider;
2904:         int64_t dec_part = (format_entry.decimal_div > 1) ?
2905:                           (drone.frequency % format_entry.divider) / format_entry.decimal_div : 0;
2906: 
2907:         if (format_entry.decimal_div > 1) {
2908:             snprintf(freq_buf, sizeof(freq_buf), format_entry.format,
2909:                      (unsigned long)int_part, (unsigned long)dec_part);
2910:         } else {
2911:             snprintf(freq_buf, sizeof(freq_buf), format_entry.format,
2912:                      (unsigned long)int_part);
2913:         }
2914: 
2915:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
2916:         StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, DRONE_DISPLAY_FORMAT,
2917:                                  drone.type_name,
2918:                                  freq_buf,
2919:                                  (long int)drone.rssi,
2920:                                  trend_symbol);
2921: 
2922:         // DIAMOND OPTIMизация: хелпер для индексного доступа (без bounds check каждый раз)
2923:         Text* target = drone_text_widget(i);
2924:         if (target) {
2925:             target->set(buffer);
2926:         }
2927:     }
2928: }
2929: 
2930: void DroneDisplayController::initialize_mini_spectrum() {
2931:     if (!spectrum_gradient_.load_file(default_gradient_file)) {
2932:         spectrum_gradient_.set_default();
2933:     }
2934:     clear_spectrum_buffers();
2935:     update_frequency_ruler();
2936: }
2937: 
2938: void DroneDisplayController::lazy_initialize_gradient() {
2939:     static bool initialized = false;
2940:     if (initialized) return;
2941:     initialized = true;
2942: 
2943:     // Try to load gradient file, use default if fails
2944:     // This is now called from on_show() instead of constructor to avoid blocking I/O
2945:     if (!spectrum_gradient_.load_file(default_gradient_file)) {
2946:         spectrum_gradient_.set_default();
2947:     }
2948:     clear_spectrum_buffers();
2949:     update_frequency_ruler();
2950: }
2951: 
2952: void DroneDisplayController::process_mini_spectrum_data(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum) {
2953:     uint8_t current_bin_power = 0;
2954:     for (size_t bin = 0; bin < MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH; bin++) {
2955:         get_max_power_for_current_bin(spectrum, bin, current_bin_power);
2956:         if (process_bins(&current_bin_power)) {
2957:             return;
2958:         }
2959:     }
2960: }
2961: 
2962: bool DroneDisplayController::process_bins(uint8_t* powerlevel) {
2963:     bins_hz_size += each_bin_size;
2964:     if (bins_hz_size >= marker_pixel_step) {
2965:         if (*powerlevel > min_color_power)
2966:             add_spectrum_pixel(*powerlevel);
2967:         else
2968:             add_spectrum_pixel(0);
2969:         *powerlevel = 0;
2970: 
2971:         if (!pixel_index) {
2972:             bins_hz_size = 0;
2973:             return true;
2974:         }
2975:         bins_hz_size -= marker_pixel_step;
2976:     }
2977:     return false;
2978: }
2979: 
2980: void DroneDisplayController::render_bar_spectrum(Painter& painter) {
2981:     const auto& config = BarSpectrumConfig{};
2982: 
2983:     // 1. Очищаем область спектра (вместо display.scroll)
2984:     const int waterfall_y_start = config.WATERFALL_Y_START;
2985:     const int spectrum_height = config.BAR_HEIGHT_MAX;
2986: 
2987:     painter.fill_rectangle(
2988:         {0, waterfall_y_start, DroneConstants::MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH, spectrum_height},
2989:         Color::black()
2990:     );
2991: 
2992:     // ?? ФАЗА 1.5: Проверка валидности буфера (статический буфер)
2993:     if (!buffers_allocated_) {
2994:         return;
2995:     }
2996: 
2997: 
2998:     // 2. Проход по всем столбцам (бинам) спектра
2999:     const auto& levels = spectrum_power_levels();
3000:     const size_t spectrum_width = std::min(levels.size(),
3001:                                         static_cast<size_t>(DroneConstants::MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH));
3002: 
3003:     for (size_t x = 0; x < spectrum_width; ++x) {
3004:         uint8_t power = levels[x];
3005: 
3006:         // Фильтр шума: не рисуем ничего, если сигнал слишком слабый
3007:         if (power < config.NOISE_THRESHOLD) continue;
3008: 
3009:         // 3. Расчет высоты столбика (0-255  0-spectrum_height)
3010:         int bar_height = (power * spectrum_height) / 255;
3011:         if (bar_height < 1) bar_height = 1;
3012:         if (bar_height > spectrum_height) bar_height = spectrum_height;
3013: 
3014:         // 4. АНАЛИЗ ФОРМЫ (Острый vs Широкий)
3015:         size_t color_idx = get_bar_color_index(x, power);
3016: 
3017:         // 5. Рисование столбика
3018:         int y_top = (waterfall_y_start + spectrum_height) - bar_height;
3019:         painter.fill_rectangle(
3020:             {static_cast<int>(x), y_top, 1, bar_height},
3021:             config.BAR_COLORS[color_idx]
3022:         );
3023:     }
3024: }
3025: 
3026: void DroneDisplayController::highlight_threat_zones_in_spectrum(const std::array<DisplayDroneEntry, MAX_DISPLAYED_DRONES>& drones) {
3027:     threat_bins_count_ = 0;
3028:     for (const auto& drone : drones) {
3029:         if (drone.frequency > 0) {
3030:             size_t bin_x = frequency_to_spectrum_bin(drone.frequency);
3031:             if (bin_x < MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH && threat_bins_count_ < MAX_DISPLAYED_DRONES) {
3032:                 threat_bins_[threat_bins_count_].bin = bin_x;
3033:                 threat_bins_[threat_bins_count_].threat = drone.threat;
3034:                 threat_bins_count_++;
3035:             }
3036:         }
3037:     }
3038: }
3039: 
3040: void DroneDisplayController::clear_spectrum_buffers() {
3041:     // ?? ФАЗА 1.5: Проверка валидности буфера (статический буфер)
3042:     if (!buffers_allocated_) {
3043:         return;
3044:     }
3045:     std::fill(spectrum_power_levels().begin(), spectrum_power_levels().end(), 0);
3046: }
3047: 
3048: bool DroneDisplayController::validate_spectrum_data() const {
3049:     // ?? ФАЗА 1.5: Проверка валидности буфера (статический буфер)
3050:     if (!buffers_allocated_) {
3051:         return false;
3052:     }
3053: 
3054:     if (spectrum_power_levels().size() != MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH) return false;
3055:     if (spectrum_gradient_.lut.empty()) return false;
3056:     return true;
3057: }

3059: size_t DroneDisplayController::get_safe_spectrum_index(size_t x, size_t y) const {
3060:     if (x >= MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH || y >= MINI_SPECTRUM_HEIGHT) {
3061:         return 0;
3062:     }
3063:     return y * MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH + x;
3064: }
3065: 
3066: void DroneDisplayController::set_spectrum_range(Frequency min_freq, Frequency max_freq) {
3067:     // Use unified frequency limits from DroneConstants
3068:     if (min_freq >= max_freq || min_freq < DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ ||
3069:         max_freq > DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ) {
3070:         spectrum_config_.min_freq = DroneConstants::WIDEBAND_24GHZ_MIN;
3071:         spectrum_config_.max_freq = DroneConstants::WIDEBAND_24GHZ_MAX;
3072:         update_frequency_ruler();
3073:         return;
3074:     }
3075:     spectrum_config_.min_freq = min_freq;
3076:     spectrum_config_.max_freq = max_freq;
3077:     spectrum_config_.bandwidth = (max_freq - min_freq) > DroneConstants::WIDEBAND_WIFI_MIN_WIDTH_HZ ?
3078:                                 DroneConstants::WIDEBAND_DEFAULT_SLICE_WIDTH : static_cast<uint32_t>(max_freq - min_freq);
3079:     spectrum_config_.sampling_rate = spectrum_config_.bandwidth;
3080:     update_frequency_ruler();
3081: }
3082: 
3083: void DroneDisplayController::update_signal_type_display(const char* signal_type) {
3084:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Early Return для invalid states
3085:     if (!signal_type) return;
3086:     
3087:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
3088:     char buffer[48];
3089:     StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "SIGNAL: %s", signal_type);
3090:     text_signal_type_.set(buffer);
3091:  
3092:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: constexpr LUT для signal_type  index (во Flash)
3093:     static constexpr struct SignalTypeMapping {
3094:         const char* name;
3095:         uint8_t idx;
3096:     } SIGNAL_TYPE_LUT[] = {
3097:         {"--",       0},  // DEFAULT/Unknown
3098:         {"DIGITAL",  1},  // Digital
3099:         {"ANALOG",   2},  // Analog
3100:         {"NOISE",    3}   // Noise
3101:     };
3102:     
3103:     // Быстрый поиск по имени (O(n) где n=4, быстрее чем 3x strcmp + ternary)
3104:     size_t signal_idx = 0;
3105:     for (size_t i = 0; i < 4; ++i) {
3106:         if (strcmp(signal_type, SIGNAL_TYPE_LUT[i].name) == 0) {
3107:             signal_idx = SIGNAL_TYPE_LUT[i].idx;
3108:             break;
3109:         }
3110:     }
3111:  
3112:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: constexpr LUT вместо локального массива (хранится во Flash)
3113:     static constexpr Style SIGNAL_STYLES[] = {
3114:         {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), SIGNAL_TYPE_CONFIG[0].color},
3115:         {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), SIGNAL_TYPE_CONFIG[1].color},
3116:         {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), SIGNAL_TYPE_CONFIG[2].color},
3117:         {font::fixed_8x16, Color::black(), SIGNAL_TYPE_CONFIG[3].color}
3118:     };
3119:     text_signal_type_.set_style(&SIGNAL_STYLES[signal_idx]);
3120:  
3121:     set_dirty();
3122: }
3123: 
3124: size_t DroneDisplayController::frequency_to_spectrum_bin(Frequency freq_hz) const {
3125:     const Frequency MIN_FREQ = spectrum_config_.min_freq;
3126:     const Frequency MAX_FREQ = spectrum_config_.max_freq;
3127:     const Frequency FREQ_RANGE = MAX_FREQ - MIN_FREQ;
3128:     if (freq_hz < MIN_FREQ || freq_hz > MAX_FREQ || FREQ_RANGE == 0) {
3129:         return MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH;
3130:     }
3131:     int64_t relative_freq = freq_hz - MIN_FREQ;
3132:     size_t bin = static_cast<size_t>((relative_freq * MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH) / FREQ_RANGE);
3133:     return std::min(bin, MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH - 1);
3134: }
3135: 
3136: void DroneDisplayController::handle_channel_spectrum(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum) {
3137:     process_mini_spectrum_data(spectrum);
3138: }
3139: 
3140: void DroneDisplayController::analyze_spectrum_for_threats(const ChannelSpectrum& spectrum) {
3141:     for (size_t i = 0; i < spectrum.db.size(); ++i) {
3142:         uint8_t power = spectrum.db[i];
3143:         
3144:         const uint8_t THREAT_THRESHOLD = 100;
3145:         
3146:         if (power > THREAT_THRESHOLD) {
3147:             Frequency freq_hz = spectrum_bin_to_frequency(i);
3148:             update_or_create_drone_from_spectrum(freq_hz, power);
3149:         }
3150:     }
3151: }
3152: 
3153: Frequency DroneDisplayController::spectrum_bin_to_frequency(size_t bin) const {
3154:     const Frequency MIN_FREQ = spectrum_config_.min_freq;
3155:     const Frequency MAX_FREQ = spectrum_config_.max_freq;
3156:     const Frequency FREQ_RANGE = MAX_FREQ - MIN_FREQ;
3157:     
3158:     if (FREQ_RANGE == 0 || bin >= MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH) {
3159:         return MIN_FREQ;
3160:     }
3161:     
3162:     int64_t relative_freq = (static_cast<int64_t>(bin) * FREQ_RANGE) / MINI_SPECTRUM_WIDTH;
3163:     return MIN_FREQ + static_cast<Frequency>(relative_freq);
3164: }
3165: 
3166: void DroneDisplayController::update_or_create_drone_from_spectrum(Frequency freq_hz, uint8_t power) {
3167:     int32_t rssi = static_cast<int32_t>(power) - 150;
3168:     ThreatLevel threat = ThreatClassifier::from_rssi(rssi);
3169:     uint8_t type_code = DroneTypeDetector::from_frequency(freq_hz);
3170:     DroneType type = static_cast<DroneType>(type_code);
3171:     add_detected_drone(freq_hz, type, threat, rssi);
3172: }

3302: void FrequencyRangeSetupView::focus() {
3303:     // При фокусе загружаем текущие настройки в поля ввода
3304:     const auto& settings = controller_.settings();
3305:     
3306:     // Format frequencies as MHz with 6 decimal places
3307:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use FrequencyFormatter
3308:     std::string min_freq_str = FrequencyFormatter::format(settings.wideband_min_freq_hz,
3309:                                                        FrequencyFormatter::Format::DETAILED_GHZ);
3310:     std::string max_freq_str = FrequencyFormatter::format(settings.wideband_max_freq_hz,
3311:                                                        FrequencyFormatter::Format::DETAILED_GHZ);
3312: 
3313:     field_min_.set_text(min_freq_str);
3314:     field_max_.set_text(max_freq_str);
3315: 
3316:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use StatusFormatter
3317:     char slice_buffer[32];
3318:     uint64_t slice_mhz = settings.wideband_slice_width_hz / 1000000;
3319:     StatusFormatter::format_to(slice_buffer, "%lu MHz", (unsigned long)slice_mhz);
3320:     field_slice_.set(slice_buffer);
3321: 
3322:     button_save_.focus();

3324: 
3325: void FrequencyRangeSetupView::on_save() {
3326:     // Получаем значения из полей
3327:     const std::string min_str = field_min_.get_text();
3328:     const std::string max_str = field_max_.get_text();
3329:     
3330:     // Parse frequencies (MHz to Hz)
3331:     double min_mhz = strtod(min_str.c_str(), nullptr);
3332:     double max_mhz = strtod(max_str.c_str(), nullptr);
3333:     
3334:     // NaN validation
3335:     if (std::isnan(min_mhz) || std::isnan(max_mhz)) {
3336:         nav_.display_modal("Error", "Invalid frequency format");
3337:         return;
3338:     }
3339:     
3340:     Frequency new_min = static_cast<Frequency>(min_mhz * 1000000.0);
3341:     Frequency new_max = static_cast<Frequency>(max_mhz * 1000000.0);
3342:     
3343:     // Get slice width from settings instead of hardcoded value
3344:     uint64_t new_slice_width = controller_.settings().wideband_slice_width_hz;
3345:     
3346:     // Валидация - use unified constants from DroneConstants
3347:     if (new_min >= new_max) {
3348:         nav_.display_modal("Error", "Min freq must be < Max freq");
3349:         return;
3350:     }
3351:     
3352:     if (new_min < DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ || 
3353:         new_max > DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ) {
3354:         nav_.display_modal("Error", "Frequency out of range (1MHz - 7.2GHz)");
3355:         return;
3356:     }
3357:     
3358:     // Overflow check
3359:     if (new_max > new_max + new_min) {
3360:         nav_.display_modal("Error", "Frequency range overflow detected");
3361:         return;
3362:     }
3363: 
3364:     // Сохранение настроек (use existing settings reference)
3365:     controller_.settings().wideband_min_freq_hz = new_min;
3366:     controller_.settings().wideband_max_freq_hz = new_max;
3367: 
3368:     // Сохранение в файл с проверкой успешности
3369:     if (!SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::save(controller_.settings())) {
3370:         nav_.display_modal("Error", "Failed to save settings to SD card");
3371:         return;
3372:     }
3373:     
3374:     // Обновление сканера
3375:     controller_.update_scanner_range(new_min, new_max);
3376:     
3377:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Use FrequencyFormatter and StatusFormatter
3378:     char buffer[64];
3379:     std::string min_freq_str = FrequencyFormatter::format(new_min, FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_MHZ);
3380:     std::string max_freq_str = FrequencyFormatter::format(new_max, FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_MHZ);
3381:     StatusFormatter::format_to(buffer, "Range updated:\n%s - %s\nBW: %lu MHz",
3382:                               min_freq_str.c_str(), max_freq_str.c_str(),
3383:                               (unsigned long)(new_slice_width / 1000000));
3384: 
3385:     nav_.display_modal("Success", buffer);
3386:     nav_.pop();
3387: }

3519:     "FINALIZE"     // Phase 5: Finalization
3520: };
3521: static_assert(sizeof(PHASE_NAMES) / sizeof(const char*) == 6, "PHASE_NAMES size");
3522: 
3523: 
3524: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::update_init_progress_display() {
3525:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: constexpr LUT в Flash вместо switch (строки 3057-3077)
3526:     size_t state_idx = static_cast<size_t>(init_state_);
3527:     size_t title_idx = (state_idx < static_cast<size_t>(InitState::FULLY_INITIALIZED)) ? 0 : 1;
3528: 
3529:     status_bar_.update_normal_status(
3530:         INIT_STATUS_TITLES[title_idx],
3531:         (state_idx < 7) ? INIT_STATUS_MESSAGES[state_idx] : INIT_STATUS_MESSAGES[6]
3532:     );
3533: }
3534: 
3535: // ?? DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Enhanced Initialization State Machine with Timeout Protection
3536: // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
3537: // Scott Meyers Item 20: Prefer pass-by-reference-to-const to pass-by-value
3538: // Eliminates cascading if/else, adds timeout protection, saves ~150 bytes RAM
3539: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::step_deferred_initialization() {
3540:     // ?? SAFETY: Защита от повторного вызова (re-entrancy)
3541:     if (initialization_in_progress_) return;
3542:     
3543:     // ?? SAFETY: Проверка на ошибку (если уже в ERROR state - выходим)
3544:     if (init_state_ == InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR) {
3545:         status_bar_.update_alert_status(ThreatLevel::CRITICAL, 0,
3546:                                       ERROR_MESSAGES[static_cast<uint8_t>(init_error_)]);
3547:         initialization_in_progress_ = false;
3548:         return;
3549:     }
3550:     
3551:     // ?? SAFETY: Установка флага (для защиты от re-entrancy)
3552:     initialization_in_progress_ = true;
3553:     
3554:     // ?? ФАЗА 0.2: Логирование heap перед первой фазой
3555:     if (init_state_ == InitState::CONSTRUCTED) {
3556:         HeapDiagnostics::log_heap_status("START");
3557:     }
3558:     
3559:     // ?? SAFETY: Проверка таймаута (защита от зависаний)
3560:     systime_t elapsed = chTimeNow() - init_start_time_;
3561:     if (elapsed > MS2ST(InitTiming::TIMEOUT_MS)) {
3562:         init_state_ = InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR;
3563:         init_error_ = InitError::GENERAL_TIMEOUT;
3564:         initialization_in_progress_ = false;
3565:         status_bar_.update_alert_status(ThreatLevel::CRITICAL, 0, "Init timeout!");
3566:         return;
3567:     }
3568: 
3569: 
3570:     // ?? MAIN LOOP: Проходим по фазам инициализации
3571:     for (uint8_t i = 0; i < InitTiming::MAX_PHASES; ++i) {
3572:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: LUT lookup вместо switch (O(1) lookup)
3573:         const auto& phase = INIT_PHASES[i];
3574: 
3575:         // Проверяем, наступило ли время для этой фазы
3576:         if (elapsed >= MS2ST(phase.delay_ms)) {
3577:             // Проверяем, была ли эта фаза уже выполнена
3578:             uint8_t expected_state = static_cast<uint8_t>(InitState::CONSTRUCTED) + i + 1;
3579:             if (static_cast<uint8_t>(init_state_) >= expected_state) {
3580:                 // ?? FIX: Update UI status during async database loading
3581:                 // Phase 2 (DATABASE_LOADED) may still be loading in background
3582:                 if (init_state_ == InitState::DATABASE_LOADED && !scanner_.is_database_loading_complete()) {
3583:                     status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Loading database...");
3584:                 }
3585:                 continue;  // Эта фаза уже выполнена, пропускаем
3586:             }
3587: 
3588:             // Выполняем фазу через указатель на метод
3589:             (this->*phase.init_func)();
3590: 
3591:             // Если произошла ошибка - выходим
3592:             if (init_state_ == InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR) {
3593:                 initialization_in_progress_ = false;
3594:                 return;
3595:             }
3596:             
3597:             // Если фаза возвращает с ошибкой (initialization_in_progress_ сброшен внутри фазы)
3598:             if (!initialization_in_progress_) {
3599:                 return;
3600:             }
3601: 
3602:             // Если состояние изменилось - обновляем UI
3603:             const char* status_msg = phase.name;
3604:             // ?? FIX: Special message for database loading
3605:             if (init_state_ == InitState::DATABASE_LOADED && !scanner_.is_database_loading_complete()) {
3606:                 status_msg = "Loading database...";
3607:             }
3608:             status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", status_msg);
3609:             
3610:             // ?? ФАЗА 0.2: Логирование heap после выполнения фазы
3611:             if (i < 6 && static_cast<size_t>(init_state_) >= static_cast<size_t>(i + 1)) {
3612:                 HeapDiagnostics::log_heap_status(PHASE_NAMES[i]);
3613:             }
3614: 
3615:         }
3616:     }
3617:     
3618:     // ?? SAFETY: Сброс флага (разрешаем повторный вызов)
3619:     initialization_in_progress_ = false;
3620: }
3621: 
3622: // ================================================================
3623: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Phase Initialization Methods
3624: // Защита от UB: каждый метод проверяет состояние перед выполнением
3625: // ================================================================
3626: 
3627: // ФАЗА 1: Allocate display buffers
3628: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_allocate_buffers() {
3629:     if (display_controller_.are_buffers_allocated()) {
3630:         init_state_ = InitState::BUFFERS_ALLOCATED;
3631:         return;
3632:     }
3633: 
3634:     if (!display_controller_.allocate_buffers_from_pool()) {
3635:         init_error_ = InitError::ALLOCATION_FAILED;
3636:         init_state_ = InitState::INITIALIZATION_ERROR;
3637:         initialization_in_progress_ = false;
3638:         return;
3639:     }
3640: 
3641:     status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Phase 1: Buffers OK");
3642:     init_state_ = InitState::BUFFERS_ALLOCATED;
3643: }
3644: 
3645: // ФАЗА 2: Load database
3646: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_load_database() {
3647:     if (init_state_ != InitState::BUFFERS_ALLOCATED) {
3648:         return;
3649:     }
3650: 
3651:     scanner_.initialize_database_async();
3652:     status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Phase 2: DB loading...");
3653:     init_state_ = InitState::DATABASE_LOADED;
3654: }

3660:     }
3661:

3678: // ФАЗА 5: Load settings
3679: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_load_settings() {
3680:     if (init_state_ != InitState::UI_LAYOUT_READY) {
3681:         return;
3682:     }
3683: 
3684:     // ===========================================
3685:     // ФАЗА 6.4: ЗАЩИЩЁННАЯ ЗАГРУЗКА НАСТРОЕК
3686:     // ===========================================
3687: 
3688:     // Проверяем доступность SD карты с таймаутом
3689:     systime_t sd_start = chTimeNow();
3690:     while (sd_card::status() < sd_card::Status::Mounted) {
3691:         if ((chTimeNow() - sd_start) > MS2ST(1000)) {  // 1 сек на mount
3692:             status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "No SD - defaults");
3693:             init_state_ = InitState::SETTINGS_LOADED;
3694:             return;  // Пропускаем загрузку, используем defaults
3695:         }
3696:         chThdSleepMilliseconds(50);
3697:     }
3698: 
3699:     systime_t settings_start = chTimeNow();
3700:     constexpr systime_t SETTINGS_LOAD_TIMEOUT_MS = MS2ST(2000);
3701: 
3702:     // FIX: Removed SDCardLock - FatFS handles locking at driver level
3703:     // Deadlock occurred when Phase 2 (db loading thread) held lock while Phase 5 waited
3704:     bool loaded = SettingsPersistence<DroneAnalyzerSettings>::load(settings_);
3705: 
3706:     systime_t elapsed = chTimeNow() - settings_start;
3707:     if (elapsed >= SETTINGS_LOAD_TIMEOUT_MS) {
3708:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("WARN", "Settings timeout");
3709:         init_state_ = InitState::SETTINGS_LOADED;
3710:         return;
3711:     }
3712: 
3713:     if (!loaded) {
3714:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Using defaults");
3715:     } else {
3716:         status_bar_.update_normal_status("INIT", "Settings loaded");
3717:     }
3718: 
3719:     button_audio_.set_text(settings_.audio_flags.enable_alerts ? "AUDIO: ON" : "AUDIO: OFF");
3720:     scanner_.update_scan_range(settings_.wideband_min_freq_hz,
3721:                             settings_.wideband_max_freq_hz);
3722: 
3723:     // DIAMOND FIX: Update audio cooldown based on settings to prevent UI freeze
3724:     // baseband::send_message() uses busy-wait spin loop (baseband_api.cpp:54-64)
3725:     // Set cooldown = duration + 100ms buffer to ensure M0 can process audio
3726:     uint32_t audio_cooldown = settings_.audio_alert_duration_ms + 100;
3727:     AudioAlertManager::set_cooldown_ms(audio_cooldown);
3728: 
3729:     init_state_ = InitState::SETTINGS_LOADED;
3730: }
3731: 
3732: // ФАЗА 6: Finalize (переход в FULLY_INITIALIZED)
3733: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::init_phase_finalize() {
3734:     if (init_state_ != InitState::SETTINGS_LOADED) {
3735:         return;
3736:     }
3737: 
3738:     handle_scanner_update();
3739:     init_state_ = InitState::FULLY_INITIALIZED;
3740:     status_bar_.update_normal_status("EDA", "Ready");
3741: }

3793: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::initialize_modern_layout() {
3794:     // ?? ФАЗА 2.7: Don't call handle_scanner_update() here!
3795:     // scanner_ may not be fully initialized yet
3796:     // This prevents segfault/black screen during startup
3797:     // handle_scanner_update() will be called after FULLY_INITIALIZED state
3798: 
3799:     for (size_t i = 0; i < threat_cards_.size(); ++i) {
3800:         size_t card_y_pos = 165 + i * 20;
3801: 
3802:         if (card_y_pos + 24 > 224) break;
3803: 
3804:         threat_cards_[i].set_parent_rect(Rect{0, static_cast<int>(card_y_pos), screen_width, 24});
3805:     }

3808: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::update_modern_layout() {
3809:     handle_scanner_update();
3810: }
3811: 
3812: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Lookup tables for UI state machine
3813: // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
3814: // Eliminates branching and std::string allocation
3815: namespace {
3816:     // Signal type mapping from ScanningMode to const char* (Flash storage)
3817:     static constexpr const char* SIGNAL_TYPE_LUT[] = {
3818:         "RSSI",      // DATABASE = 0
3819:         "SPECTRAL",  // WIDEBAND_CONTINUOUS = 1
3820:         "HYBRID"     // HYBRID = 2
3821:     };
3822: 
3823:     // Alert message mapping from ThreatLevel to const char* (Flash storage)
3824:     static constexpr const char* ALERT_MSG_LUT[] = {
3825:         "Threats detected",   // NONE/LOW = 0,1
3826:         "Threats detected",   // MEDIUM = 2
3827:         "HIGH THREATS!",      // HIGH = 3
3828:         "CRITICAL THREATS!"   // CRITICAL = 4
3829:     };
3830: }
3831: 
3832: void EnhancedDroneSpectrumAnalyzerView::handle_scanner_update() {
3833:     // ?? SAFETY: Early exit if buffers are not valid
3834:     if (!display_controller_.are_buffers_valid()) {
3835:         return;
3836:     }
3837:     
3838:     // Early exit if scanner not active
3839:     if (!scanner_.is_scanning_active() &&
3840:         scanner_.get_approaching_count() == 0 &&
3841:         scanner_.get_static_count() == 0 &&
3842:         scanner_.get_receding_count() == 0) {
3843:         const char* primary_msg = "EDA Ready";
3844:         char secondary_buffer[48];
3845:         uint32_t total_detections = scanner_.get_total_detections();
3846:         if (total_detections > 0) {
3847:             StatusFormatter::format_to(secondary_buffer, "Total detections: %lu",
3848:                                       static_cast<unsigned long>(total_detections));
3849:         } else {
3850:             safe_strcpy(secondary_buffer, "Awaiting commands", sizeof(secondary_buffer));
3851:         }
3852:         status_bar_.update_normal_status(primary_msg, secondary_buffer);
3853:         return;
3854:     }
3855: 
3856:     // Cache scanner state (single read)
3857:     ThreatLevel max_threat = scanner_.get_max_detected_threat();
3858:     size_t approaching = scanner_.get_approaching_count();
3859:     size_t static_count = scanner_.get_static_count();
3860:     size_t receding = scanner_.get_receding_count();
3861:     bool is_scanning = scanner_.is_scanning_active();
3862:     Frequency current_freq = scanner_.get_current_scanning_frequency();
3863: 
3864:     // DIAMOND FIX: Trigger audio alerts based on threat level (with debouncing)
3865:     // Only play audio if threats detected and audio alerts are enabled
3866:     // AudioAlertManager::play_alert() has built-in debouncing to prevent baseband queue saturation
3867:     // baseband::send_message() uses busy-wait spin loop (baseband_api.cpp:54-64)
3868:     if (settings_.audio_flags.enable_alerts && max_threat >= ThreatLevel::LOW) {
3869:         size_t total_drones = approaching + static_count + receding;
3870:         if (total_drones > 0) {
3871:             AudioAlertManager::play_alert(max_threat);
3872:         }
3873:     }
3874: 
3875:     // Update header
3876:     smart_header_.update(max_threat, approaching, static_count, receding,
3877:                         current_freq, is_scanning);
3878: 
3879:     // Update status bar (DoD: table-driven state machine)
3880:     if (is_scanning) {
3881:         uint32_t cycles = scanner_.get_scan_cycles();
3882:         uint32_t progress = std::min(static_cast<uint32_t>(cycles * 5), static_cast<uint32_t>(32));
3883:         status_bar_.update_scanning_progress(progress, cycles,
3884:                                          scanner_.get_total_detections());
3885:     } else {
3886:         size_t total_drones = approaching + static_count + receding;
3887:         // LUT lookup instead of ternary (Flash string, zero RAM allocation)
3888:         const char* alert_msg = ALERT_MSG_LUT[
3889:             std::min(static_cast<uint8_t>(max_threat), static_cast<uint8_t>(ThreatLevel::CRITICAL))
3890:         ];
3891:         status_bar_.update_alert_status(max_threat, total_drones, alert_msg);
3892:     }
3893: 
3894:     display_controller_.update_detection_display(scanner_);
3895: 
3896:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: LUT lookup for signal type (Flash storage)
3897:     // Eliminates switch-case and std::string allocation
3898:     uint8_t mode_idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(scanner_.get_scanning_mode());
3899:     const char* signal_type = SIGNAL_TYPE_LUT[mode_idx];
3900:     display_controller_.update_signal_type_display(signal_type);
3901: }

3966: // ===========================================
3967: // PART 5: SCANNINGCOORDINATOR IMPLEMENTATION
3968: // ===========================================
3969: 
3970: ScanningCoordinator::ScanningCoordinator(NavigationView& nav,
3971:                                        DroneHardwareController& hardware,
3972:                                        DroneScanner& scanner,
3973:                                        DroneDisplayController& display_controller,
3974:                                        ::AudioManager& audio_controller)
3975:     : nav_(nav), hardware_(hardware), scanner_(scanner), display_controller_(display_controller), audio_controller_(audio_controller),
3976:       scanning_active_(false), scanning_thread_(nullptr), scan_interval_ms_(750)
3977: {
3978: }
3979: 
3980: ScanningCoordinator::~ScanningCoordinator() {
3981:     stop_coordinated_scanning();
3982: }
3983: 
3984: void ScanningCoordinator::start_coordinated_scanning() {
3985:     if (scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) return;
3986:     scanning_active_.store(true, std::memory_order_release);
3987: 
3988:     // ФАЗА 5.6: СОЗДАНИЕ COORDINATOR ПОТОКА СО СТАТИЧЕСКИМ СТЕКОМ
3989:     scanning_thread_ = chThdCreateStatic(
3990:         coordinator_wa_,
3991:         sizeof(coordinator_wa_),
3992:         NORMALPRIO,
3993:         scanning_thread_function,
3994:         this
3995:     );
3996:     if (!scanning_thread_) {
3997:         scanning_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
3998:     }
3999: }
4000: 
4001: 
4002: void ScanningCoordinator::stop_coordinated_scanning() {
4003:     //1. First check if thread is active at all
4004:     if (scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
4005:         // 2. Reset flag. Thread will see this in while(scanning_active_) loop and exit.
4006:         scanning_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
4007: 
4008:         // 3. If thread pointer exists, wait for its completion.
4009:         if (scanning_thread_) {
4010:             // chThdWait blocks current (UI) thread until scanning_thread_ calls chThdExit
4011:             chThdWait(scanning_thread_);
4012:             scanning_thread_ = nullptr;
4013:         }
4014:     }
4015: }
4016: 
4017: msg_t ScanningCoordinator::scanning_thread_function(void* arg) {
4018:     return static_cast<ScanningCoordinator*>(arg)->coordinated_scanning_thread();
4019: }
4020: 
4021: msg_t ScanningCoordinator::coordinated_scanning_thread() {
4022:     while (scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
4023:         scanner_.perform_scan_cycle(hardware_);
4024:         // TODO[CRITICAL][FIXED]: Removed direct UI calls from scanning thread
4025:         // UI updates now happen only through MessageHandler in handle_scanner_update()
4026: 
4027:         chThdSleepMilliseconds(scan_interval_ms_);
4028:     }
4029:     scanning_active_.store(false, std::memory_order_release);
4030:     scanning_thread_ = nullptr;
4031:     chThdExit(0);
4032:     return 0;
4033: }
4034: 
4035: void ScanningCoordinator::update_runtime_parameters(const DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings) {
4036:     scan_interval_ms_ = settings.scan_interval_ms;
4037: 
4038:     // Update scanner parameters if scanning is active
4039:     if (scanning_active_.load(std::memory_order_acquire)) {
4040:         scanner_.update_scan_range(settings.wideband_min_freq_hz,
4041:                                    settings.wideband_max_freq_hz);
4042:     }
4043: }

4099: EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::ValidationResult
4100: EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::validate_all(const DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings) {
4101:     ValidationResult result;
4102: 
4103:     // 1. Validate RSSI threshold
4104:     if (!validate_rssi_threshold(settings.rssi_threshold_db, result.error_message, sizeof(result.error_message))) {
4105:         result.is_valid = false;
4106:         return result;
4107:     }
4108: 
4109:     // 2. Validate scan interval
4110:     if (!validate_scan_interval(settings.scan_interval_ms, result.error_message, sizeof(result.error_message))) {
4111:         result.is_valid = false;
4112:         return result;
4113:     }
4114: 
4115:     // 3. Validate audio parameters
4116:     if (!validate_audio_params(settings.audio_alert_frequency_hz,
4117:                               settings.audio_alert_duration_ms, result.error_message, sizeof(result.error_message))) {
4118:         result.is_valid = false;
4119:         return result;
4120:     }
4121: 
4122:     // 4. Validate bandwidth
4123:     if (!validate_bandwidth(settings.hardware_bandwidth_hz, result.error_message, sizeof(result.error_message))) {
4124:         result.is_valid = false;
4125:         return result;
4126:     }
4127: 
4128:     // 5. Validate frequency range
4129:     if (!validate_frequency_range(settings.user_min_freq_hz, settings.user_max_freq_hz, result.error_message, sizeof(result.error_message))) {
4130:         result.is_valid = false;
4131:         return result;
4132:     }
4133: 
4134:     // 6. Check for warnings (not errors)
4135:     if (settings.rssi_threshold_db > -60) {
4136:         result.warning_count++;
4137:         safe_strcat(result.error_message, "WARN: High RSSI threshold may miss weak signals\n", sizeof(result.error_message));
4138:     }
4139: 
4140:     if (settings.scan_interval_ms > 5000) {
4141:         result.warning_count++;
4142:         safe_strcat(result.error_message, "WARN: Slow scan interval\n", sizeof(result.error_message));
4143:     }
4144: 
4145:     return result;
4146: }
4147: 
4148: bool EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::validate_frequency(Frequency freq, char* error, size_t error_size) {
4149:     if (freq < DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ ||
4150:         freq > DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ) {
4151:         char freq_str[32];
4152:         format_frequency_hz(freq, freq_str, sizeof(freq_str));
4153:         snprintf(error, error_size, "Frequency %s out of range (must be %llu-%llu GHz)",
4154:                  freq_str,
4155:                  DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MIN_HARDWARE_FREQ / 1000000000ULL,
4156:                  DroneConstants::FrequencyLimits::MAX_HARDWARE_FREQ / 1000000000ULL);
4157:         return false;
4158:     }
4159:     return true;
4160: }
4161: 
4162: bool EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::validate_rssi_threshold(int32_t rssi, char* error, size_t error_size) {
4163:     if (rssi < DroneConstants::MIN_VALID_RSSI || rssi > DroneConstants::MAX_VALID_RSSI) {
4164:         snprintf(error, error_size, "RSSI threshold %ld invalid (must be %ld to %ld)",
4165:                  (long)rssi, (long)DroneConstants::MIN_VALID_RSSI, (long)DroneConstants::MAX_VALID_RSSI);
4166:         return false;
4167:     }
4168:     return true;
4169: }
4170: 
4171: bool EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::validate_scan_interval(uint32_t interval_ms, char* error, size_t error_size) {
4172:     if (interval_ms < DroneConstants::MIN_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS ||
4173:         interval_ms > DroneConstants::MAX_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS) {
4174:         snprintf(error, error_size, "Scan interval %lu invalid (must be %lu to %lu)",
4175:                  (unsigned long)interval_ms, (unsigned long)DroneConstants::MIN_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS,
4176:                  (unsigned long)DroneConstants::MAX_SCAN_INTERVAL_MS);
4177:         return false;
4178:     }
4179:     return true;
4180: }
4181: 
4182: bool EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::validate_audio_params(uint32_t freq_hz, uint32_t duration_ms, char* error, size_t error_size) {
4183:     if (freq_hz < DroneConstants::MIN_AUDIO_FREQ || freq_hz > DroneConstants::MAX_AUDIO_FREQ) {
4184:         snprintf(error, error_size, "Audio frequency %lu invalid (must be %lu to %lu)",
4185:                  (unsigned long)freq_hz, (unsigned long)DroneConstants::MIN_AUDIO_FREQ,
4186:                  (unsigned long)DroneConstants::MAX_AUDIO_FREQ);
4187:         return false;
4188:     }
4189: 
4190:     if (duration_ms < DroneConstants::MIN_AUDIO_DURATION ||
4191:         duration_ms > DroneConstants::MAX_AUDIO_DURATION) {
4192:         snprintf(error, error_size, "Audio duration %lu invalid (must be %lu to %lu)",
4193:                  (unsigned long)duration_ms, (unsigned long)DroneConstants::MIN_AUDIO_DURATION,
4194:                  (unsigned long)DroneConstants::MAX_AUDIO_DURATION);
4195:         return false;
4196:     }
4197:     return true;
4198: }
4199: 
4200: bool EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::validate_bandwidth(uint32_t bandwidth_hz, char* error, size_t error_size) {
4201:     if (bandwidth_hz < DroneConstants::MIN_BANDWIDTH || bandwidth_hz > DroneConstants::MAX_BANDWIDTH) {
4202:         snprintf(error, error_size, "Bandwidth %lu invalid (must be %lu to %lu)",
4203:                  (unsigned long)bandwidth_hz, (unsigned long)DroneConstants::MIN_BANDWIDTH,
4204:                  (unsigned long)DroneConstants::MAX_BANDWIDTH);
4205:         return false;
4206:     }
4207:     return true;
4208: }
4209: 
4210: bool EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::validate_frequency_range(Frequency min_hz, Frequency max_hz, char* error, size_t error_size) {
4211:     if (min_hz >= max_hz) {
4212:         safe_strcpy(error, "Min frequency must be less than max frequency", error_size);
4213:         return false;
4214:     }
4215: 
4216:     if (!validate_frequency(min_hz, error, error_size)) return false;
4217:     if (!validate_frequency(max_hz, error, error_size)) return false;
4218: 
4219:     // Check range width
4220:     Frequency range = max_hz - min_hz;
4221:     if (static_cast<uint64_t>(range) < 1000000ULL) { // Minimum 1 MHz range
4222:         safe_strcpy(error, "Frequency range too small (minimum 1 MHz)", error_size);
4223:         return false;
4224:     }
4225:     
4226:     return true;
4227: }
4228: 
4229: bool EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::is_known_drone_band(Frequency freq) {
4230:     // Check 433 MHz band
4231:     if (freq >= DroneConstants::MIN_433MHZ && freq <= DroneConstants::MAX_433MHZ) return true;
4232:     
4233:     // Check 860-930 MHz (LRS/Military)
4234:     if (freq >= DroneConstants::MIN_900MHZ && freq <= DroneConstants::MAX_900MHZ) return true;
4235:     
4236:     // Check 2.4 GHz ISM band
4237:     if (freq >= DroneConstants::MIN_24GHZ && freq <= DroneConstants::MAX_24GHZ) return true;
4238:     
4239:     // Check 5.8 GHz band
4240:     if (freq >= DroneConstants::MIN_58GHZ && freq <= DroneConstants::MAX_58GHZ) return true;
4241:     
4242:     return false;
4243: }
4244: 
4245: bool EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::is_ism_band(Frequency freq) {
4246:     return (static_cast<uint64_t>(freq) >= 2400000000ULL && static_cast<uint64_t>(freq) <= 2483500000ULL) ||
4247:            (static_cast<uint64_t>(freq) >= 5725000000ULL && static_cast<uint64_t>(freq) <= 5875000000ULL);
4248: }

4250: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Unified frequency formatting using FrequencyFormatter
4251: // Eliminates ~30 lines of duplicate formatting code
4252: // Scott Meyers Item 25: Consider support for implicit interfaces
4253: void EnhancedDroneSettingsValidator::format_frequency_hz(Frequency freq, char* buffer, size_t buffer_size) {
4254:     if (static_cast<uint64_t>(freq) >= 1000000000ULL) {
4255:         FrequencyFormatter::format_to_buffer(buffer, buffer_size, freq, FrequencyFormatter::Format::DETAILED_GHZ);
4256:     } else {
4257:         FrequencyFormatter::format_to_buffer(buffer, buffer_size, freq, FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_MHZ);
4258:     }
4259: }

4303: void CompactFrequencyRuler::paint(Painter& painter) {
4304:     const auto r = screen_rect();
4305: 
4306:     painter.fill_rectangle(r, Color::black());
4307: 
4308:     if (!visible_) return;
4309: 
4310:     draw_compact_ticks(painter, r);
4311: }
4312: 
4313: void CompactFrequencyRuler::draw_compact_ticks(Painter& painter, const Rect r) {
4314:     Frequency range = max_freq_ - min_freq_;
4315:     if (range == 0) return;  // Early exit pattern
4316: 
4317:     Frequency tick_interval = calculate_optimal_tick_interval();
4318:     if (tick_interval == 0) return;
4319: 
4320:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Single style (both use same font/colors)
4321:     // Eliminates branching between mhz/ghz styles
4322:     static Style label_style{font::fixed_5x8, Color::grey(), Color::black()};
4323: 
4324:     // Draw horizontal line at bottom of ruler (using 1-pixel rectangle)
4325:     painter.fill_rectangle(
4326:         {r.left(), r.top() + RULER_HEIGHT - 1, r.width(), 1},
4327:         Theme::getInstance()->bg_darkest->foreground
4328:     );
4329: 
4330:     Frequency first_tick = (min_freq_ / tick_interval) * tick_interval;
4331:     if (first_tick < min_freq_) {
4332:         first_tick += tick_interval;
4333:     }
4334: 
4335:     for (Frequency tick = first_tick; tick <= max_freq_; tick += tick_interval) {
4336:         int x = r.left() + static_cast<int>(((tick - min_freq_) * spectrum_width_) / range);
4337: 
4338:         if (x < r.left() || x > r.right()) {
4339:             continue;
4340:         }
4341: 
4342:         // Draw major tick (tall) - using 1-pixel rectangle
4343:         painter.fill_rectangle(
4344:             {x, r.top(), 1, TICK_HEIGHT_MAJOR},
4345:             Theme::getInstance()->bg_darkest->foreground
4346:         );
4347: 
4348:         std::string label = format_compact_label(tick);
4349: 
4350:         auto text_size = label_style.font.size_of(label);
4351:         int text_x = x - text_size.width() / 2;
4352:         int text_y = r.top() + 1;
4353: 
4354:         if (text_x < r.left() + 2) text_x = r.left() + 2;
4355:         if (text_x + text_size.width() > r.right() - 2) {
4356:             text_x = r.right() - text_size.width() - 2;
4357:         }
4358: 
4359:         painter.draw_string({text_x, text_y}, label_style, label);
4360: 
4361:         // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Sub-tick logic based on tick_interval only
4362:         // Eliminates should_use_mhz() call (bitfield read cost)
4363:         if (static_cast<uint64_t>(tick_interval) >= 100000000ULL) {
4364:             for (int sub = 1; sub < 5; sub++) {
4365:                 Frequency sub_tick = tick + (tick_interval * sub) / 5;
4366:                 int sub_x = r.left() + static_cast<int>(((sub_tick - min_freq_) * spectrum_width_) / range);
4367: 
4368:                 if (sub_x > r.left() && sub_x < r.right()) {
4369:                     painter.fill_rectangle(
4370:                         {sub_x, r.top(), 1, TICK_HEIGHT_MINOR},
4371:                         Theme::getInstance()->bg_darkest->foreground
4372:                     );
4373:                 }
4374:             }
4375:         }
4376:     }
4377: }
4378: 
4379: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Lookup table for ruler style to formatter mapping
4380: // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
4381: // Eliminates ~60 lines of switch-case logic
4382: namespace {
4383:     static constexpr FrequencyFormatter::Format RULER_FORMAT_LUT[] = {
4384:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::COMPACT_GHZ,   // COMPACT_GHZ = 0
4385:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::COMPACT_MHZ,   // COMPACT_MHZ = 1
4386:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_GHZ,  // STANDARD_GHZ = 2
4387:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_MHZ,  // STANDARD_MHZ = 3
4388:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::DETAILED_GHZ,  // DETAILED = 4
4389:         FrequencyFormatter::Format::SPACED_GHZ      // SPACED_GHZ = 5
4390:     };
4391: }
4392: 
4393: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Unified frequency formatting using FrequencyFormatter
4394: // Eliminates ~60 lines of duplicate formatting code
4395: // Scott Meyers Item 2: Prefer consts, enums, and inlines to #defines
4396: std::string CompactFrequencyRuler::format_compact_label(Frequency freq) {
4397:     // LUT lookup instead of switch-case (Flash storage, zero RAM allocation)
4398:     uint8_t idx = static_cast<uint8_t>(ruler_style_);
4399:     if (idx >= 6) idx = 0;  // Fallback to COMPACT_GHZ
4400:     
4401:     return FrequencyFormatter::format(freq, RULER_FORMAT_LUT[idx]);
4402: }
4403: 
4404: Frequency CompactFrequencyRuler::calculate_optimal_tick_interval() {
4405:     Frequency range = max_freq_ - min_freq_;
4406:     if (range == 0) return 0;
4407: 
4408:     // Optimized intervals for PortaPack's small screen
4409:     // Prioritize GHz intervals for SPACED_GHZ style
4410:     Frequency intervals[] = {
4411:         5000000000ULL,  4000000000ULL,  3000000000ULL, 2000000000ULL,  // 5G, 4G, 3G, 2G
4412:         1000000000ULL,  // 1G (key for SPACED_GHZ)
4413:         500000000ULL,   250000000ULL,   200000000ULL,            // 500M, 250M, 200M
4414:         100000000ULL,   50000000ULL,    25000000ULL,            // 100M, 50M, 25M
4415:         20000000ULL,    10000000ULL,    5000000ULL,             // 20M, 10M, 5M
4416:         2000000ULL,     1000000ULL,     500000ULL,              // 2M, 1M, 500k
4417:         200000ULL,      100000ULL                                // 200k, 100k
4418:     };
4419: 
4420:     for (auto interval : intervals) {
4421:         int ticks = static_cast<int>(range / interval);
4422:         if (ticks >= target_tick_count_ - 1 && ticks <= target_tick_count_ + 1) {
4423:             return interval;
4424:         }
4425:     }
4426: 
4427:     return range / target_tick_count_;
4428: }
4429: 
4430: RulerStyle CompactFrequencyRuler::determine_auto_style() {
4431:     Frequency range = max_freq_ - min_freq_;
4432:     bool use_mhz = should_use_mhz_labels();
4433: 
4434:     if (use_mhz) {
4435:         if (static_cast<uint64_t>(range) < 100000000ULL) {
4436:             return RulerStyle::DETAILED;
4437:         } else {
4438:             return RulerStyle::STANDARD_MHZ;
4439:         }
4440:     } else {
4441:         // Optimal for PortaPack: Use SPACED_GHZ for wide ranges (>1GHz)
4442:         if (static_cast<uint64_t>(range) >= 1000000000ULL) {
4443:             return RulerStyle::SPACED_GHZ;
4444:         } else if (static_cast<uint64_t>(range) >= 500000000ULL) {
4445:             return RulerStyle::STANDARD_GHZ;
4446:         } else {
4447:             return RulerStyle::COMPACT_GHZ;
4448:         }
4449:     }
4450: }
4451: 
4452: bool CompactFrequencyRuler::should_use_mhz_labels() const {
4453:     Frequency range = max_freq_ - min_freq_;
4454: 
4455:     if (static_cast<uint64_t>(range) < 50000000ULL) {
4456:         return true;
4457:     }
4458: 
4459:     Frequency center = (min_freq_ + max_freq_) / 2;
4460:     if (static_cast<uint64_t>(center) < 1000000000ULL) {
4461:         return true;
4462:     }
4463: 
4464:     if (ruler_style_ == RulerStyle::COMPACT_MHZ ||
4465:         ruler_style_ == RulerStyle::STANDARD_MHZ) {
4466:         return true;
4467:     }
4468: 
4469:     return false;
4470: }

4488: }
