4495: void FrequencyRuler::set_visible(bool visible) {
4496:     visible_ = visible;
4497:     if (!visible) {
4498:         hidden(true);
4499:     } else {
4500:         hidden(false);
4501:     }
4502: }
4503: 
4504: Frequency FrequencyRuler::calculate_tick_interval() {
4505:     Frequency freq_range = max_freq_ - min_freq_;
4506:     if (freq_range == 0) {
4507:         return 1000000000ULL;  // Default: 1 GHz
4508:     }
4509: 
4510:     // Possible intervals in Hz (from largest to smallest)
4511:     Frequency intervals[] = {
4512:         4000000000ULL,  // 4 GHz
4513:         2000000000ULL,  // 2 GHz
4514:         1000000000ULL,  // 1 GHz
4515:         500000000ULL,   // 500 MHz
4516:         200000000ULL,   // 200 MHz
4517:         100000000ULL,   // 100 MHz
4518:         50000000ULL,    // 50 MHz
4519:         20000000ULL,    // 20 MHz
4520:         10000000ULL,    // 10 MHz
4521:         5000000ULL,     // 5 MHz
4522:         2000000ULL,     // 2 MHz
4523:         1000000ULL      // 1 MHz
4524:     };
4525: 
4526:     size_t num_intervals = sizeof(intervals) / sizeof(intervals[0]);
4527: 
4528:     // Select interval so that we have 4-8 ticks on screen
4529:     for (size_t i = 0; i < num_intervals; i++) {
4530:         if (freq_range / intervals[i] <= 8 && freq_range / intervals[i] >= 4) {
4531:             return intervals[i];
4532:         }
4533:     }
4534: 
4535:     // Fallback: use 6 ticks evenly distributed
4536:     return freq_range / 6;
4537: }
4538: 
4539: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Lookup tables for frequency ruler configuration
4540: // Scott Meyers Item 15: Prefer constexpr to #define
4541: // Eliminates conditional std::string allocation and branching
4542: namespace {
4543:     // Tick configuration LUT (Flash storage, zero RAM at runtime)
4544:     struct TickConfig {
4545:         FrequencyFormatter::Format format;
4546:         uint8_t sub_ticks;  // Bitfield: 0=none, 1..5=count
4547:     };
4548: 
4549:     static constexpr TickConfig TICK_CONFIG_LUT[] = {
4550:         {FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_GHZ, 5},  // >= 1 GHz
4551:         {FrequencyFormatter::Format::STANDARD_MHZ, 5},  // >= 1 MHz
4552:         {FrequencyFormatter::Format::COMPACT_MHZ, 0}    // < 1 MHz
4553:     };
4554: 
4555:     // Get config index from tick_interval (constexpr-friendly)
4556:     constexpr uint8_t get_tick_config_index(Frequency tick_interval) {
4557:         return (static_cast<uint64_t>(tick_interval) >= 1000000000ULL) ? 0 :
4558:                (static_cast<uint64_t>(tick_interval) >= 1000000ULL) ? 1 : 2;
4559:     }
4560: }
4561: 
4562: // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Unified frequency formatting using FrequencyFormatter
4563: // Eliminates ~40 lines of duplicate formatting code
4564: std::string FrequencyRuler::format_frequency_label(Frequency freq, Frequency tick_interval) {
4565:     // LUT lookup instead of conditional (Flash string, zero RAM allocation)
4566:     uint8_t idx = get_tick_config_index(tick_interval);
4567:     return FrequencyFormatter::format(freq, TICK_CONFIG_LUT[idx].format);
4568: }
4569: 
4570: void FrequencyRuler::draw_frequency_ticks(Painter& painter, const Rect r) {
4571:     Frequency tick_interval = calculate_tick_interval();
4572:     Frequency range = max_freq_ - min_freq_;
4573:     if (range == 0) return;  // Early exit pattern
4574: 
4575:     // LUT lookup for configuration (Flash storage, zero RAM allocation)
4576:     const TickConfig& config = TICK_CONFIG_LUT[get_tick_config_index(tick_interval)];
4577: 
4578:     // Style for tick labels (small font 5x8)
4579:     static Style ruler_style{font::fixed_5x8, Color::grey(), Color::black()};
4580: 
4581:     // Draw horizontal line at bottom of ruler (using 1-pixel rectangle)
4582:     painter.fill_rectangle(
4583:         {r.left(), r.top() + RULER_HEIGHT - 1, r.width(), 1},
4584:         Theme::getInstance()->bg_darkest->foreground
4585:     );
4586: 
4587:     // Find first tick
4588:     Frequency first_tick = (min_freq_ / tick_interval) * tick_interval;
4589:     if (first_tick < min_freq_) {
4590:         first_tick += tick_interval;
4591:     }
4592: 
4593:     // Draw ticks and labels
4594:     for (Frequency tick = first_tick; tick <= max_freq_; tick += tick_interval) {
4595:         // Convert frequency to x position
4596:         int x = r.left() + static_cast<int>(((tick - min_freq_) * spectrum_width_) / range);
4597: 
4598:         if (x < r.left() || x > r.right()) {
4599:             continue;
4600:         }
4601: 
4602:         // Draw major tick (tall) - using 1-pixel rectangle
4603:         painter.fill_rectangle(
4604:             {x, r.top(), 1, TICK_HEIGHT_MAJOR},
4605:             Theme::getInstance()->bg_darkest->foreground
4606:         );
4607: 
4608:         // Format and draw text label (LUT lookup, no std::string allocation for unit)
4609:         std::string label = format_frequency_label(tick, tick_interval);
4610: 
4611:         auto text_size = ruler_style.font.size_of(label);
4612:         int text_x = x - text_size.width() / 2;
4613:         int text_y = r.top() + 1;
4614: 
4615:         // Clamp text position to screen bounds
4616:         if (text_x < r.left() + 2) text_x = r.left() + 2;
4617:         if (text_x + text_size.width() > r.right() - 2) {
4618:             text_x = r.right() - text_size.width() - 2;
4619:         }
4620: 
4621:         painter.draw_string({text_x, text_y}, ruler_style, label);
4622: 
4623:         // Add intermediate ticks if configured (LUT lookup, zero branching)
4624:         for (uint8_t sub = 1; sub <= config.sub_ticks; sub++) {
4625:             Frequency sub_tick = tick + (tick_interval * sub) / (config.sub_ticks + 1);
4626:             int sub_x = r.left() + static_cast<int>(((sub_tick - min_freq_) * spectrum_width_) / range);
4627: 
4628:             if (sub_x > r.left() && sub_x < r.right()) {
4629:                 painter.fill_rectangle(
4630:                     {sub_x, r.top(), 1, TICK_HEIGHT_MINOR},
4631:                     Theme::getInstance()->bg_darkest->foreground
4632:                 );
4633:             }
4634:         }
4635:     }
4636: }
4637: 
4638: void FrequencyRuler::paint(Painter& painter) {
4639:     const auto r = screen_rect();
4640: 
4641:     // Fill background
4642:     painter.fill_rectangle(r, Color::black());
4643: 
4644:     // Draw frequency ticks and labels
4645:     if (visible_) {
4646:         draw_frequency_ticks(painter, r);
4647:     }
4648: }
4649: 
4650: void DroneDisplayController::update_frequency_ruler() {
4651:     compact_frequency_ruler_.set_frequency_range(spectrum_config_.min_freq, spectrum_config_.max_freq);
4652:     compact_frequency_ruler_.set_spectrum_width(SPEC_WIDTH);
4653:     compact_frequency_ruler_.set_dirty();
4654: }
4655: 
4656: void DroneDisplayController::set_ruler_style(RulerStyle style) {
4657:     compact_frequency_ruler_.set_ruler_style(style);
4658:     compact_frequency_ruler_.set_visible(true);
4659:     frequency_ruler_.set_visible(false);
4660: }
4661: 
4662: void DroneDisplayController::apply_display_settings(const DroneAnalyzerSettings& settings) {
4663:     if (settings.display_flags.show_frequency_ruler) {
4664:         compact_frequency_ruler_.set_visible(true);
4665:         frequency_ruler_.set_visible(false);
4666: 
4667:         if (settings.display_flags.auto_ruler_style) {
4668:             compact_frequency_ruler_.set_ruler_style(RulerStyle::COMPACT_GHZ);
4669:         } else {
4670:             // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: constexpr LUT в Flash вместо switch (строки 4135-4144)
4671:             uint8_t style_idx = (settings.frequency_ruler_style < 7) ?
4672:                                 settings.frequency_ruler_style : 0;
4673:             compact_frequency_ruler_.set_ruler_style(RULER_STYLE_LUT[style_idx]);
4674:         }
4675: 
4676:         compact_frequency_ruler_.set_tick_count(settings.compact_ruler_tick_count);
4677:     } else {
4678:         compact_frequency_ruler_.set_visible(false);
4679:         frequency_ruler_.set_visible(false);
4680:     }
4681: }

4685: // ===========================================
4686: // AudioAlertManager Implementation
4687: // ===========================================
4688: // AudioAlertManager is declared in ui_drone_audio.hpp inside namespace ui::apps::enhanced_drone_analyzer
4689: 
4690: bool AudioAlertManager::audio_enabled_ = true;
4691: systime_t AudioAlertManager::last_alert_timestamp_ = 0;
4692: uint32_t AudioAlertManager::cooldown_ms_ = 600;
4693: 
4694: void AudioAlertManager::play_alert(ThreatLevel level) {
4695:     if (!audio_enabled_) return;
4696: 
4697:     // DIAMOND OPTIMIZATION: Time-based debouncing to prevent UI freeze
4698:     // baseband::send_message() contains busy-wait spin loop (baseband_api.cpp:54-64)
4699:     // If called at 60 FPS with 200ms beeps, UI would spin-wait ~180ms per frame
4700:     // This would completely freeze the UI - no touch/key events processed
4701:     systime_t now = chTimeNow();
4702:     systime_t elapsed_ticks = now - last_alert_timestamp_;
4703: 
4704:     if (elapsed_ticks < MS2ST(cooldown_ms_)) {
4705:         return;
4706:     }
4707: 
4708:     // Update timestamp for next call
4709:     last_alert_timestamp_ = now;
4710: 
4711:     uint16_t freq_hz = 800;
4712:     switch (level) {
4713:         case ThreatLevel::NONE: return;
4714:         case ThreatLevel::LOW: freq_hz = 800; break;
4715:         case ThreatLevel::MEDIUM: freq_hz = 1000; break;
4716:         case ThreatLevel::HIGH: freq_hz = 1200; break;
4717:         case ThreatLevel::CRITICAL: freq_hz = 2000; break;
4718:         default: freq_hz = 800; break;
4719:     }
4720:     baseband::request_audio_beep(freq_hz, 24000, 200);
4721: }
4722: 
4723: void AudioAlertManager::set_enabled(bool enable) {
4724:     audio_enabled_ = enable;
4725: }
4726: 
4727: bool AudioAlertManager::is_enabled() {
4728:     return audio_enabled_;
4729: }
4730: 
4731: void AudioAlertManager::set_cooldown_ms(uint32_t cooldown_ms) {
4732:     cooldown_ms_ = cooldown_ms;
4733: }
